# NewCo ERP — Decision Register

Running register of decisions taken during the NewCo greenfield ERP track. Append-only.

## Schema
- **DEC-NNN — short title (date)**
  - **Context**: why the decision was needed.
  - **Decision**: what was chosen.
  - **Supersedes / superseded by**: links if applicable.
  - **Owner**: who signed off.

---

## DEC-001 — NewCo greenfield ERP track opened (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Crurated ERP v17 frozen / paused; NewCo is a separate venture and needs its own from-scratch ERP.
- **Decision**: Open a greenfield design track. NewCo treated as a standalone business; ownership / commercial structure between NewCo and Crurated is OUT OF SCOPE.
- **Supersedes**: prior "Plan B parent-sub" framing in `07-NewCo/` and `06-Producer-Club/`, and corresponding auto-memory entries (`project_newco_plan_b`, `project_producer_club_current_erp`, `project_producer_club_agreement_checklist`, `project_producer_club_prd_v13_updates` — all now directional only).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-002 — Business Model Document outline approved (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: BMD must be locked before any technical methodology / module PRD work (per `feedback_business_scope_first.md`).
- **Decision**: 13-section BMD + 3 appendices. Front-ends covered in §7; NFC/NFT in §6; Crurated contrast contained to Appendix B. Standalone document, not written as a delta vs Crurated.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-003 — Five-wave module sequence approved (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Crurated v17 module shape (0/S/K/A/D/B/C/E) is the baseline; NewCo will adapt order to dependency-first.
- **Decision**:
  - Wave 1 — Foundations: Module 0 + Module K.
  - Wave 2 — Supply side: Module A + Module D.
  - Wave 3 — Sell side: Module S.
  - Wave 4 — Physical side: Module B + Module C.
  - Wave 5 — Finance + cross-cutting: Module E + §1 architecture + dashboards + deferred-items/open-questions register.
- **Rationale**: Products and parties before commercial commitments; commerce after supply; physical state after commerce; finance last.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-004 — Seven-stage QA cadence approved (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Need an analogue of Crurated's `project_prd_testing_methodology` (the 6-layer methodology stable across v15 and v16) and the v13 Stage 2.x stage-gate naming.
- **Decision**:
  - Stage 1 — Outline + elicitation.
  - Stage 2 — BMD drafting (hard gate before any module work).
  - Stage 3 — Per-module PRD drafting, one wave at a time, each gated by clarifying-questions doc.
  - Stage 4 — Cross-module integration pass (`qa.integration.md`).
  - Stage 5 — Six-layer agent-driven testing (`qa.layer1.md` … `qa.layer6.md`).
  - Stage 6 — Editorial pass (`qa.editorial.md`).
  - Stage 7 — Release.
- **Naming**: `qa.bm.md`, `qa.mod{X}.md`, `qa.integration.md`, `qa.layer{N}.md`, `qa.editorial.md`. Decisions appended here.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-005 — Folder structure approved (2026-05-01)
- **Decision**: `11-NewCo-greenfield/` at working-directory root, with subfolders `00-business-model/`, `01-prd/`, `02-elicitation/`, `03-qa/`, `04-decisions/`, `05-archive/`.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-006 — Hard gate on BMD sign-off (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Standing rule from `feedback_business_scope_first.md` — lock business scope before technical methodology.
- **Decision**: No module work begins until the BMD is signed off. No PRD wave begins until the prior wave is signed off.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-007 — Hero-package = membership-fee model (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: B2 / B3 / C6 / K1 — model differs from Crurated tier-based membership.
- **Decision**: Each club's annual membership cost equals the price of that year's **hero package** (a producer-curated mixed case). Member pays the cost at registration / annual renewal and receives the hero package. If the hero package value drops below the membership cost in a given year, the difference becomes a **club credit / coupon** spendable on that club. Membership auto-renews annually; producer can kick out; rejected applicants → waiting list. # of members = # of hero packages producer makes available.
- **Implication**: A single transaction at registration is both a membership state change AND a purchase order. Module S / K / E need to model the dual nature.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-008 — Discovery Tab as core feature (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: A2 / B9 / C6 / D15 / L1 — central NewCo differentiator beyond producer clubs.
- **Decision**: NewCo portal exposes a global **Discovery Tab** with offers from any producer (and per L1, Crurated as a supplier — see DEC-009). All members see Discovery; waiting-list applicants and legacy ex-members access Discovery as their only access surface. Producer earns 5% on Discovery purchases made by members originated in that producer's club (first club gets the 5%).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-009 — Crurated as Discovery supplier (open framing) (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: L1 — Paolo confirmed Crurated will be a Discovery supplier, which appeared to contradict the original brief carve-out on intragroup mechanics.
- **Decision**: Provisional — Crurated treated as one Producer-Registry entry like any other supplier (commercial-only). Confirmation pending Q-CL-1 in `02-elicitation/elicitation_v2.md`. If Q-CL-1 returns "intragroup mechanics", this decision is amended.
- **Owner**: Paolo (provisional).

## DEC-010 — 12.5% margin on club sales, 5% revenue share on Discovery (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: C5 / C6 / H1.
- **Decision**: NewCo is always Seller of Record. Club sale: NewCo sells at producer-set price, creates PO at 87.5% of that price → NewCo retains 12.5% margin. Discovery sale: standard NewCo margin + 5% to the buyer's originating club. No producer-side membership fee.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-011 — Both V1 and V2 passive consignment in scope; no active consignment (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: C7 / E1 / L3 — overrides v1's "flatten to single sourcing model" assumption.
- **Decision**: Default sourcing model is passive consignment V2 (stock physically at Vinlock warehouse). Passive consignment V1 (stock stays at producer until needed) supported as an exception for very expensive / rare bottles. No active consignment (no B2B). No drop-shipping.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-012 — Customer segments (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: B2 / B4 / B6 / B7 / B9 / K4.
- **Decision**: Three customer segments coexist:
  - **Member** — approved by a producer; one profile per club; can have many memberships → many profiles.
  - **Waiting-list applicant** — applied for a club but not yet approved; cannot access producer pages but CAN access Discovery; can store bottles bought from Discovery; pays storage fees per the standard policy.
  - **Legacy** — ex-member with stored bottles; same Discovery-only access; same storage rules.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-013 — Storage fee policy (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: B9 / E6 / H4.
- **Decision**: 12 months free per bottle. After 12 months: €3/bottle/year, accounted monthly, charged every 6 months or at shipping. Applies to all customer segments (Member, Waiting-list, Legacy).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-014 — External system stack (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: E2 / E4 / F3 / J3 / J4 / J6 / J7 / J9. Some choices differ from Crurated.
- **Decision**:
  - **Warehouse**: Vinlock (same physical WH as Crurated, separate contracts).
  - **WMS**: Logilize (same provider as Crurated, separate integration).
  - **Blockchain**: **Avalanche** (differs from Crurated's chain).
  - **Payments**: **Airwallex** (differs from Crurated's Stripe).
  - **CRM + Marketing automation**: HubSpot.
  - **Customer support**: deferred (TBD post-launch).
  - **Accounting**: pending Q-AD-4 confirmation (Xero with SDI connector recommended).
- **Owner**: Paolo (Airwallex and Avalanche locked; accounting pending).

## DEC-015 — Italy incorporation likely; French VAT registration likely (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: D10 / H13 / I1 / I2.
- **Decision**: Provisional — NewCo legal entity incorporated in Italy. French VAT registration anticipated due to French warehouse (Vinlock). Cancellation policy and VAT regime detail follow from Italian incorporation. Final legal-entity confirmation pending.
- **Owner**: Paolo (provisional).

## DEC-016 — AI / Operator Copilot kept at launch (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: L6 — overrides Crurated v17's deferral of AI to a later phase.
- **Decision**: AI / Copilot in scope at launch. Specific scope (operator-only vs customer-facing, anomaly/fraud, etc.) pending Q-CL-2.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-017 — No B2B; consumer-only NewCo (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: B13 / D7 / D9.
- **Decision**: NewCo serves only individual collectors (B2C). No B2B wholesale, no active consignment, no B2B credit terms. Differs materially from Crurated v17 which covered B2B wholesale and active consignment.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-018 — Mobile-web only at launch (no native apps) (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: G3.
- **Decision**: Consumer portal launches as web + mobile-web (responsive). No native iOS/Android apps at launch.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-019 — Discovery contains only multi-product/multi-vintage cases, never multi-producer cases (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: D3.
- **Decision**: Mixed-case packages are allowed multi-product / multi-vintage but always single-producer. No cross-producer composite SKUs (which differs from Crurated v17 §1.4 Composite SKU which allowed multi-producer).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-020 — Crurated as Discovery supplier — commercial-only (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-CL-1 resolved.
- **Decision**: Crurated is one Producer-Registry entry on standard commercial terms. No shared identity, no catalog cross-access, no parent-sub mechanics. Original brief's "intragroup OUT" carve-out remains in force.
- **Supersedes**: DEC-009 (provisional).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-021 — AI / Operator Copilot DEFERRED at launch (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-CL-2 resolved. Paolo reversed his earlier preference.
- **Decision**: AI / Copilot deferred from launch (analogous to Crurated v17 §14). Re-evaluated post-launch.
- **Supersedes**: DEC-016.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-022 — NFC/NFT recovery policies — Claude proposes defaults in BMD (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-CL-3 resolved. Paolo asked Claude to propose defaults.
- **Decision**: BMD §6 will include proposed default policies for the four scenarios: (1) damaged tag in WH, (2) damaged tag post-shipment, (3) NFT lost in NewCo wallet, (4) bottle destroyed pre-shipment with NFT alive. Paolo reviews during BMD review.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-023 — Allocation visibility model: club + Discovery + dual-listing with pricing differential (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-CL-4 + Q-CL-5 resolved. Producer decides club content; NewCo curates Discovery.
- **Decision**:
  - All club members see allocations simultaneously (one tier per club; no time-based priority).
  - Discovery is global — open simultaneously to all NewCo members (Member, Waiting-list, Legacy).
  - Producer's discretion: same Bottle Reference can appear in BOTH the club (lower price, club members only) AND Discovery (higher price, all members) at the same time.
  - Allocation carries a visibility flag (e.g., CLUB_ONLY, DISCOVERY_ONLY, BOTH).
  - The "tiered priority" concept (D16 in v1) does NOT apply.
- **Implication**: Module A allocation has a visibility flag. Module S supports either dual-offer-from-same-allocation OR two parallel allocations from the same producer commitment — Module A design call deferred to PRD work.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-024 — SSO / cross-surface identity (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-CL-6 resolved.
- **Decision**:
  - No SSO across the four surfaces (Admin / Consumer / Producer / Bottle).
  - Within Consumer Portal: a single login surfaces all the customer's profiles (Netflix-style B7 model), with profile switcher.
  - Bottle Page: anonymous public; no personalization based on a logged-in consumer-portal session.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-025 — Refund cost matrix (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-CL-7 resolved.
- **Decision**:
  - Producer fault (defective bottle, corked, etc.) → producer absorbs.
  - In-custody breakage (NewCo / Vinlock) → NewCo absorbs (insurance recovery if applicable).
  - Transit damage → carrier insurance + NewCo absorbs gap.
  - Customer cancellation in legal window → NewCo absorbs.
  - Customer dissatisfaction post-shipment → no refund (per E10 — no returns post-shipment).
  - Customer fraud → NewCo absorbs immediately, recovers via dispute.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-026 — Marketing consent — double opt-in marketing, single opt-in transactional (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-AD-1 confirmed.
- **Decision**: Marketing emails require double-opt-in (signup + confirmation link click). Transactional emails (order confirmations, shipment updates, account state changes) use single-opt-in (allowed under EU/Italian e-privacy without explicit marketing consent).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-027 — GDPR posture — standard Italian EU compliance (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-AD-2 confirmed.
- **Decision**:
  - Lawful bases: contract (account + purchase + fulfillment) + consent (marketing) + legitimate interest (security, fraud, anti-abuse).
  - Data subject rights: access, rectification, erasure, portability, objection, restriction.
  - Erasure constraint: cannot fully erase customer holding unredeemed vouchers or stored bottles → soft-delete account, anonymize personal identifiers, retain transactional records for 10-year Italian invoice retention.
  - DPO: internal assignment (no external mandate at NewCo scale).
  - Breach notification: 72 hours to Italian Garante per Article 33 GDPR.
  - Cookie / consent banner: required on consumer portal and bottle page; producer portal exempt as authenticated B2B-style tool.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-09)**: GDPR right-to-erasure × active Hold edge — anonymisation precedence is **per-Hold-type and case-by-case**. Regulatory-record-retention Holds (sanctions Holds carrying OFAC / UIF obligations) block anonymisation until lift; non-regulatory Holds (payment, fraud, KYC, compliance, admin per Module K v0.2 §4.8) do not block anonymisation. Compliance × Legal coordination playbook is operating-manual scope per `feedback_prd_rr_approval`. Anchored at Module K v0.2 §8.2; closes E6-09 + E6-04 (cluster-folded).

## DEC-028 — Accounting platform — Xero + Italian SDI connector (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-AD-4 confirmed.
- **Decision**: Xero (best-in-class API, multi-currency, MPV-VAT-friendly, ~€30–50/month) with a third-party Italian e-invoicing connector to bridge SDI (Sistema di Interscambio).
- **Updates**: DEC-014 (now locked, was pending).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-029 — Data residency — EU (Italian/French regions preferred) (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-AD-5 confirmed.
- **Decision**: All primary databases, backups, and customer-data warehouses in EU regions. Third-party SaaS (HubSpot, Airwallex, Xero, Logilize, Vinlock) configured for EU data-residency where possible; DPAs signed. Avalanche on-chain global by nature — non-PII only on-chain (NFT IDs, hashes); off-chain personal data stays in EU.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-030 — Sanctions screening — lightweight EU + Italian UIF at onboarding (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-AD-6 confirmed.
- **Decision**: EU consolidated sanctions list + Italian UIF screening at customer onboarding (~€0.30–€1/check via ComplyAdvantage / Onfido / similar). Re-screen every 12 months and on flagged events (large transactions, country change). OFAC layered on if US shipping confirmed in I3.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-10)**: KYC re-screening trigger-event detection between 12-month sanctions re-screen cycles operates at NewCo launch via two paths — (i) **AML-threshold detection** per DEC-035 (€10k single or €50k cumulative breach fires the lightweight DEC-030 sanctions re-check + enhanced KYC review queue entry per DEC-035 ops workflow); (ii) **Compliance ad-hoc trigger** via Admin Panel for case-by-case re-screening. **Country-change automated detection is NOT enabled at NewCo launch** (signal-to-noise concerns; deferred to Phase 2+ per qa.deferred.md). Sanctions screening at the payment moment is independent of this workflow and handled at the payment-rail layer (Airwallex per BMD §10.7); E6-10 trigger-detection scope addresses re-KYC cycles, not payment-time sanctions checks. Anchored at Module K v0.2 §9.2; closes E6-10.

## DEC-031 — Localization scope across four surfaces (2026-05-01)
- **Context**: Q-AD-3 originally scoped only to bottle page; Paolo correctly flagged this should also cover consumer portal, producer portal, admin panel.
- **Decision**: CONFIRMED.
  - **Bottle page**: EN + IT + FR + DE + JP + ZH at launch. Auto-detect from browser `Accept-Language`; EN fallback; manual selector.
  - **Consumer portal**: same launch locales as bottle page. Auto-detect first visit; persist preference in profile.
  - **Producer portal**: EN + IT at launch. Add per-producer locale on opt-in (e.g., FR for Bordeaux/Burgundy houses) when needed.
  - **Admin panel**: EN + IT at launch.
  - **Data model i18n-ready from day one** regardless of launch locale set (translatable strings, locale-aware date/number/currency, locale-aware sort). Adding a locale post-launch is config, not migration.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-032 — Discovery margin model: negotiated allocation cost, not 87.5% PO (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-CL-1 in [`qa.bm.md`](../03-qa/qa.bm.md). DEC-010's "+5%" phrasing was ambiguous; v0.1 BMD modeled Discovery the same as club (87.5% PO + 12.5% margin minus 5%). Paolo clarified Discovery operates under a different mechanic.
- **Decision**: Discovery sales operate under a different margin mechanic from club sales:
  - NewCo negotiates an allocation cost C with the producer (per allocation, not formulaic).
  - NewCo sets the customer-facing Discovery price `P_d` — NewCo controls Discovery pricing; producer does not set Discovery price.
  - On sale: producer of the bottle is paid C; NewCo's gross margin is `P_d − C`.
  - 5% × `P_d` is paid to the buyer's Originating Club producer (which can be a different producer than the bottle's).
  - The producer of the bottle on Discovery does not need to have a NewCo club at all. Discovery-only suppliers are admitted.
- **Worked example**: Producer X gives NewCo a Discovery-only allocation at €100/bottle. NewCo sets Discovery price €200. Customer A buys at €200. NewCo gross margin = €100. If A's Originating Club is Producer B's club, Producer B receives €10 (5% × €200). NewCo nets €90.
- **Implication for BMD**: §0.5, §1.3, §3.1, §3.5, §3.6, §3.7, §3.10, §8.2, §8.14 require revision; Glossary updated; Appendix B updated.
- **Amends**: DEC-010 — club margin 87.5% / 12.5% remains for *club* sales; Discovery side replaced by this decision.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-033 — Renewal notice 30 days, customizable; Hero Package price stable in principle (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-1.
- **Decision**: Auto-renewal notice fires 30 days before period end; the cadence is a customizable platform setting. Hero Package price is stable year-over-year in principle (producers can adjust but the baseline expectation is no annual hike).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-034 — Lapsed grace window 30 days post-period (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-2.
- **Decision**: Lapsed memberships can be re-activated within 30 days post-period-end by paying the renewal cost without reapplying. After 30 days, terminal Cancelled; customer must reapply.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-035 — KYC threshold: €10k single / €50k cumulative annual (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-3.
- **Decision**: Trigger enhanced KYC review at €10,000 single transaction or €50,000 cumulative annual purchases per customer. Below: light EU + UIF screening per DEC-030. Above: ops review + optional document-based identity verification.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-036 — Cross-border gifting tax: customer responsibility (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-4.
- **Decision**: Customer is responsible for any gift-tax / customs implications of cross-border voucher gifting. NewCo records the transfer for audit but does not compute, withhold, or remit gift-tax. Customer terms surface a brief notice.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-037 — Customer-facing currency launch set: EUR + USD + GBP + CHF + JPY (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-5.
- **Decision**: Five currencies at launch — EUR (base), USD, GBP, CHF, JPY. Add others post-launch on demand.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-038 — FX policy mechanics deferred to PRD (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-6.
- **Decision**: BMD records the principle (EUR base, daily-snapshot mid-rate-plus-buffer); operational mechanics (snapshot time, buffer %, refresh cadence) specified in PRD.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-039 — Platform promotions: never silent on producer prices; NewCo-funded only on Discovery (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-7.
- **Decision**:
  - NewCo never silently discounts a producer-set price.
  - No NewCo-funded promotions on club offers; any club promotion requires the producer's explicit per-campaign opt-in.
  - On Discovery, NewCo controls pricing (per DEC-032) and is therefore free to run promotions without producer consent.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-040 — Discovery purchase without Originating Club: allowed; no 5% recipient (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-8.
- **Decision**: Customers without an Originating Club can purchase from Discovery. Where no Originating Club exists, no 5% accrues; full Discovery margin (`P_d − C`) goes to NewCo. Past Discovery purchases do not retroactively gain an Originating Club when the customer is later approved by a club.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-041 — Destination country list at launch: mirror Crurated; US INCLUDED; OFAC required (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-9.
- **Decision**: Launch destination countries mirror Crurated's current shipping universe, including the US. As a consequence, OFAC screening is required at customer onboarding (in addition to EU + UIF per DEC-030).
- **Amends**: DEC-030 — OFAC layered on at launch, not conditional anymore.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-042 — Producer settlement: quarterly default, agreement-configurable (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-10.
- **Decision**: Producer settlement cadence defaults to quarterly; each producer agreement can modify cadence and any related payment terms. (Confirms C10 from elicitation v1.)
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-043 — Club Credit on producer offboarding: convert to Discovery store credit at face, 12-month validity (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-11.
- **Decision**: When a Producer offboards, residual Club Credit balances of members are converted to Discovery store credit at face value, valid for 12 months from conversion.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-044 — Store-credit goodwill premium admin-configurable (default 105%) (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-12.
- **Decision**: When NewCo offers store credit as a refund alternative, the goodwill premium is admin-configurable per case (default 105% of face; ops can adjust). Customer can always opt for cash refund at 100% face.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-045 — Two-invoice model (INV1 bottle/voucher only; INV2 at shipment with excise + VAT) (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-13. Inherited pattern from Crurated v17 §0.7.
- **Decision**: Customer transactions are governed by a two-invoice mechanic mirroring Crurated:
  - **INV1 at checkout** — covers the bottle / Voucher purchase only. No excise duty, no VAT recognized at this point (destination unknown under late binding; MPV regime defers VAT recognition).
  - **INV2 at shipment** — destination known; excise duty and destination-country VAT applied to the customer total. Customer pays INV2 (or a delta against pre-paid amounts) at shipment.
- No reconciliation of estimated-vs-actual excise/VAT is needed because INV1 does not include estimates.
- **Implication for BMD**: §4.7, §5.4, §8.6, §8.7, §8.13 updated to reference INV1 / INV2 explicitly.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-046 — Storage-fee refund on partial cellar refund: pro-rata where cause warrants (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-14.
- **Decision**: When part of a cellar is refunded, accrued storage fee on the refunded item is refunded pro-rata, where the underlying refund cause makes it appropriate (e.g., NewCo-fault breakage refund — yes; customer-fraud refund — no). Cause-conditional, not blanket.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-44)**: For `customer_cancellation_pre_shipment` cause, storage-fee refund treatment covers **bottle cost only** — pre-shipment cancellation is structurally bounded by Cart Hold + Order timeout window + 14-day cancellation window; storage accrual generally has not fired in this window (12-month free starts at INV1). No auto-waiver of storage-fee for this cause. Anchored at Module S §12.6; closes E6-44.

## DEC-047 — Chargeback process via Airwallex; ops responds within 7 business days (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-15.
- **Decision**: Chargebacks handled via Airwallex's standard dispute interface; NewCo Operations owns response. Evidence package submitted within 7 business days. Loss tracked in Finance; customer flagged for fraud-pattern review on chargeback. Launch KPI target: chargeback rate under 2%.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-048 — Insurance basis deferred to Vinlock/Crurated conditions (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-16. Reverses v0.1 BMD's working baseline of "customer-paid value".
- **Decision**: Insurance basis for stored bottles is deferred — Vinlock / Crurated contractual conditions apply for now. Detailed basis (customer-paid value, market value, replacement cost) determined operationally in alignment with Vinlock contract terms; not locked at BMD level.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-049 — Bank-transfer cart-hold extension: 7 calendar days (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-17.
- **Decision**: For bank-transfer orders, cart hold extended for 7 calendar days from order placement. After that, hold expires, order voids, stock returns to available pool.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-050 — NFT legal status: provenance/authentication artifact (not legal title) (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-18.
- **Decision**: NFT acts as a provenance / authentication artifact, not legal title. Title to the wine is governed by the off-chain Italian sale-of-goods regime. Confirmed as the working stance; flagged for Italian counsel review pre-launch as non-blocking validation.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-051 — Post-shipment NFC tag damage: no re-tagging; customer service case-by-case (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-19. Amends §6.11.2 in v0.1 BMD.
- **Decision**: Post-shipment NFC tag damage is NOT remediated by re-tagging (no exception path for physical bottle return for re-tagging). Customer service handles case-by-case with options: bottle replacement (where producer/inventory permits), goodwill coupon, store credit, or other case-appropriate intervention. The non-NFT provenance certificate remains available on request.
- **Amends**: §6.11.2 (v0.1 default — re-tagging via exception was offered; now removed).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-052 — Discovery listing of non-serialized stock allowed with badge (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-20.
- **Decision**: Non-serialized bottles allowed on Discovery with a clear "non-serialized" badge on the offer. Customer-facing implication (no Bottle Page, no NFT-backed provenance) surfaced upfront. Producer or NewCo can opt out per allocation.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-053 — Bottle Page content: core only at launch (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-21.
- **Decision**: Bottle Page launches with core content only — link to NFT, provenance chain, producer profile, tasting notes, allocation context. Richer media (video, immersive, AR) deferred to post-launch.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

- **Decision**: BMD locks the principle (mint at NFC tag application). Operational details (single vs batch mint, latency tolerance, retry on chain congestion) specified in PRD Module B.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-055 — NFC/NFT recovery defaults confirmed (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Q-AD-23.
- **Decision**: All four §6.11 default policies confirmed as drafted in BMD v0.1, with one amendment:
  - §6.11.1 Damaged tag in warehouse — re-tag + new NFT with predecessor reference + burn old NFT; NewCo absorbs.
  - §6.11.2 Damaged tag post-shipment — non-NFT provenance certificate by default; physical re-tagging exception path **removed** per DEC-051; customer service case-by-case.
  - §6.11.3 NFT lost in NewCo wallet — mint new NFT linked to same NFC tag with lost-predecessor reference; NewCo absorbs.
  - §6.11.4 Bottle destroyed pre-shipment, NFT alive — burn NFT; substitute via late binding or refund per DEC-025.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

- **Decision**: Launch VAT registrations: Italian (incorporation), French (warehouse-driven), and EU One-Stop-Shop (OSS). Non-EU destinations handled via DDP / DAP shipping terms — VAT/duty paid by customer at delivery via carrier; NewCo not registered in destination. Re-evaluated quarterly post-launch as volume builds.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-059 — Producer PO model: club vs Discovery commercially distinct; data-model representation deferred to PRD (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Raised during BMD v0.2 drafting completion summary as a candidate v0.3 item. Paolo's directional answer during v0.2 review.
- **Decision**: The Producer PO concept is **commercially distinct** for club allocations vs Discovery allocations:
  - Club PO: 87.5% × `P` (per DEC-010); customer-facing price drives the producer's settled amount.
  - Discovery PO: per-unit negotiated allocation cost `C` (per DEC-032); decoupled from the customer-facing Discovery price `P_d`.
- The **data-model representation** — whether this is one PO entity with a purpose flag (`club` vs `discovery`) or two distinct PO entities — is a Module A / Module S design call **deferred to PRD work**.
- **Implication for BMD**: §3.6, §3.10, §8.10 already separate the two mechanics in prose; Glossary entry for Producer PO updated to flag the deferred modeling choice.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-060 — PRD inherits Crurated v17 as default substrate; BMD Appendix B is the divergence map (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Raised by Paolo at Wave 1 kickoff: v17's already-resolved decisions should not be re-litigated. Confirmation that the NewCo PRD inherits v17 by default, with divergences enumerated by the BMD.
- **Decision**:
  - The Crurated v17 PRD (FROZEN at `01-PRD-current/Crurated_ERP_PRD_v17.md`) is the **default substrate** for NewCo PRD work.
  - **Inheritance rule**: every v17 pattern (data model, state machine, domain event, accounting treatment, naming convention, attribute set, etc.) carries forward **unchanged** into NewCo PRD unless one of the following applies:
    1. A locked NewCo DEC (DEC-001..DEC-060 + later) modifies it.
    2. BMD v0.2 Appendix B explicitly catalogs it as a divergence (B.2 Simplified, B.3 Removed, or B.4 Net-New).
  - **Application during Stage 3 elicitation**: clarifying-question docs (`qa.mod{X}.md`) MUST NOT re-elicit on v17 patterns that are inherited unchanged. Q-CL / Q-AD questions concentrate on B.2 / B.3 / B.4 divergence surfaces, on Q-OQs deferred from BMD that touch the module, and on genuine v17 ambiguities the BMD doesn't pick. The BMD's Appendix B doubles as the divergence map for this purpose.
  - **Application during Stage 3 drafting**: Module PRD docs **cite v17 by section number** for inherited patterns; v17 prose is never copied. New PRD content is reserved for divergence surfaces and BMD-specified design calls. The PRD is not standalone vs v17 the way the BMD is — the PRD reads alongside v17 by reference.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-061 — Multi-producer composite SKU: club mixed-cases stay single-producer; Discovery inherits v17 multi-producer composite (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Paolo flagged at Wave 1 kickoff that v0.2 Appendix B.3 incorrectly listed "composite multi-producer SKU" as removed. The Discovery surface is a marketplace and should mirror Crurated's v17 selling shapes — including multi-producer composites. The single-producer constraint from DEC-019 is correct *for clubs* (a club is by definition one producer's identity) but should not extend to Discovery.
- **Decision**: The mixed-case constraint is **surface-asymmetric**:
  - **Club allocations**: mixed-case packages are always **single-producer** (DEC-019 retained for clubs). Multi-product / multi-vintage / verticals allowed; cross-producer never.
  - **Discovery allocations**: NewCo may publish **multi-producer composite SKUs** inheriting Crurated v17's §1.4 Composite SKU pattern. NewCo curates which constituents combine into a Discovery composite.
- **Settlement mechanics for multi-producer Discovery composites** (clean inheritance from v17, adapted to DEC-032's Discovery cost mechanic):
  - Each constituent bottle settles to its own producer at that allocation's per-unit negotiated cost `C_i` (per DEC-032). NewCo holds a separate Discovery allocation with cost negotiation per constituent producer.
  - NewCo's gross margin on the composite = `P_d − Σ C_i` across constituents.
  - The 5% × `P_d` Originating-Club share goes to the **buyer's single Originating Club** producer regardless of how many bottle-producers contributed (one buyer = one Originating Club = one share recipient; the 5% is on the headline `P_d`, not split per constituent).
  - Producer reporting visibility (per BMD §3.11): each constituent producer sees the aggregate-Discovery view of their constituent's sales, not the composite's other constituents.
- **Amends**: DEC-019 — refined to club-only.
- **Implication for BMD**: §0.2, §3.4 (or §4.3), §4.3, Appendix B.1 (add row), Appendix B.3 (remove "composite multi-producer SKU"), Glossary as needed.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-062 — Multi-tier membership: data model inherited from v17; launch single-tier; multi-tier is a post-launch configuration, not a migration (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Paolo flagged at Wave 1 kickoff that v0.2 Appendix B.3 listed "tiered memberships within a club" as removed. While launch keeps every club as single-tier (per B4 elicitation), the data model should retain v17's multi-tier capability so that activating a second tier later is a configuration change rather than a migration.
- **Decision**:
  - Per DEC-060's inheritance principle, NewCo's PRD **inherits v17's multi-tier club model in the data layer**. Membership / Profile / Club entities carry the tier attributes from v17 unchanged.
  - **Launch configuration**: every NewCo club at launch is configured as single-tier. The Producer Portal exposes a single tier per club; the Consumer Portal does not surface tier UI.
  - **Multi-tier activation is post-launch and configuration-only**: adding a second tier to a club is a Producer Portal configuration change (define a new tier in the club's `tiers` collection, attach members), never a database migration or schema change.
  - This decision **does not commit NewCo to ever activating multi-tier**; it commits to leaving the data-model door open at zero cost.
- **Amends**: B4 elicitation framing (single-tier per club at launch remains; data-model retention added).
- **Implication for BMD**: §3.4 (multi-brand/multi-club producers note), Appendix B.2 (refine tiered-membership entry), Appendix B.3 (remove "tiered memberships within a club").
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-063 — Direct purchase admitted as exceptional sourcing model alongside passive consignment V1+V2 (2026-05-02)
- **Context**: Surfaced during Wave 1 Module 0 elicitation. Paolo's Q-CL-2 answer ([`../03-qa/qa.mod0.md`](../03-qa/qa.mod0.md)) noted in passing that "in principle all allocations for Newco will be passive consignment v2, but there can be exceptions (pass consignment v1, but also **direct purchase** exceptionally)." Direct purchase was previously framed as OUT in BMD §3.7 and §5.1 prose alongside active consignment and drop-shipping (though never explicitly listed in §13.x out-of-scope items). Paolo confirmed on follow-up: "yes, direct purchase needs to be a potential allocation model in the system."
- **Decision**: NewCo admits **direct purchase** as a third sourcing model alongside passive consignment V1 and V2:
  - **Default** remains passive consignment V2 (stock at Vinlock; producer holds title until sell-through).
  - **Exception 1**: passive consignment V1 (stock at producer; ships to Vinlock per customer order) — for very expensive / very rare bottles per DEC-011.
  - **Exception 2 — NEW**: **direct purchase** — NewCo pays the producer / supplier outright at purchase, takes title at purchase, holds the inventory at Vinlock, and sells through to the customer with full title transfer at sale (NewCo as Seller of Record unchanged).
  - Use cases include but are not limited to: strategic stock-up on a limited release the producer will not consign; one-off Discovery sourcing where the producer prefers a clean sale; supplier relationships where outright purchase is the commercial norm (e.g., Crurated as a Discovery supplier per DEC-020 may operate this way for some allocations).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module A**: the Allocation entity carries a `sourcing_model` enum admitting `passive_consignment_v2 / passive_consignment_v1 / direct_purchase`. The enum addition is the only data-model change at allocation level; the rest of the Allocation lifecycle (visibility flag DEC-023, negotiated cost on Discovery DEC-032, etc.) is unaffected by sourcing model.
  - **Module E (Wave 5)**: direct-purchase batches emit producer-payment and title-transfer events at purchase time (not at sell-through); passive-consignment batches emit those events at sell-through. The accounting integration (Xero per DEC-028) receives these events and determines accounting treatment per its own policy. Module E records the events; it does not specify GL classification (per DEC-072 — BMD / PRD do not take positions on accounting policy; reinforces Module E boundary).
  - **Producer settlement (BMD §3.10)**: bypassed for direct-purchase batches — payment is at purchase, not at sell-through; no quarterly settlement statement entry for that batch (the producer was already paid in full at purchase). The 5% × `P_d` Originating-Club share (DEC-032) on Discovery sales of direct-purchased stock still applies and accrues to the buyer's Originating-Club producer through normal settlement.
  - **VAT / MPV regime (BMD §8.7) + INV1/INV2 mechanic (DEC-045)**: unchanged — the customer-side mechanics (Voucher, late binding, two-invoice flow) operate independently of sourcing model.
  - **Refund-cost matrix (DEC-025)**: producer-fault clawback (BMD §4.11) is harder to recover on direct-purchase batches (the producer was already paid and may not accept a clawback) — flagged for operational handling at agreement-negotiation time; not a launch blocker.
- **Amends**: DEC-011 (no longer "passive consignment only"; now "passive consignment V1+V2 default + direct purchase exception"). The "no active consignment, no drop-shipping" parts of DEC-011 stand unchanged.
- **BMD revision**: §3.7 prose "Active consignment, drop-shipping, and direct-purchase sourcing are all OUT" needs surgical edit to remove "direct-purchase" from the OUT list and add it as a third option; §5.1 needs analogous edit (section title and prose); §0.5 / §0.7 need minor updates if they reference the sourcing model; Glossary should add a Direct Purchase entry; Appendix B does not need a row (direct purchase is not a v17 carryover — it is a NewCo-specific net-new variant). **Deferred to Wave-1-end BMD v0.4 consolidation**, which will fold DEC-063 plus any other BMD-level revisions surfaced during Wave 1 elicitation in one surgical pass.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-064 — Translatable strings: i18n-keyed JSON per attribute on existing PIM entities (no separate translation registry at launch) (2026-05-03)
- **Context**: Surfaced during Wave 1 Module 0 elicitation. Q-AD-11 (Bottle Page producer-supplied content shape) and Q-AD-12 (translatable string pattern, generally) both asked for the implementation shape of DEC-031's "data-model i18n-readiness from day one". Paolo confirmed Path X / JSON-with-locale-keys on both.
- **Decision**: NewCo PIM implements translatable strings as **i18n-keyed JSON columns on existing entities** (Wine Master, Wine Variant, BR — and any other entity carrying v17 §4.8 `i18n-candidate` annotations). No separate `Translation`, `ProducerContent`, or `BottlePageContent` registry at launch.
  - **Pattern**: each translatable string field carries a JSON value of shape `{"<locale>": "<text>", ...}` with one entry per supported locale; six launch locales per DEC-031.
  - **Locale validation**: application-layer (the database column is schema-less JSON).
  - **Field-by-field i18n list**: the v17 §4.8 `i18n-candidate` set carries forward verbatim as the NewCo i18n field set (no field-level additions or removals at launch).
  - **Read profile**: single-row, no join; upserts atomic per row.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module 0 PRD draft (Wave 1)**: specifies the JSON shape and enumerates which fields are translatable (cite v17 §4.8 by section number).
  - **Module B (Wave 4) Bottle Page (DEC-053)**: producer-supplied content (tasting notes, producer profile, allocation context) reads from these JSON columns at the BR / Wine Variant / Wine Master level — no separate Bottle-Page-content entity is introduced.
  - **Future scaling**: if translation workflows grow complex post-launch (per-translator review queues, version history, fallback chains), a Y-style separate `Translation` entity can be introduced as a discrete future-DEC item; not a launch concern.
- **Amends**: DEC-031 — refines the implementation shape. DEC-053 — confirms the Bottle Page content layer is a read over PIM JSON columns, not a separate entity.
- **BMD revision**: none — this is a PRD-implementation pick that operates within DEC-031's locked scope. BMD body untouched.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-065 — Module 0 PIM scope at launch: bottled wine only (LiquidProduct stripped, no Service / Experience SKU subtype) (2026-05-03)
- **Context**: Surfaced during Wave 1 Module 0 elicitation. Q-AD-14 (LiquidProduct entity disposition) and Q-OQ-8 (Service / Experience as catalog items) both asked whether v17 PIM constructs not in NewCo's launch scope should be stripped or carried as deferred-feature hooks. Paolo confirmed "strip at launch" on Q-AD-14 and "bottled-only stance" on Q-OQ-8.
- **Decision**: NewCo Module 0 PIM at launch is **strictly bottled wine only**:
  - **LiquidProduct entity** (v17 §4.7) is **not carried into NewCo PIM**. The associated `LiquidProductCreated / Activated / Retired` events are also stripped from the NewCo Module 0 event set. (BMD §13.4 / Appendix B.3 already mark "liquid voucher resolution + pre-bottling sales" as removed.)
  - **Service / Experience SKU subtype** is **not introduced** as a SellableSKU subtype at launch. Free experiences (BMD §4.14) are booked operationally without a catalog representation; paid mechanics are deferred per Q-OQ-8 / DEC-058.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module 0 PRD draft (Wave 1)**: only bottled-wine PIM constructs (Wine Master, Wine Variant, Bottle Reference, CompositeSKU); no LiquidProduct, no Service / Experience SKU subtype.
  - **Future re-introduction**: if liquid sales (Phase 2+ per BMD §13.4) or paid services / experiences are operationalised post-launch, the corresponding entities can be re-introduced via discrete future-DEC items. Not a launch blocker.
  - **No-unused-entities posture**: this DEC formalises a broader principle the BMD already applies elsewhere (e.g., B2B fields stripped per BMD §13.2 — see [`../03-qa/qa.modK.md`](../03-qa/qa.modK.md) Q-AD-1) — entities not used at launch are stripped, not retained dormant.
- **Amends / supersedes**: none. Operationalises BMD §13.4 + Appendix B.3 + DEC-058 within Module 0 scope.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §13.4 already lists liquid sales OUT and Appendix B.3 already removes the entity. This DEC locks the PIM-side implementation choice that flows from those BMD positions.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
