## DEC-091 — Module D event catalogue at launch (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 2 Module D elicitation Q-AD-15. Locks the Module D event set at NewCo launch: v17 §8 inheritance (most events) + 2 NewCo additions.
- **Decision**: Module D emits the following event set at launch:
  - **Inherited from v17 §8** (10 events): `ProcurementIntentCreated`, `ProcurementIntentBackCommitted`, `PurchaseOrderIssued` (with ownership flag per DEC-085), `PurchaseOrderAcknowledged`, `PurchaseOrderInTransit`, `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` (Phase 1), `InboundEventCostFinalized` (Phase 2; carries landed-cost breakdown per Q-AD-7), `ConsignmentReceiptRecorded` (V2-only), `DiscrepancyResolutionRecorded` (with path enum + cost-impact payload per Q-AD-11), `SupplierPaymentCompleted` (per BMD §3.10 settlement; carries cadence context per DEC-070; preserves v12 atomicity per `project_v12_partial_po_settlement_gap` memory), `SupplierProducerLinkActivated` / `SupplierProducerLinkDeactivated`.
  - **NewCo additions** (2 events):
    - `POIssuedUnderNonActiveAgreement` (admin-override audit per Q-AD-4 — exact triggering condition pending Q-AD-4 resolution; event existence is locked by Paolo's Q-AD-15 confirmation).
    - `ReverseInboundEventRecorded` (producer recall per DEC-090).
- **Implications**:
  - Module D PRD: full event catalogue documented with v17-inheritance vs NewCo-addition flags; per DEC-073, payload field-by-field listings stay out of the PRD (event names + business signals only).
  - Module E (Wave 4+) consumes the event set at the financial-recognition layer per DEC-072.
  - Module S (Wave 3) consumes `SupplierPaymentCompleted` at the Allocation FSM trigger (cross-link DEC-086).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-060 (v17 inheritance), DEC-072 (event-only framing), DEC-073 (event names + business signals only), DEC-090 (reverse-inbound event); DEC-094 finalises `POIssuedUnderNonActiveAgreement` triggering condition (Producer-counterparty Level 1 override only).
- **BMD revision**: none — event catalogue lives at PRD level.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-25 — landed in Stage 6 editorial pass)**: The Module D event catalogue extends to enumerate the PI lifecycle's CANCELLED terminal-event explicitly. **`ProcurementIntentCancelled`** is added to the NewCo-additions group at Module D §16.2 (NewCo additions: 3 events total). Module D consumes Module S `VoucherVoided` and transitions DRAFT/COMMITTED PIs to CANCELLED with carve-outs for V2 / Direct Purchase per Module D §14.4. The transition to CANCELLED emits `ProcurementIntentCancelled` carrying the cancellation trigger source. Closes E6-25.

---

## DEC-092 — Allocation `commercial_terms` structure: shape × value, orthogonal to sourcing model and counterparty type; supersedes DEC-078 (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 2 Module D elicitation Q-CL-9. Original recommendation framed Crurated-as-Supplier sourcing as default-direct-purchase + the 12.5%/87.5% mechanic as producer-economic-only. Paolo overrode: the 12.5% margin is one specific instance of a generic percent-of-selling-price commercial-terms shape; sourcing model and commercial-terms shape are independent dimensions; passive consignment is NewCo's preferred sourcing model whenever achievable (cashflow-positive — no upfront cash), with direct purchase the FALLBACK when passive isn't on offer; intra-group framing for Crurated dropped (NewCo's ownership relationship to Crurated is undecided). Confirmed via brief 2026-05-04.
- **Decision**: Allocation carries a unified `commercial_terms` structure orthogonal to both `sourcing_model` (passive_v1 / passive_v2 / direct_purchase) and the `producer_id` / `supplier_id` counterparty pattern (DEC-082):
  - **`commercial_terms.shape`** ∈ {`fixed_per_unit`, `percent_of_selling_price`}.
  - **`commercial_terms.value`** = a per-unit amount when shape = `fixed_per_unit`; a percentage when shape = `percent_of_selling_price`.
  - **Applicability**: every sourcing × visibility × counterparty combination admits either commercial-terms shape. There is no schema constraint coupling sourcing model to commercial-terms shape; the choice reflects the negotiated commercial relationship per allocation.
  - **The 12.5%/87.5% is the club-default instance of `percent_of_selling_price`**: produces the BMD §3.10 sell-through-split mechanic (NewCo retains 12.5%; producer/supplier gets 87.5% of selling price). The same percent mechanism is admissible in Discovery and Direct Purchase contexts whenever the producer/supplier and NewCo agree to share the selling price rather than fix a per-unit cost.
  - **Sourcing-model preference at NewCo**: passive consignment is the preferred sourcing model for both Club and Discovery (cashflow-positive); direct purchase is the FALLBACK when passive isn't on offer.
  - **Crurated-as-Supplier framing**: drops intra-group assumption per Paolo (NewCo's ownership relationship to Crurated is undecided). Crurated is one Discovery Supplier on standard commercial terms (DEC-020); commercial-terms shape is per-allocation, same as any other Supplier.
- **Implications**:
  - **DEC-078 SUPERSEDED** — the two-field design (`producer_price` for club + `negotiated_cost` for Discovery) collapses into the unified `commercial_terms` structure. Module A PRD drafts against `commercial_terms`, not the prior two-field split. The naming reflects what the field IS (commercial terms negotiated per allocation) rather than which channel uses it.
  - **Module D PRD** PO line read: PO references `commercial_terms.shape` + `commercial_terms.value`; for `fixed_per_unit`, PO line is `value × qty`; for `percent_of_selling_price`, PO settles at sell-through with `value% × selling_price × qty`.
  - **Discovery PO timing** (cross-link DEC-086): if Discovery allocation is passive consignment, PO timing is sell-through-cadence regardless of commercial-terms shape; if direct purchase, PO timing is at-PO-payment regardless of commercial-terms shape. **Sourcing model drives timing; commercial-terms shape drives the value computation**.
  - **NewCo prefers passive consignment for Discovery** — Module D PRD prose reflects this default rather than the original Q-CL-9 "direct purchase as Discovery default" framing (which was rejected).
  - Producer-recall mechanics (DEC-090) and inbound-receiving-party rule (DEC-088) are unaffected — both are independent of commercial-terms shape.
- **Amends / supersedes**: **supersedes DEC-078**. Refines DEC-020 (Crurated-as-Supplier on standard commercial terms; intra-group dropped). Composes with DEC-082 (counterparty pattern), DEC-086 (PO timing per sourcing model), DEC-093 (procurement flow uniformity).
- **BMD revision**: required at Wave-2-end v0.6 consolidation. BMD §3.10 12.5%/87.5% prose generalises from "club economic mechanism" to "percent-of-selling-price shape; club default 12.5%/87.5%". Glossary entry for "Sell-through" generalises likewise. §12.1 table entry for DEC-078 refreshes to reflect supersession by DEC-092.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-093 — ProcurementIntent / PurchaseOrder / InboundEvent flow uniform across sourcing models; trigger + timing parameterised (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 2 Module D elicitation Q-AD-1. Recommendation framed Direct Purchase as a "carve-out" with separate auto-vs-manual PI trigger and at-PO-vs-sell-through PO timing. Paolo pushed back: "direct purchase was also present in v17; the flow should be the same". Confirmed via brief 2026-05-04 — flow shape is uniform; trigger + timing parameterise per sourcing model.
- **Decision**: The Module D procurement flow shape — `ProcurementIntent` → `PurchaseOrder` → `InboundEvent` (PHYSICALLY_ACCEPTED + COST_FINALIZED) → optional `ConsignmentReceipt` (V2 only) — is **uniform across all sourcing models**. What parameterises per sourcing model:
  - **PI trigger**:
    - **V1 (passive consignment, customer-order-driven)**: PI auto-fires at voucher issuance.
    - **V2 (passive consignment, pre-positioned)**: PI auto-fires at voucher issuance (referencing already-arrived stock).
    - **Direct Purchase**: PI manually created by NewCo ops at allocation creation time (operator-initiated; surfaced from Producer Portal + Admin Panel per DEC-083).
  - **PO timing** (per DEC-086):
    - **V1**: PO at producer-settlement-cadence (per ProducerAgreement, DEC-070).
    - **V2**: PO at sell-through-settlement cadence (financial PO against pre-positioned stock).
    - **Direct Purchase**: PO at PI creation (operator-initiated, full-amount-at-purchase financial commitment).
  - **Allocation FSM trigger** (Module A — DEC-081): `SupplierPaymentCompleted` triggers DRAFT → ACTIVE for Direct Purchase; producer-commitment for V1/V2.
- **Implications**:
  - Module D PRD: single procurement flow described once; sourcing-model parameterisation table summarises trigger + timing per sourcing model. **No separate "Direct Purchase flow" or "Direct Purchase PI subtype" in the data model.**
  - Refines DEC-063 (Direct Purchase as third sourcing model) — DEC-063 introduces the sourcing-model enum value but does NOT imply a separate procurement flow shape; this DEC explicitly establishes flow-uniformity to prevent future PRD drafting drift toward over-engineering Direct Purchase as a separate flow.
- **Amends / supersedes**: refines DEC-063; composes with DEC-070 (settlement cadence), DEC-081 (Allocation FSM trigger), DEC-086 (PO timing), DEC-091 (event catalogue), DEC-092 (commercial-terms shape — orthogonal to flow uniformity).
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §3.7 / §5.1 don't claim a separate Direct Purchase flow; PRD-level clarification suffices.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-094 — PO issuance two-level gate: ProducerAgreement umbrella for Producer counterparties + valid Allocation state for all (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 2 Module D elicitation Q-AD-4. Recommendation framed PO issuance gating against ProducerAgreement state uniformly. Paolo flagged confusion: ProducerAgreement regulates the CLUB relationship (and only partially the allocation); the agreement that regulates individual allocations is the per-allocation commercial terms (DEC-084 + DEC-092). Confirmed via brief 2026-05-04 — two-level gate model with branching by counterparty type.
- **Decision**: PO issuance applies a **two-level gate** depending on PO counterparty:
  - **Producer-counterparty POs** (counterparty = Module K Producer, with or without delegated Supplier per DEC-082):
    - **Level 1 — ProducerAgreement umbrella**: the Producer's ProducerAgreement (Module K §4.6, DEC-070) must be in `active` state. Blocks PO if `draft / superseded / terminated`. Operator override surface (`POIssuedUnderNonActiveAgreement` audit event per DEC-091) for in-flight commitments under terminating agreements.
    - **Level 2 — Allocation state**: the source Allocation must be in valid sellable state (Module A FSM per DEC-081 + DEC-077).
  - **Supplier-not-Producer-counterparty POs** (counterparty = Module K Supplier without a Producer counterparty; DEC-082 admitted pattern):
    - **Level 1 — N/A** (no SupplierAgreement entity at launch per DEC-084; supplier commercial terms live at allocation level per DEC-092).
    - **Level 2 — Allocation state** is the only gate: valid sellable Allocation state required.
  - **`POIssuedUnderNonActiveAgreement` event** (DEC-091 catalogue) fires only on the Producer-counterparty path Level 1 override; not applicable to Supplier-not-Producer POs (no umbrella to override).
- **Implications**:
  - Module D PRD: two-level gate documented with explicit branching by counterparty type. Cross-link to DEC-070 (ProducerAgreement lifecycle), DEC-082 (counterparty pattern), DEC-084 (no SupplierAgreement entity), DEC-091 (event catalogue including POIssuedUnderNonActiveAgreement), DEC-092 (commercial-terms shape).
  - Two-tier conceptual model from DEC-084 + this DEC: **ProducerAgreement is umbrella** (club-relationship-level); **per-allocation commercial terms** (DEC-092) are specific (transaction-level). The two are independent gates with different scopes.
  - Cross-link to qa.modA Q-CL-7's allocation-lifecycle policy (Allocation lifecycle is orthogonal to ProducerAgreement transitions per DEC-077; this DEC adds the umbrella-state gating discipline at PO issuance, which is distinct from ongoing per-allocation operations).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-070, DEC-077, DEC-082, DEC-084, DEC-091, DEC-092. Refines Q-AD-4 recommendation framing.
- **BMD revision**: none — gating rule lives at Module D PRD level.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-095 — Offer entity as separate first-class entity at NewCo (Wave 3 Module S Q-CL-10) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-CL-10. After DEC-076 collapsed Allocation visibility to 2-value with sibling Allocation rows per visibility, the relationship between Allocation and Offer at NewCo was ambiguous. Two plausible interpretations: separate first-class Offer entity (v17 §5.2 inheritance) vs Offer collapsed onto Allocation row.
- **Decision**: Offer is a **separate first-class entity** at NewCo, inheriting v17 §5.2 baseline. Multi-Offer-per-Allocation pattern explicitly admitted (per DEC-099): one Allocation can carry multiple Offers (bottle Offer + case Offer + Hero Package Offer + time-windowed promotion Offer) all reading the same Allocation pool with shared-pool decrement at sell-through.
- **Implications**: Offer ↔ Allocation cardinality is N:1 (single-Allocation Offer) or N:M (multi-producer Discovery composite per DEC-097); Offer carries its own FSM (DRAFT → REVIEWED → SUBMITTED → ACTIVE → PAUSED → CLOSED), pricing surface, granularity, eligibility filters, time-window, Layer 3 commercial_unbreakable. Producer-relationship state (Allocation lifecycle, mutability per DEC-079) stays separate from commercial-presentation state (Offer publication).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-060, DEC-076, DEC-082, DEC-099, DEC-100, DEC-115.
- **BMD revision**: none — entity boundary lives at Module S PRD level; BMD §4.5 already defers to PRD work.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-096 — Hero Package = boolean flag on Offer with three conditional concerns (Wave 3 Module S Q-CL-11) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-CL-11. BMD glossary calls Hero Package "Module S Offer-level designation" but does not lock data shape. Three plausible interpretations: boolean flag on Offer / Offer subtype / separate entity.
- **Decision**: Hero Package = `Offer.is_hero_package` boolean flag (default `false`) with three Hero-Package-conditional concerns: (1) **single-purchase-per-Profile-per-club-year** enforced at order completion; (2) **Capacity Invariant** cross-check at order completion against Module K v0.2 §13 (Active Profiles ≤ Allocation.qty); (3) **`MembershipFeePaid` event** emission on Hero Package purchase (Module K consumer per qa.modK §15.5), in addition to standard `OrderCompleted` / `VoucherIssued` events.
- **Implications**: Module 0 v0.2 §3.7 framing preserved (Hero Package is NOT a PIM Composite SKU attribute; it lives at Module S Offer level). Module K v0.2 §13 Capacity Invariant reads `Allocation.qty` at runtime per DEC-079 mutability. Hero Package = N vouchers (one per constituent bottle per DEC-109 1-voucher-per-bottle invariant); the membership-fee character is at Order/Offer level, not Voucher level. Cross-link DEC-114 (three-gate eligibility check at checkout).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-007 (Hero Package = Membership), DEC-069 (mid-year capacity mutability), DEC-079 (qty mutability generalised), DEC-095 (Offer entity), DEC-114 (eligibility gate).
- **BMD revision**: none — flag-on-Offer pattern aligns with BMD glossary "Module S Offer-level designation" framing.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-097 — Multi-producer Discovery composite Offer publication = ONE composite Offer reading N Allocations atomically (Wave 3 Module S Q-CL-12) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-CL-12. Per DEC-061, multi-producer Discovery composite SKUs are admissible; per qa.modA Q-AD-11 / DEC-082 follow-through, Module S binds N constituent Allocations atomically at Offer publication. The data shape was unconfirmed: ONE composite Offer reading from N Allocations vs N grouped Offers under a parent Offer.
- **Decision**: Multi-producer Discovery composite = **ONE composite Offer (single Offer row) referencing N constituent Allocations atomically**. Offer carries `composite_constituent_allocation_ids[]` (single FK for non-composite Offers; multi-FK for multi-producer Discovery composites). Customer-facing `P_d` lives on the Offer; per-constituent cost `C_i` reads constituent `Allocation.commercial_terms.value` at sell-through emission time (no caching, per qa.modA Q-AD-12 read-at-emission). Atomic decrement across N constituents at sale.
- **Implications**: Mid-life rules: any constituent Allocation transitioning ACTIVE → CLOSED forces composite Offer to PAUSED; capacity-decrease on any constituent re-validates against composite-Offer issued count (anti-orphan rule per DEC-079); composite Offer cannot violate any constituent's Layer 1+2 breakability constraints (per DEC-095 / Layer 3). Originating Club 5% × P_d share computed once on the composite Offer's headline `P_d` (NOT per-constituent), single OC recipient resolved via `Customer.originating_club_id` per DEC-066.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-061 (multi-producer composite admitted), DEC-066 (OC FK target), DEC-082 (Module S composite binding contract), DEC-092 (commercial_terms shape × value), DEC-095 (Offer entity), DEC-098 (publication validation), DEC-112 (OC share emission).
- **BMD revision**: none — composite binding pattern lives at Module S PRD level; BMD §4.3 already defers data shape to PRD.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-098 — Module S Offer publication 5-rule validation contract (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-2) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-2. Module S Offer publication validation rule set was implicit in upstream Wave 1 + 2 locks but not explicitly contracted.
- **Decision**: Module S verifies five rules at Offer publication (DRAFT/SUBMITTED → ACTIVE transition): (1) **Allocation state** = ACTIVE for each bound Allocation; (2) **visibility match strict** (Offer surface ↔ Allocation visibility per DEC-076 2-value enum); (3) **serialization alignment** with `non_serialized_offer_admitted` per DEC-080; (4) **`commercial_terms.value` populated** per DEC-092; (5) **Layer 3 cannot downgrade Layer 2** (effective rule = Layer 2 OR Layer 3 per Module 0 v0.2 §7.4). Composite Offer publication: all N constituent Allocations must satisfy + mid-life violations cascade to PAUSED per DEC-097.
- **Implications**: `OfferPublicationValidationFailed` event emitted on validation failure with reason payload. Per DEC-073, PRD names rules + events; tech team picks the violation-error UX.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-076, DEC-080, DEC-081, DEC-092, DEC-095, DEC-097.
- **BMD revision**: none — validation contract lives at Module S PRD level.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-21)**: Validation rule (5) — "Layer 3 cannot downgrade Layer 2" — governs the **default** Offer-creation path. Layer 2 propagates as the default Layer 3 value: at Module S Offer creation, Layer 3 defaults to the bound Allocation's Layer 2 producer-breakability for each Case Configuration; an operator-without-action publishes the Offer with `effective_unbreakable` matching the Producer's declaration. Stage 6.5 admits an explicit **operator-override path** for the rare commercial exception: the operator may deliberately set Layer 3 to breakable on a Layer-2-unbreakable Allocation via Admin Panel UI with **mandatory reason capture** (free-text reason + operator ID + timestamp) for audit trail. Override is a deliberate, audited action; default behavior remains rule (5)'s strict rejection. When override is exercised, Layer 3 (override-set value) is the binding fulfillment rule; Module C late-binding optimization is preserved (reads only Layer 3 final value). Producer-relationship management around the override decision (notify producer, retro-coordination) is operating-manual scope per `feedback_prd_rr_approval`. Anchored at Module 0 v0.2 §7.4 + Module S Offer-creation prose; closes E6-21. Note: qa.editorial.md §6 E6-21 row referenced "DEC-126" — that was an editorial mistake; the correct anchor is DEC-098 (this DEC) per Module 0 §7.4 + Module S Offer-publication validation.

---

## DEC-099 — Multi-Offer per Allocation pattern + shared-pool decrement contract (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-3) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-3. NewCo admits multiple Offers publishing off a single Allocation; the cross-Offer atomicity rule was not explicit.
- **Decision**: Multi-Offer-per-Allocation pattern is admitted. Each Offer's voucher issuance decrements the shared `Allocation.available_qty = qty - issued`; first-to-consume-last-unit wins; subsequent issuance fails with `AllocationCapacityExhausted` until capacity restored or new units added per DEC-079. Bottle Offer + case Offer + Hero Package Offer + time-windowed promotion Offer all reading the same Allocation pool is the canonical pattern.
- **Implications**: Cross-Offer atomicity at sell-through is a Module S concern; Allocation `qty` is the cross-Offer ceiling. Offers publishing off the same Allocation may have independent FSMs, pricing surfaces, time-windows, granularities, Hero Package designations, Layer 3 settings.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-079, DEC-095, DEC-098, DEC-100.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-100 — Offer pricing surface derivation + Offer-level promotion overlay (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-4) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-4. Offer pricing derivation from Allocation `commercial_terms` was implied by DEC-092 but the promotional overlay pattern (per DEC-039) was not explicit.
- **Decision**: Offer pricing derives strictly from Allocation `commercial_terms` (per DEC-092 shape × value): for `shape = fixed_per_unit`, club P = `value × 100 / 87.5` for club Offers, Discovery P_d = NewCo-set on Offer with `value` as cost C; for `shape = percent_of_selling_price`, producer share = `value × selling_price`. Promotion overlay per DEC-039: `Offer.promotional_price` is Offer-level overlay (Allocation untouched); producer-opt-in via `ProducerPromotionConsent` event referencing campaign for club promotions; absent consent, NewCo absorbs the discount on its margin.
- **Implications**: For percent_of_selling_price shape, promotional discount passes through to producer proportionally; for fixed_per_unit shape, producer cost stays fixed and NewCo absorbs the entire promotional discount. Sell-through settlement always reads Allocation `commercial_terms`, not the Offer's promotional_price.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-039 (producer opt-in for club promotions), DEC-092 (commercial_terms shape × value), DEC-095, DEC-099.
- **BMD revision**: none — overlay pattern aligns with BMD §4.12 framing.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-101 — Order FSM v17 inheritance + PENDING_PAYMENT as bank-transfer credit-terms state; no other B2C credit-terms at launch (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-5) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-5. Paolo flagged: "we need to deal somehow with credit terms for members that pay via bank transfer; is the PENDING_PAYMENT status accounting for it?"
- **Decision**: Order FSM inherits v17 §5.6 verbatim (12-state machine: PENDING_PAYMENT → PAYMENT_CONFIRMED → CONFIRMED → FULFILLMENT_STARTED → PARTIALLY_FULFILLED → FULFILLED + HOLD_PLACED + AMENDMENT_REQUESTED + AMENDMENT_APPROVED + AMENDMENT_REJECTED + CANCELLED), with NewCo simplifications (B2B credit-terms branches DEFERRED per DEC-068; active-consignment-driven branches DROPPED per BMD §13; CruTrade-related branches DROPPED per BMD §4.4). **PENDING_PAYMENT IS the bank-transfer credit-terms state at NewCo launch**. The flow: customer cart-submits with payment_method = bank_transfer → Cart Hold extends to 7 calendar days per DEC-049; Order in PENDING_PAYMENT; Voucher in PENDING_PAYMENT pre-state (per DEC-102); Allocation reservation held for 7-day window; **INV1 NOT issued until funds clear** at Airwallex; on funds-cleared, PENDING_PAYMENT → ISSUED, INV1 fires (per DEC-107), Order PENDING_PAYMENT → CONFIRMED. Customer fails to complete bank-transfer in 7 days → hold expires; voucher auto-VOIDS without INV1 issuance; Allocation reservation releases; no financial event.
- **Implications**: **No other B2C credit-terms flow at launch** — card payments authorize-and-capture in one step (no PENDING_PAYMENT for cards); B2B credit-terms (e.g., net-30) DEFERRED per DEC-068. The 7-day bank-transfer window is the ONLY credit-terms-equivalent at launch. Voucher in PENDING_PAYMENT is non-shippable (Module C fulfilment gates on Voucher state ≥ ISSUED).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-049 (bank-transfer 7-day extension), DEC-068 (B2B segment dropped), DEC-102 (Voucher state machine), DEC-107 (INV1 / INV2 events), DEC-105 (Cart Hold default).
- **BMD revision**: none — PENDING_PAYMENT framing aligns with BMD §4.7 saved-payment-method commitment.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-102 — Voucher state machine = 8 states with ON_CRUTRADE drop + RESOLVED + BOUGHT_BACK defer (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-6) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-6. v17 carries multiple voucher states; NewCo simplifications dictated by BMD scope-out (CruTrade + active consignment + liquid sales OUT).
- **Decision**: NewCo Voucher state machine at launch = **8 states**: PENDING_PAYMENT (bank-transfer pre-state per DEC-049 / DEC-101) → ISSUED → REDEMPTION_REQUESTED → SHIPPED → CONSUMED + VOIDED / EXPIRED / GIFTED. Drops:
  - **v17 ON_CRUTRADE** state DROPPED at launch (no CruTrade marketplace per BMD §4.4).
  - **v17 RESOLVED + BottlingResolution N:M reissuance** machinery DEFERRED at launch (no liquid-voucher product per BMD §13; Crurated v13 Stage 2.2 design is preserved as known-good template if NewCo introduces liquid vouchers post-launch).
  - **v17 BOUGHT_BACK** state DEFERRED (post-launch capability per BMD §13).
- **Implications**: GIFTED state covers transfer-pending phase per DEC-116. PENDING_PAYMENT state covers bank-transfer credit-terms phase per DEC-101. EXPIRED state IN at launch with allocation_expiry_date trigger per DEC-103.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-049, DEC-101, DEC-103, DEC-116, DEC-117. Cites BMD §4.4 + §9.7 + §13 + Appendix B.2.
- **BMD revision**: none — state set already locked in BMD §9.7.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-103 — Voucher EXPIRED state IN at launch with allocation_expiry_date trigger (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-7) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-7. EXPIRED state listed in BMD §9.7 but trigger and refund policy unspecified.
- **Decision**: Voucher EXPIRED state IN at NewCo launch. Trigger = scheduled job firing on bound `Allocation.expiry_date` for any voucher not yet REDEMPTION_REQUESTED / SHIPPED / CONSUMED / VOIDED / GIFTED. `Allocation.expiry_date` is optional (default null = no expiry); when null, voucher persists indefinitely. Refund policy on EXPIRED: customer-fault default = no refund per DEC-025 matrix; NewCo-fault EXPIRED (e.g., Direct Purchase voucher in-transit per DEC-081 prevents redemption) = NewCo-fault matrix entry refund.
- **Implications**: Producer-relationship use cases (Hero Package, time-bound vintage releases, end-of-year clearance) get an expiry mechanism via Allocation.expiry_date setting at allocation creation or via mutation per DEC-079.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-025 (refund-cost matrix), DEC-079 (qty mutability, may extend to expiry_date mutability post-launch), DEC-081 (Direct Purchase ACTIVE before physical receipt), DEC-102.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-08)**: Voucher EXPIRED is a long-tail operational state at NewCo launch. **Default Voucher expiry is 10-20 years** from issuance, aligned with fine-wine aging horizons; expiry is configurable per Allocation at Admin Panel. The Voucher sale completes at INV1 (`PaymentCaptureSucceeded`) — customer pays for the wine and receives the Voucher (the right to redeem); bottle ownership remains with NewCo until Voucher redemption at shipment-request, when the customer pays VAT / duties / shipping and ownership transfers from NewCo to customer. **At Voucher EXPIRY the redemption right lapses without refund of the INV1 payment** (the customer's option-like right has expired; the commercial sale of the Voucher is preserved); bottle ownership has never transferred; NewCo handles physical bottle disposition ad-hoc per Admin Panel (write-off via DEC-132, return-to-Producer for V1/V2 via DEC-090, or resale via fresh sibling Allocation are all available case-by-case). No VAT / duty unwind — none was ever paid. EXPIRED is structurally rare at launch given the long expiry horizon; no automated disposition path is locked into the spec. The customer-fault refund-matrix-entry (above) holds as the default — explicit no-refund — for the long-expiry case; NewCo-fault EXPIRED scenarios (e.g., Direct Purchase prevented from redemption) remain on the NewCo-fault matrix path. Anchored at Module S §11.4; closes E6-08 + E6-15 + E6-16.

---

## DEC-104 — Voucher reissuance / substitution = manual operator capability at launch; passive-consignment-makes-rare framing (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-8) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-8. BMD §3.13 names producer-offboarding voucher-substitution mechanic; Crurated lineage (memory `project_v12_consignment_recall_gap`) has acknowledged but unmodeled mechanics. Paolo: "should be edge case; with passive consignment NewCo will always be in position to honour the vouchers."
- **Decision**: Manual operator capability at launch via NewCo Admin Panel: operator records `VoucherSubstitutionExecuted` event (original Voucher → substitute Bottle Reference / SKU + reason); customer notification surface separate; refund-vs-substitute decision per DEC-025 matrix. Passive consignment as NewCo-preferred sourcing per DEC-092 keeps substitution scenarios rare (producer relationships continue mid-offboarding; residual stock or comparable-producer arrangement typically resolves). Full automation (catalogue-driven substitute matching, automated customer notification flow) deferred to Phase 2+.
- **Implications**: Cross-link DEC-090 (voucher void on recall — distinct from substitution) + DEC-117 (recall scope unsold-only — substitution applies to ISSUED vouchers when producer-offboarding committed-but-not-yet-shipped vouchers need alternate stock).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-025, DEC-090, DEC-092 (passive-consignment-default framing), DEC-117. References BMD §3.13.
- **BMD revision**: none — framing aligns with BMD §3.13's existing prose.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-20)**: Substitution refund-vs-credit consent capture — the customer's consent gate captures refund-vs-credit-vs-silent-absorption choice **before the substitution executes**. Implementation surface: `customer_consent_mode ∈ {refund, credit, silent}` payload field on `VoucherSubstitutionExecuted` event; operator captures consent at substitution-proposal time via Customer Care touchpoint. The consent gate addresses the buyer-experience severity Phase 4 W-BO-08 escalated as REAL_BUG. Anchored at Module S §11.5 + §12.3; closes E6-20.

---

## DEC-105 — Cart Hold timeout = 15 minutes default, system-wide configurable (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-9) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-9. BMD §4.6 explicitly defers cart-hold timeout duration to PRD work; v17 §5.7 default is 15 minutes.
- **Decision**: Cart Hold timeout = **15 minutes default**, system-wide configurable by NewCo ops, NOT per-Offer (v17 §5.7 inheritance). Bank-transfer extension to 7 calendar days per DEC-049 / DEC-106 / DEC-101 is the only payment-method-conditional override at launch.
- **Implications**: Cart session timeout is 48 hours (separate v17 mechanic — cart contents persist 48 hours but holds release at 15 min unless re-acquired). Pricing snapshot at re-add is at-that-moment per DEC-038 FX policy.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-038 (FX policy), DEC-049 (bank-transfer extension), DEC-101, DEC-106.
- **BMD revision**: none — value lives at Module S PRD level.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-106 — Cart Hold strict-timeout discipline; no re-extension on customer activity (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-10) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-10. Cart Hold timer behaviour on customer interaction was unspecified.
- **Decision**: **Strict-timeout** discipline locked at NewCo: 15-minute hold timer counts down regardless of customer interaction; customer activity (browsing, cart adjustments) does NOT reset the timer. Only DEC-049 bank-transfer payment-method selection extends the timer (to 7 calendar days). Cart-session-vs-cart-hold distinction preserved per v17 §5.7.
- **Implications**: Long-browse customers cannot indefinitely block other customers from scarce Allocation capacity. Cart contents persist 48 hours (cart session) but Allocation reservations release at 15 min unless re-acquired.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-049, DEC-101, DEC-105.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-107 — INV1 / INV2 issuance event names + business signals (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-13) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-13. INV1 + INV2 event names + business-signal payload composition needed locking per DEC-073 (event names + business signals only; tech team picks payload schema).
- **Decision**: Module S emits two customer-facing invoice events:
  - **`InvoiceINV1Issued`** at order confirmation (post-payment-cleared per DEC-112): business signals = Order ref + Customer ref + Profile ref (for club / Hero Package) + Voucher refs + total amount + currency + Address ref (with optional company_name + vat_id per DEC-068) + OC 5% × P_d carve-out (Discovery sales per DEC-112). MPV VAT regime: no excise / no destination VAT on INV1.
  - **`InvoiceINV2Issued`** at shipment / fulfilment: business signals = original INV1 ref + Voucher ref (REDEMPTION_REQUESTED → SHIPPED transition) + shipping Address ref + excise amount + destination-jurisdiction VAT.
  - **Hero Package**: one INV1 covering the package + N `VoucherIssued` events per constituent bottle; INV2 fires per shipped constituent.
  - **Ship-on-confirmation case**: distinct INV1 + INV2 fire simultaneously; collapsing into combined event REJECTED (would lose v17 INV1/INV2 trace + DEC-045 commitment).
- **Implications**: Per DEC-073, PRD names events + signals; tech team picks payload schema. Module D's supplier-side payment events stay domain-separated per DEC-089.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-045 (INV1/INV2 mechanic), DEC-068 (company-billing affordance), DEC-073, DEC-089 (customer-facing-only domain separation), DEC-101 (PENDING_PAYMENT for bank-transfer), DEC-109 (1-voucher-per-bottle), DEC-112 (OC share emission timing).
- **BMD revision**: none — event signal list aligns with BMD §8.13 framing.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-108 — 14-day cancellation window: timer-start at INV1; cancellation right WAIVED post-shipment (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-14) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-14. Recommendation framed "Z — at delivery confirmation, with X for cellared vouchers" per generic EU-Distance-Contracts framing. Paolo: "OK for INV-1 for voucher sales; once shipped, please double check v17 — the idea is that it's NOT possible to get the refund. Customer waives the right at moment of shipping (too complicated + expensive to bring those back + provenance compromised)." v17 verification confirms (lines 109 / 234 / 386 / 3768 / 3849): "14-day customer cancellation window from order confirmation, **pre-shipment only**, full refund (binary — no partials)"; "Once an SO has entered shipped state, cancellation is not available. No refund after shipping."
- **Decision**: 14-day cancellation window timer-start = **INV1 issuance** (= post-payment-cleared per DEC-112 = order confirmation). Window applies **ONLY pre-shipment** (Voucher in PENDING_PAYMENT / ISSUED / REDEMPTION_REQUESTED states); once Voucher transitions REDEMPTION_REQUESTED → SHIPPED, cancellation right is **WAIVED** (customer cannot cancel post-shipment). Rationale: returning shipped wine compromises provenance + temperature integrity + reverse-logistics cost prohibitive. Permitted under EU Distance Contracts Directive 2011/83/EU Article 16 (withdrawal right does not apply to "goods which are liable to deteriorate or expire rapidly" — wine post-shipment qualifies). Customer-facing T&C must clearly disclose the waiver-at-shipment rule.
- **Implications**: Post-delivery issues (damage / loss / fault) handled via Module C returns + replacement flow (NOT Module S cancellation); replacement shipment issued (no new voucher, no new INV2 per v17 line 3768); cost recorded as non-revenue event by Module E. Exceptional post-delivery refunds require supervisor override (auditable). Voucher VOIDED on cancellation in pre-shipment window → Allocation `qty - issued` restored per DEC-079.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-025 (refund-cost matrix), DEC-057 (Italian/EU consumer-law working baseline), DEC-079 (capacity-restored-on-void), DEC-102 (Voucher state machine), DEC-109 (per-voucher partial refund), DEC-112 (post-payment-cleared timing).
- **BMD revision**: required at Wave-3-end v0.7 consolidation. BMD §4.10 (Cancellation) and BMD §4.11 (Refund) need explicit "pre-shipment only" prose + post-shipment WAIVED rule + EU Distance Contracts Article 16 carve-out citation.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-109 — Partial refund per voucher; 1-voucher-per-bottle invariant (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-15) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-15. Partial-refund mechanic + voucher granularity needed locking. Paolo: "Yes confirmed, please remember that it's always 1 voucher = 1 bottle (NOT 1 voucher = 1 Hero Package, for example)."
- **Decision**: **1-voucher-per-bottle invariant locked**: vouchers are bottle-granular at NewCo launch (one Voucher row per bottle, regardless of Offer granularity). Hero Package = N vouchers (one per constituent bottle); 12-bottle case Offer purchase = 12 vouchers; multi-producer Discovery composite of 6 bottles = 6 vouchers (one per constituent bottle, per constituent Allocation per DEC-097). **Partial refund mechanic per voucher**: cancelling one voucher in a multi-voucher Order = void that voucher + refund per-bottle amount (proportional split of any package-level pricing); Allocation `qty - issued` restored per voucher; Order transitions PARTIALLY_FULFILLED until all vouchers resolve.
- **Implications**: Hero Package partial refund: N constituent vouchers individually voidable in 14-day pre-shipment window (per DEC-108); membership-status implications of partial-Hero-Package cancellation handled at Module K side. Module D V1/V2 PI auto-fire + Module E settlement events all fire per voucher (per DEC-093 procurement uniformity + DEC-086 PO timing).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-093, DEC-097, DEC-108, DEC-112.
- **BMD revision**: none — 1-voucher-per-bottle aligns with BMD §4.4 voucher framing.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-110 — Stacking algebra: v17 7-step chain + mutual-exclusivity matrix; OC 5% on headline P_d (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-16) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-16. BMD §4.12 explicitly defers stacking algebra to PRD work.
- **Decision**: Module S inherits v17's **7-step price-resolution chain**: (1) Allocation commercial_terms / Price Book lookup; (2) Policy discounts; (3) Club credit; (4) Promo codes / coupons; (5) Volume / early-bird multipliers; (6) FX conversion; (7) Final price (immutable at order). Mutual-exclusivity matrix per v17 §5.14: promo + club credit ME; REFUND_COMPENSATION + promo ME; REFUND_COMPENSATION + club credit ALLOWED. **Originating Club 5% × P_d share computed on headline P_d (NOT post-stacking net price)** per BMD §8.14 — preserves originating-club-producer economic interest regardless of NewCo's discount discretion.
- **Implications**: Per DEC-073, algebra described as ordered application + named exclusion rules; tech team implements computation pipeline. NewCo Club Credit (per Module K v0.2 §11) substitutes for v17 club-credit at step 3.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-032 (5% × P_d), DEC-039 (promo opt-in), DEC-066 (OC FK), DEC-111 (Club Credit auto-apply), DEC-112 (OC share emission).
- **BMD revision**: none — algebra lives at Module S PRD level.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-111 — Club Credit auto-apply at checkout for eligible cart; customer can remove (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-17) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-17. Recommendation: Y — checkout-apply line-level. Paolo added: "if there is club credit and at checkout there is an offer from that club, the credit should appear automatically at checkout (user can remove that coupon, but it's there by default, for the capacity needed)."
- **Decision**: When a customer has Club Credit on a Profile AND the cart contains at least one line eligible (Offer from that Profile's Club), Module S **auto-applies the credit at checkout-render time** to eligible line(s) up to **capacity needed** (= min(`credit.balance`, sum of eligible line totals)). Customer can **remove** the credit via explicit UX action (keeps cash payment + reserves credit for later; removal voluntary). Multi-Profile customer: each credit auto-applies to its respective eligible lines (no cross-Club credit pooling per Module K v0.2 §11.2 strict `credit.profile.club_id` match).
- **Implications**: Default UX surface = credit pre-applied; non-default action = remove. Eligibility + capacity-needed semantics cross-link Module K v0.2 §11.2 read pattern. Per DEC-073, PRD names UX behaviour; tech team picks rendering implementation.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-043 (Club Credit conversion at offboarding), DEC-110 (stacking step 3 = club credit), Module K v0.2 §11.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-112 — Originating Club 5% × P_d share emission at INV1 (post-payment-cleared) (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-19) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-19. Trigger event for `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` was unconfirmed. Paolo: "X (at OrderCompleted/INV1) — important part is that after the order has been paid and payment has cleared."
- **Decision**: `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` fires at **INV1 issuance**, which is **post-payment-cleared** (NOT post-payment-authorized; NOT at OrderPlaced). Specifically:
  - **Card payments**: authorize-and-capture is one step → INV1 + OC share fire together at OrderCompleted.
  - **Bank-transfer payments** (per DEC-049 / DEC-101): INV1 + OC share fire when bank-transfer funds clear at Airwallex (PENDING_PAYMENT → ISSUED transition); NOT at customer cart-submit.
- **Implications**: Tying the share to payment-cleared (not payment-authorized) prevents accruing OC share on Orders that ultimately fail (bank-transfer never received, card auth reversed). Aligns with Module D `SupplierPaymentCompleted` discipline (DEC-086). Read-at-emission per qa.modA Q-AD-12 / DEC-066: payload reads `Customer.originating_club_id` → derefs to `Club.partner_producer_id` → that Producer is the recipient; null-OC payload (DEC-040) records null recipient. Cancellation reversal: 14-day pre-shipment cancellation per DEC-108 reverses share proportionally to cancelled vouchers (per DEC-109 1-voucher-per-bottle).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-008 (OC + 5% Discovery share), DEC-032 (5% × P_d), DEC-040 (no-OC admitted), DEC-049, DEC-066 (OC FK), DEC-086 (PO timing analogue), DEC-101, DEC-107 (INV1 event), DEC-108 (cancellation), DEC-109 (per-voucher).
- **BMD revision**: none — emission timing aligns with BMD §8.14 "share accrues on the sale" framing; the post-payment-cleared refinement is implicit but worth flagging in §8.14 prose at next BMD touch (NOT urgent).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-113 — Sanctions-screening enforcement gate at pre-PaymentAuthorization (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-21) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-21. DEC-071 mandates sanctions check at order completion in Module S; the trigger point in checkout flow (between OrderPlaced / PaymentAuthorization / OrderCompleted) was unconfirmed.
- **Decision**: Sanctions check fires **between OrderPlaced and PaymentAuthorization** (pre-payment). Module S reads `Customer.sanctions_status` (per Module K v0.2 §9.3); non-`passed` blocks order + emits `OrderBlockedBySanctionsGate` event with reason payload; **no card authorization fires for blocked Order**.

- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-071 (sanctions enforcement at order completion), Module K v0.2 §9.3.

- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-114 — Hero Package three-gate eligibility check at order completion (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-23) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-23. Hero Package purchase eligibility combines Profile state + single-per-year + Capacity Invariant; the three-gate check needed locking.
- **Decision**: Module S validates Hero Package purchase eligibility at order completion via **three gates**: (1) **Profile state precondition** — Customer has Approved Profile for the Hero Package's Club (Lapsed / Suspended / Cancelled blocks; renewal flow re-uses existing Lapsed Profile per BMD §2.4); (2) **single-per-club-year** — re-purchase blocked until next club year or prior-Hero-Package CONSUMED + year transition; (3) **Capacity Invariant lookup** — Active Profiles ≤ Allocation.qty per Module K v0.2 §13. Failure → `HeroPackagePurchaseRejected` event with reason. Non-Hero club Offers only check Profile state + Allocation capacity (not single-per-year).
- **Implications**: Cross-link DEC-007 (Hero Package = Membership), DEC-069 (mid-year capacity mutability), DEC-079 (qty mutability), DEC-096 (boolean flag on Offer), Module K v0.2 §13. Hero Package + Club Credit can coexist on different lines of same Order (Hero Package = membership fee, not Club-Credit-eligible line per DEC-043 + DEC-110 stacking matrix).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-007, DEC-069, DEC-079, DEC-096.
- **BMD revision**: none — gate aligns with BMD §2.3 + §9.1 framing.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-115 — Producer Portal ↔ Admin Panel parity extends to Module S Offer-level operations; Discovery NewCo-only carve-out (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-24) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-24. DEC-083 locked Producer Portal ↔ Admin Panel parity for Module A allocation operations + flagged extension to Module S Offer-level operations as Wave 3 elicitation item.
- **Decision**: DEC-083 parity extends to Module S Offer-level operations: Offer create / submit / publish / pause / close / promotional-pricing / Hero-Package-designate (per DEC-096) / Layer-3-set / granularity / time-window are all parity-shared for **club Offers** (Producer Portal + NewCo Admin Panel both surface). **Discovery Offers are NewCo-Admin-Panel-only at launch** (NewCo-curatorial commercial discretion per DEC-039 NewCo-unilateral-on-Discovery; multi-producer composite binding per DEC-097 is curatorial; producers don't author Discovery Offers). Audit trail: every Offer-level event carries `actor_role: producer | newco_ops`.

## DEC-116 — Gifting voucher transferability mechanism; Originating Club preservation (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-25) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-25. v17 Module A §12 has gifting mechanic; BMD §4.13 requires giver's OC preservation on gifted vouchers; NewCo-specific recipient gates needed locking.
- **Decision**: Gifting voucher transferability inherits v17 Module A §12 with NewCo-specific gates:
  - **Inherits**: 7-day accept window; voucher locked to sender during PENDING_TRANSFER; no financial event (original INV1 stands; non-revenue transfer); Allocation lineage preserved.
  - **NewCo recipient gates**: registered NewCo Customer + KYC `passed` + Offer-eligibility match (e.g., club Offer voucher only giftable to Customer with Approved Profile in that Club; Discovery Offer voucher giftable to any Customer with KYC `passed`).
  - **OC preservation per BMD §4.13**: giver's `originating_club_id` preserved as the OC for the gifted voucher's eventual sell-through (giver's purchase moment locked the OC reference per DEC-066); event payload carries `giver_customer_id` + `recipient_customer_id` + giver's locked OC reference.
  - **Voucher state**: GIFTED state covers transfer-pending phase per DEC-102.
  - **Terminal vouchers** (REDEMPTION_REQUESTED / SHIPPED / CONSUMED / VOIDED / EXPIRED) NOT transferable.
- **Implications**: Cross-link DEC-066 (OC FK target = Club entity, one-shot lock), Module K v0.2 §6 (OC Mechanic).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-008, DEC-049, DEC-050, DEC-066, DEC-102. Cites BMD §4.13.
- **BMD revision**: none — mechanism aligns with BMD §4.13 framing.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-117 — Producer recall scope = unsold sub-pool only; ISSUED vouchers immutable post-INV1 (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-26 — refines DEC-090) (2026-05-04)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-26. Recommendation framed state-conditional auto-VOID with manual review for REDEMPTION_REQUESTED. Paolo: "Yes, but technically a voucher issued (with INV-1 and cash paid) should not be recalled by producer."
- **Decision**: Producer recall scope (per DEC-090) is **the unsold sub-pool only** (`Allocation.qty - issued`). **ISSUED vouchers are NOT subject to producer recall**: once INV1 has fired and the customer has paid, the voucher's underlying allocation portion is committed to the customer; the producer's recall request does not affect committed customer holdings. Module D's `ReverseInboundEventRecorded` (per qa.modD Q-AD-14 / DEC-090) records the reverse-inbound flow only for the unsold portion. Refined state-conditional matrix:
  - **PENDING_PAYMENT vouchers** (bank-transfer 7-day window per DEC-101): edge case — recall propagation typically slower than cart hold; ops review case-by-case if collision occurs; if recall lands before INV1 fires, voucher VOIDS (no INV1, no refund); if INV1 already fired (= ISSUED), voucher committed and NOT subject to recall.
  - **ISSUED / REDEMPTION_REQUESTED / SHIPPED / CONSUMED / GIFTED vouchers**: NOT void-target on producer recall.
  - **VOIDED / EXPIRED vouchers**: terminal; recall has no effect.
- **Implications**: **Producer recall (DEC-090) ≠ producer offboarding (BMD §3.13)**. Recall = unsold-stock-recall (limited scope). Offboarding = relationship lifecycle exit + commitment to honour all outstanding ISSUED vouchers (NewCo's commitment, regardless of producer status — substitute / honour from residual stock per DEC-104).
- **Amends / supersedes**: **refines DEC-090's voucher-void-on-recall scope** explicitly to unsold-only. Composes with DEC-101 (PENDING_PAYMENT bank-transfer window), DEC-102 (Voucher state machine), DEC-104 (substitution mechanic).
- **BMD revision**: required at Wave-3-end v0.7 consolidation. BMD §3.9 (Unsold Stock Handling — recall scope) + BMD §3.13 (Producer Offboarding — honour-outstanding-vouchers commitment) need explicit unsold-only-recall + ISSUED-voucher-immunity framing.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-119 — Storage-fee ownership flipped to Module S + storage-clock-start refined to bottle-at-warehouse trigger (Wave 3 Module S PRD review — supersedes DEC-118 ownership clause; refines accrual trigger) (2026-05-06)
- **Context**: Raised by Paolo during Wave 3 Module S PRD v0.1 review 2026-05-06. Two refinements to DEC-118: (a) the bidirectional Module S ↔ Module E INV2 mid-semester roll-in contract was the densest cross-module surface in the Module S PRD; flipping ownership eliminates it. Module S already owns all customer-facing transactional logic (Voucher state machine, INV1 / INV2 issuance, Voucher lifecycle); co-locating storage-fee computation removes the need for Module E to mirror Voucher state. (b) DEC-118's implicit framing assumed storage clock starts at purchase (INV1) — correct for V2 (NewCo default per DEC-092 where stock is pre-positioned at Vinlock at allocation activation), but **wrong for V1 + Direct Purchase in-transit-at-purchase per DEC-081** where the bottle is not yet physically at Vinlock at INV1 issuance. No storage = no charge; the clock must wait for the bottle to be at warehouse.
- **Decision**:
  - **Ownership flip — Module S owns storage-fee computation + INV3 issuance + per-bottle accrual events**:
    - Module S owns the **`StorageFeeAccrued` event emission** (per bottle per month after the 12-month-free window + bottle-at-warehouse condition).
    - Module S owns **INV3 issuance** (semi-annual aggregation per DEC-118 cadence — end of June + end of December).
    - Module S owns **storage-clock-start computation** per the refined trigger below.
    - Module S owns the **mid-semester INV2 storage roll-in** as Module-S-internal logic at INV2 issuance (no cross-module query — Module S has all the storage state natively because it owns the Voucher and the storage clock).
    - Module S owns the **storage-fee pro-rata refund computation** per DEC-046 + §12.6 (no cross-module query).
    - Module S owns **customer-account-history rendering** of all three customer-facing invoices (INV1 / INV2 / INV3) natively (no event-subscription pattern across modules).
  - **Module E retains** (per DEC-072 boundary):
    - Consume Module S's customer-facing invoice events (`InvoiceINV1Issued`, `InvoiceINV2Issued`, `InvoiceINV3Issued`) + route to Xero accounting integration.
    - Charge execution against saved payment method via Airwallex (per DEC-014) for INV3 — same downstream pattern as INV1 / INV2.
    - Supplier-side settlement events (sell-through, PO settlement, producer settlement statements per BMD §3.10) — unchanged, supplier-side ownership preserved.
    - Failed-charge handling per chargeback / Hold mechanics per DEC-047.
  - **Document-generation layer = Xero (clarified 2026-05-12 during Wave 5 Q-AD-18 review)**: "ownership flip" in this DEC means **commercial-state and event ownership** (storage-fee accrual, INV2 mid-semester roll-in, INV3 issuance trigger, Voucher lifecycle transitions, customer-account-history rendering) — NOT physical document generation. Xero remains the **Document Generator** per v17 §E.3 rule 14 inheritance + DEC-028: Xero composes the PDF / template / document numbering / legal-text / jurisdiction-specific compliance (SDI / MTD / Factur-X plugin compatibility). Module E remains the sole NewCo-side Xero integration point per DEC-014 + DEC-028: when Module S emits the issuance event, Module E routes it to Xero for both accounting AND document generation; Xero returns document URL/reference; Module E confirms back to Module S; Customer Portal surfaces the Xero-hosted document via that link. **Three-actor split**: Module S = the event (commercial-state moment); Xero = the artifact (PDF + numbering + legal text); Module E = the payment + the accounting record + Xero routing layer. Avoids building a multi-jurisdiction template engine at NewCo + preserves SDI plugin model intact (per DEC-171 Q-AD-15 deferral). Composes with DEC-072 + DEC-014 + DEC-028 + v17 §E.3 rule 14.
  - **Storage-clock-start refined trigger**:
    - **Storage accrual begins for month M if and only if BOTH**:
      - Month M > 12 months after INV1 issuance (the **first-12-months-free-from-purchase** protection per DEC-118).
      - Bottle was at Vinlock for any part of month M (the **bottle-must-be-in-warehouse** condition per Paolo's refinement).
    - **Operational expression**: `storage_accrual_start_date = max(INV1_date + 12 months, InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted_date_for_the_bound_allocation)`.
    - **Sourcing-model implications**:
      - **V2 (passive consignment, pre-positioned — NewCo default per DEC-092)**: bottle is at Vinlock at INV1 (stock pre-positioned at allocation activation per Module D PRD §3 + §8 ConsignmentReceipt). `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` fired at allocation activation, well before INV1. Effective trigger collapses to `INV1 + 12 months`. Accrual begins month 13 from INV1. Same operational behaviour as DEC-118's original framing.
      - **V1 (passive consignment, customer-order-driven)**: stock at producer until customer order. Bottle ships to Vinlock at customer-order-time per BMD §5.1. `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` fires at customer-order + N months (typically fast — V1 customer-order-driven flow ships immediately). If bottle arrives within 12 months of INV1 (typical fast-ship): accrual begins month 13 from INV1. If bottle arrives after 12 months (rare slow-ship): accrual begins from physical arrival, with partial-month rounding per DEC-118.
      - **Direct Purchase, already-at-Vinlock-at-INV1**: bottle inbound completed before customer purchase (inventory pre-positioned strategic stock-up scenario). Same as V2: accrual begins month 13 from INV1.
      - **Direct Purchase, in-transit-at-INV1 (per DEC-081 in-transit voucher case)**: bottle ships to Vinlock per Module D / Module C in-transit display. Accrual begins at the later of (month 13 from INV1) and (physical arrival date). Module S surfaces "in transit; ETA X" on the Voucher per Module C / Module S surface (per Module A PRD §11.6 cross-link); customer cannot redeem until physical receipt anyway (Module C shipment gates on `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted`).
    - **Cross-module read**: Module S subscribes to Module D's `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` events for the bound Allocation; the event date is recorded on the Voucher's storage-clock state. Late-binding (BMD §5.5) selects the specific physical bottle at shipment, but storage-fee accrual operates on the bound Allocation's stock-arrival event, not on the specific-bottle binding (which only happens at shipment time, after most or all of the storage period has elapsed).
  - **Mid-semester INV2 roll-in mechanics preserved** (per DEC-118): when a Voucher transitions REDEMPTION_REQUESTED → SHIPPED mid-semester, Module S includes any unbilled storage months on the shipped bottle as additional INV2 line items rather than carrying forward to the next INV3 cycle. After the bottle ships, no further storage accrues against the Voucher.
  - **All other DEC-118 mechanics preserved**: rate (€3/bottle/year = €0.25/bottle/month); partial-month rounding rule (any partial month counts as a full month); semi-annual INV3 cadence (end of June + end of December covering prior 6-month period); first-12-months-free-from-purchase customer protection; saved-payment-method charging via Airwallex; INV3 as the third customer-facing invoice type beyond INV1 / INV2.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module S PRD revision** (in-place edit per DEC-119 — v0.1 not yet signed off): §11.2 Voucher `storage_clock_start` attribute refined; §10.7 INV2 mid-semester roll-in becomes Module-S-internal (no cross-module query); §12.6 storage-fee pro-rata refund becomes Module-S-internal; §14 retitled and rewritten — storage-fee coordination Module S ↔ Module D (inbound event consumption) replaces the prior bidirectional Module S ↔ Module E contract; §16.9 customer-facing invoice events extended with `InvoiceINV3Issued` (Module S emits, NOT consumed from Module E); §16.10 storage-fee events flipped (Module S emits `StorageFeeAccrued` and `InvoiceINV3Issued`; Module E consumes); §17.7 Module E coordination simplified to "consume customer-facing invoice events + route to Xero + execute Airwallex charge"; §18.9 BR-S-Invoice-* extended to INV3; §19 Module S Boundary updated (INV3 issuance no longer "out"); §21 v17 inheritance trace + Cross-references + App A divergence summary refreshed.
  - **BMD revision queued for v0.8 consolidation** (post Wave 3 PRD signoff, alongside any Wave 4 elicitation outcomes): BMD §2.7 / §5.6 / §8.4 / §8.13 + Glossary (Storage Fee, INV3, Storage Service, Two/Three-Invoice Mechanic) refresh to attribute INV3 issuance + storage-fee computation to Module S; Module E retained as consumer + Xero router + payment-execution layer. The DEC-118 BMD revisions already landed at v0.7 stay in place; v0.8 surgical edits flip the module-ownership prose only (mechanics preserved).
  - **Module E PRD impact (Wave 5)**: Module E's role on customer-facing invoices becomes uniformly "consume Module S `Invoice*Issued` events + route to Xero + execute Airwallex charge for the saved payment method." Storage-fee aggregation + first-12-months-free + partial-month-rounding + bottle-at-warehouse condition all live in Module S. Module E's supplier-side settlement events (per BMD §3.10) are unchanged. Cleaner Module E scope.
  - **Module D cross-link**: Module S consumes Module D's `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` events (per Module D PRD §7 + §16) for the storage-clock-start trigger. This is a new Module D → Module S read that was implicit-but-not-documented at DEC-118 (when Module E owned storage); under DEC-119 it becomes explicit on the Module S side (cross-module read documented at Module S §17.4 + §14). Module D side has no change.
- **Amends / supersedes**: **supersedes DEC-118's module-ownership clause** ("Module E owns storage-fee issuance"); refines DEC-118's storage-clock-start framing ("first 12 months from purchase = FREE; charges begin month 13") to add the bottle-at-warehouse condition. All other DEC-118 mechanics (rate, cadence, partial-month rounding, mid-semester INV2 roll-in, customer protection) preserved verbatim. Composes with DEC-046 (storage-fee pro-rata refund — now Module-S-internal); DEC-072 (Module E records financial events; Xero decides GL treatment — preserved + Module E role made cleaner); DEC-081 (Direct Purchase ACTIVE-on-payment — in-transit voucher case where storage clock waits for physical arrival); DEC-093 (V1/V2 procurement flow — V2 stock at Vinlock at activation; V1 stock at producer until customer order); DEC-107 (INV1 / INV2 issuance event names — INV3 added to the customer-facing invoice family).
- **BMD revision**: required at v0.8 consolidation (queued; surgical edits to §2.7 / §5.6 / §8.4 / §8.13 + Glossary; mechanics preserved, ownership prose flipped). DEC-118's v0.7 BMD edits stay in place; v0.8 refines.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-118 — Storage fees: Module E owned + INV3 invoice type + €3/bottle/year + 6-month cadence + 12-month free + mid-semester INV2 roll-in (Wave 3 Module S Q-AD-27) (2026-05-04 — module-ownership clause SUPERSEDED by DEC-119; mechanics preserved)
- **Context**: Wave 3 Module S elicitation Q-AD-27. Recommendation framed Module S issuing storage fees as sale-line. Paolo override: "No, here it's different. Storage fees are charged every 6 months (end of June, end of December) based on # months each bottle is stored (partial month = 1 month) at €3/bottle/year (€0.25 × month); Module E will emit a specific invoice INV3 for storage services. If the bottle is shipped during the semester, storage fee until that date (month) will be charged on the INV2 (shipping) as an additional line item. First 12 months from purchase, storage is free."
- **Decision**: Storage fees mechanics at NewCo launch:
  - **Module E owns storage-fee issuance** (NOT Module S).
  - **NEW invoice type — INV3** (third customer-facing invoice type beyond INV1 / INV2) for storage services. Net-new vs current BMD §8.13 INV1 / INV2 framing.
  - **Cadence**: semi-annual — issuance dates **end of June + end of December**; covers prior 6-month period.
  - **Rate**: **€3 per bottle per year = €0.25 per bottle per month**.
  - **Partial-month rule**: any partial month counts as a full month (rounded up).
  - **First 12 months from purchase = FREE**: no storage charge for bottles in their first 12 months from purchase; charges begin month 13.
  - **Mid-semester shipment carve-out**: if a bottle ships during a semester, storage charge for months stored in that semester rolls into the bottle's **INV2** (shipping invoice) as additional line item — NOT issued separately as INV3. Bottles shipped after first-12-months but within a semester have storage portion appear on INV2.
  - **Customer payment method**: saved payment method per BMD §4.7; INV3 charges saved card; failures handled per chargeback / Hold mechanics per DEC-047.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module S role**: Module S consumes Module E's `InvoiceINV3Issued` event for customer-account-history rendering (does NOT issue INV3 directly); Module S coordinates with Module E on INV2 line-item composition for mid-semester-shipped bottles (Module S's INV2 issuance queries Module E for any unbilled storage months for the shipped bottle).
  - **Module E PRD impact (Wave 5)**: Module E owns INV3 issuance, per-bottle storage-month accrual mechanic (`StorageFeeAccrued` per BMD §8.4 fires per bottle per month after month 12), semi-annual aggregation into INV3, mid-semester roll-into-INV2 carve-out, rate-configuration + first-12-months-free rule.
  - **DEC-046 update**: storage-fee-refund-pro-rata (DEC-046) applies to mid-semester refund/cancellation cases; pro-rata mechanism reads INV3/INV2 cycles + first-12-months-free rule.
  - **Q-OQ-13 cross-link**: storage IS the sole "service" active at NewCo launch (per Q-OQ-13 answer); other services / experiences deferred per BMD §4.14. INV3 is therefore the only non-INV1 / non-INV2 customer-facing invoice at launch.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-014 (Airwallex), DEC-046 (storage-fee pro-rata refund), DEC-047 (chargeback), DEC-072 (BMD/PRD don't take accounting positions). Refines BMD §2.7 / §5.6 / §8.4 / §8.13 framing.
- **BMD revision**: required at Wave-3-end v0.7 consolidation (substantial). Sites: BMD §2.7 (storage overview — €3/bottle/year + €0.25/month + partial-month-rounding + first-12-months-free); BMD §5.6 (storage fees prose — align with cadence + mechanics); BMD §8.4 (introduce INV3 invoice type + semi-annual cadence + mid-semester INV2-line-item carve-out); BMD §8.13 (extend INV1/INV2 sequence with INV3 — distinct timing); BMD Appendix A Glossary (INV3 entry + refresh "Storage Fee" entry); BMD §12.1 decisions table (DEC-118 row).
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-120 — Recovery-scenario predecessor / successor chain shape — verbatim v17 §9 inheritance (Wave 4 Module B Q-CL-13) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-CL-13. Strategic fork: verbatim v17 §9 chain (symmetric link, chain depth unbounded) vs simplified flat-predecessor-only reference. Anchored in BMD §6.11.1 + §6.11.3 ("preserve the chain of provenance for any future audit").
- **Decision**: NewCo inherits v17 §9 chain shape verbatim at the business-concept layer — symmetric `predecessor_nft_id` recorded on the successor + `successor_nft_id` recorded on the predecessor's terminal event; chain depth unbounded; predecessor + successor events emitted per recovery action. Same NFC tag may carry multiple sequential NFTs over time without special-casing. Working-hypothesis disposition: blockchain-expert review pending — Wave 4 NFT-touching DECs (DEC-120 / DEC-121 / DEC-122 / DEC-124) carry "validation-pending" caveat; Paolo's blockchain colleague engagement queued post-Wave-4.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD** (Wave 4): cites v17 §9 by section number for chain-of-provenance machinery; recovery scenarios (§6.11.1 / §6.11.3) emit predecessor / successor signals on `NFTReissued` / burn events; chain depth unbounded; tech-team picks storage representation (on-chain registry contract vs off-chain attestation per BMD §6.11.1) downstream per DEC-073.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: Bottle Page (per DEC-126) renders the full chain without forward-traversal queries; zero impact on Module A / Module S / Module C entities.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-022 + DEC-055 (4 confirmed recovery defaults) + DEC-051 (post-shipment re-tagging removed) + DEC-060 (v17 inheritance) + DEC-073 (business-concept layer).
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §6.11.1 + §6.11.3 prose already aligns with verbatim inheritance.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-121 — NFT mint timing — single mint per bottle (1:1 with NFCTagApplied) (Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-2) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-2. Operationalises DEC-054 mint-timing principle. Single-vs-batch mint dimension picked.
- **Decision**: Each `NFCTagApplied` event emits exactly one corresponding `NFTMinted` event (1:1 cardinality at the business-event layer). Strict 1:1 NFC-to-NFT linkage preserved at the event-emission layer; batched mints rejected at PRD level to avoid the "tagged-but-not-yet-on-chain" gap window that complicates audit + recovery scenarios.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD** (Wave 4): 1:1 cardinality contract locked; tech-team picks on-chain transaction shape downstream (single transaction per mint vs aggregated multi-mint transaction within a single block — both qualify as "single mint per bottle" at the event-emission layer per DEC-073).
  - **Latency tolerance** between `NFCTagApplied` + `NFTMinted`: PRD-level business-rule SLA; actual SLA value operational + downstream per DEC-054.
  - **Working-hypothesis caveat**: blockchain-expert review may revisit batch-mint pattern as alternative.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-054 (mint-timing principle) + DEC-014 (Avalanche platform) + DEC-073 (operational details downstream).
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

Tech team picks on-chain encoding (raw on-chain field list vs content-addressed hash + URL pointer to off-chain metadata for gas-cost reasons) downstream — both qualify as "non-PII provenance + NFC-UID linkage" at the business layer.

Logilize WMS executes the physical workflow (Vinlock employee applies the tag; Logilize records application; Logilize emits a downstream event Module B consumes to fire `NFCTagApplied`). ## DEC-125 — Module B consumes Module D `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` + reads Module A sub-pool partition (Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-7) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-7. Cross-module consumption contract: Module B's serialization workflow runs against the serialized portion of Module A's sub-pool partition only.
- **Decision**: Module B consumes Module D `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` (per Module D PRD §7); for each accepted unit, Module B reads the source Allocation's sub-pool partition (Module A PRD §7) — only the `qty_to_serialize` portion enters Module B's NFC + NFT serialization pipeline; the `qty_non_serialized` portion skips the pipeline entirely (no SerializedBottle record, no NFC tag, no NFT, no Bottle Page, no recovery chain). Module B is read-only on Module A state (does NOT mutate sub-pool numerics; respects Module A's anti-orphan rule for post-issuance not-yet-issued-only mutations).
- **Implications**:

Pre-burn vs post-burn variants per BMD §6.8.

## DEC-127 — Six-locale launch on Bottle Page — locale fallback chain + per-attribute fallback discipline (Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-9) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-9. Operationalises DEC-031 (six launch locales) + DEC-064 (i18n-keyed JSON shape) at the Bottle Page surface.
- **Decision**: At launch the Bottle Page locale-resolution mechanic is: (1) auto-detect on first scan from `Accept-Language` HTTP header; (2) fallback chain: visitor preference (sticky cookie if present) → browser `Accept-Language` → English (final fallback); (3) manual locale switcher on every Bottle Page render; (4) **per-attribute fallback** within a single locale-resolution: if a translatable string is missing in the resolved locale, fall back to English for that string only (not for the entire page); (5) producer-supplied content reads from i18n-keyed JSON columns per DEC-064 — Module B reads resolved-locale strings; Module 0 PIM owns the translatable-string entities themselves.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD** (Wave 4): locale-fallback chain locked at business-spec layer; tech team picks switcher UI + cookie format downstream per DEC-073.
  - **Cookie-consent banner gate**: per DEC-027 — locale-cookie management complies with consent-banner gate.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-031 + DEC-064 + DEC-027 + DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-128 — Bottle Page provenance-trail anonymisation — location waypoints with dates, no PII (Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-10 — Paolo refinement) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-10. **Paolo refinement** of analyst's "shipped to Customer on YYYY-MM-DD" anonymisation framing: the Bottle Page renders a **chronological provenance trail** with location waypoints + dates (e.g., "in producer cellar from 1996 → in NewCo warehouse from dd/mm/yyyy → delivered to private cellar dd/mm/yyyy") — no personal info; data about the bottle is available, but the customer-as-actor is replaced by customer-as-anonymous-destination. Actual Bottle Page UX deferred per Paolo.
- **Decision**: Module B's Bottle Page data feed contains zero customer identifiers (no Customer.id, no Profile.id, no Voucher.id, no shipment-recipient-name, no shipment-address). The post-shipment label is **"delivered to private cellar on dd/mm/yyyy"** (not "shipped to Customer on…"). The provenance trail is composed from upstream module events: producer-cellar period (vintage / bottling date from Module 0 + Module D context); NewCo-warehouse period (Module D `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` + Module C `ShipmentDispatched`); private-cellar handover date (Module C delivery context — date only, no recipient). Predecessor / successor chain (per DEC-120) records on-chain provenance only — NFT IDs, NFC UIDs, allocation references; no Customer references in the chain.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD** (Wave 4): provenance-trail framing locked; data-source-by-module contract documented (Module 0 / Module D / Module C as upstream sources for waypoint + date data).
  - **Cross-module cascades**: reads Module D `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` + Module C `ShipmentDispatched` (date metadata only, no recipient PII).
  - Bottle Page UX layout deferred per Paolo (downstream tech per DEC-073).
- **Amends / supersedes**: refines DEC-024 (anonymisation) + DEC-029 (non-PII on-chain) at the Bottle Page rendering surface; composes with DEC-126 (Module B as Bottle Page system of record) + DEC-053 (core only at launch).
- **BMD revision**: optional at v0.8 — BMD §6.8 anonymisation prose could refresh "shipped to Customer on YYYY-MM-DD in anonymized form" to "delivered to private cellar on dd/mm/yyyy" framing. Surgical edit.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-129 — §6.11.1 Damaged tag in warehouse — Module B 5-event chain (Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-11) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-11. BMD §6.11.1 names the recovery flow + four event names; PRD lock of event chain composition + cross-module signals required.
- **Decision**: Five-event chain at Module B for §6.11.1 damaged-tag-in-warehouse: (1) `NFCTagDamagedInCustody` (Vinlock detection via Logilize); (2) NewCo ops authorisation audit-trail event (actor / timestamp / Bottle ref); (3) `NFCTagReapplied` (new-tag application — parallel to standard `NFCTagApplied` but with damaged-predecessor reference); (4) `NFTReissued` (new-NFT mint with `predecessor_nft_id` per DEC-120 chain shape); (5) `NFTBurnedAsTagDamaged` (old-NFT burn with `reason = tag_damaged_in_custody` + `successor_nft_id`). Bottle Lifecycle stays `SERIALIZED → AVAILABLE` — no lifecycle-state regression; bottle stays salable. Customer-facing impact none.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD** (Wave 4): event chain locked at business-event layer; payload schema downstream per DEC-073.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: cost absorption = NewCo per DEC-025; financial event flows through Module E for accounting integration per DEC-072.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-022 + DEC-055 + DEC-025 + DEC-072 + DEC-120.

## DEC-130 — §6.11.2 Damaged tag post-shipment — Module B event-recording role + no re-tagging (Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-12) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-12. BMD §6.11.2 + DEC-051 removed the post-shipment re-tagging exception path; PRD lock of Module B event chain + Customer Care boundary required.
- **Decision**: Module B event chain at §6.11.2 (event-recording role only): (1) `BottlePostShipmentTagIssueReported` fires when Customer reports the issue (Customer Care Operator records via NewCo Admin Panel); (2) `ProvenanceCertificateIssued` fires when NewCo issues the non-NFT signed certificate (digital + optional physical) attesting pre-burn provenance — Module B owns certificate generation + signing. **No re-tagging event** at Module B per DEC-051; the §5.10 no-returns-post-shipment rule + §6.7 burn-finality rule both stand. The NFT is already burned; re-mint post-burn is rejected per BMD §6.11.2 to avoid "ghost token". `CustomerServiceRemedyApplied` is **Customer Care scope, not Module B** — recorded in Module S (Voucher state if applicable) or Module E (financial event for store credit / coupon).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD** (Wave 4): event-recording role + no-re-tagging discipline locked; certificate format + signing workflow downstream per DEC-073.

## DEC-131 — §6.11.3 NFT lost in NewCo wallet — Module B event chain + dangling-token discipline (Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-13) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-13. BMD §6.11.3 names a recovery flow structurally different from §6.11.1 — NFC tag fine, NFT itself lost (wallet incident). PRD lock of event chain required.
- **Decision**: Two-event chain at Module B: (1) `NFTLossInWalletDetected` fires when NewCo confirms the NFT is unrecoverable (operator-initiated after wallet diagnostics); (2) `NFTReissuedDueToWalletLoss` fires on new-NFT mint with `predecessor_nft_id` (per DEC-120) + `predecessor_status = lost_in_wallet`. The lost NFT is **NOT burned** per BMD §6.11.3 (NewCo cannot reach to burn) — recorded as stale via registry / on-chain attestation marking the lost NFT as superseded; future scanners see "this NFT is stale; live NFT for this NFC tag is X". The NFC tag is unchanged (no `NFCTagReapplied` event). Bottle Lifecycle unaffected (recovery is on-chain only).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD** (Wave 4): event chain + dangling-token discipline locked; on-chain stale-attestation mechanism (registry contract entry vs off-chain attestation) downstream per DEC-073.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: cost absorption = NewCo per DEC-055.
  - **Working-hypothesis caveat**: blockchain-expert review pending — operational mechanism for stale-attestation is part of validation set.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-055 + DEC-120 + DEC-025 + DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
