## DEC-132 — §6.11.4 Bottle destroyed pre-shipment — Module B event chain + cross-module Module A + Module S coordination (Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-14) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-14. BMD §6.11.4 names a flow crossing three modules: Module B (NFT burn + write-off) + Module A (Allocation pool debit) + Module S (Voucher substitution if already-bound, per DEC-104). PRD lock of cross-module chain required.
- **Decision**: Module B event chain: (1) `BottleDestroyedInCustody` (operator-initiated via NewCo Admin Panel + Logilize write-off integration per BMD §5.9); (2) `BottleNFTBurnedAsDestroyed` (NFT burn with `reason = bottle_destroyed_in_custody` + cross-reference to write-off record). Module A consumes for `AllocationPoolDebitedDueToLoss` (Module A side; Module B records destruction; Module A debits pool). Module S consumes if there's a bound Voucher already (rare per BMD §5.5 late binding) — Module S fires `VoucherSubstitutionExecuted` per DEC-104 (manual operator capability) OR refund per BMD §4.11 if no alternative. Bottle Lifecycle terminates `WRITTEN_OFF`. Producer notification per BMD §3.10 settlement statement at next cadence.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD** (Wave 4): event chain at Module B + recording-role-on-cross-module-coordination discipline locked; payload schema downstream per DEC-073.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: Module A debits pool; Module S substitutes per DEC-104 or refunds; cost absorption = NewCo per DEC-025; financial event flows Module E per DEC-072.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-104 (substitution manual + passive-consignment-rare) + DEC-025 + DEC-072 + DEC-055.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-133 — Module B no-op on non-serialized stock — module-boundary discipline (Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-16) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module B Q-AD-16. Non-serialized stock has no Bottle Page, no NFT, no NFC scan target per BMD §6.2 + DEC-080. Module B's no-op posture needs PRD lock.
- **Decision**: Module B is no-op on non-serialized stock at launch: (1) no SerializedBottle record is created; (2) no NFC tag is applied (Logilize knows from Module A sub-pool partition not to apply NFC for non-serialized units per DEC-125); (3) no NFT is minted; (4) no Bottle Page is generated; (5) no recovery chain exists. Module B's interaction with non-serialized stock is the **absence** of state. The "non-serialized" badge on the Module S Offer (per DEC-052 + DEC-080) is Module S's concern.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD** (Wave 4): five no-op clauses locked; tech-team ensures Module B's APIs / queries return empty / not-applicable for non-serialized BR-allocation tuples per DEC-073.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-080 + DEC-052 + DEC-125; Cellar render data composition per DEC-154 reads Module B as no-NFT-reference for non-serialized.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-080 (per-allocation non-serialization opt-out) + DEC-052 + DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-47)**: Non-serialized informational events. Module B emits `BottleShippedAsNonSerialized` informational event for non-serialized bottles, mirroring the serialized chain for audit consistency; payload mirrors the serialized event with `null` NFT-related fields. The event is **informational-only** (no state change; no SerializedBottle record per the no-op clauses above). The `originating_club_id` field is preserved in the event payload through gifting → burn (no-op for non-serialized) → settlement chain per DEC-066 OC immutability — non-serialized OC accrual + reversal mechanics (per DEC-182) compose normally on the informational-event chain. Anchored at Module B §6 + Module S §11.5; closes E6-47 (informational-event dimension; OC-preservation dimension lands at DEC-066 Stage 6.5 clarification).
- **Superseded by**: DEC-186 (Stage 8 / 2026-05-09) — Stage 8 reframes Module B no-op posture as digital-provenance-only; non-serialized inventory has full ERP-side ledger discipline (4 counters on InboundBatch per v17 §B.5a).

## DEC-137 — Late-binding selection algorithm — FIFO at warehouse level + warehouse-efficiency-driven physical bottle pick (Wave 4 Module C Q-CL-14) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module C Q-CL-14. Strategic fork: FEFO / FIFO / producer-discretionary algorithm at Module C late-binding moment. **Paolo confirms B with refined two-surface framing**: (i) voucher-side selection = FIFO by Voucher expiry (irrelevant to Customer who doesn't request a specific Voucher); (ii) bottle-side selection = Logilize warehouse-efficiency rules (most efficient physical pick wins) within allocation-pool constraint. Producer-override (Interpretation C in original Q-CL — producer can specify per-allocation algorithm) **deferred to Phase 2+**; Paolo asks for explanation before any Phase 2+ commitment (open question — addressed in Wave 4 closure brief).
- **Decision**: At late binding (BMD §5.5 — specific physical bottle assigned at pick time), Module C drives selection on two surfaces: (1) **voucher-side** = FIFO by Voucher expiry — among vouchers in the same allocation pool referencing identical bottles, the longest-held / earliest-expiry voucher gets the bottle; (2) **bottle-side** = Logilize warehouse-efficiency rules — among physical bottles in the same allocation pool, the most efficient pick (storage-location proximity, pick-routing optimisation, etc. — Logilize-driven) wins. Allocation-pool boundary is invariant (cannot pick across pools). Producer-override remains deferred Phase 2+.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C PRD** (Wave 4): two-surface selection algorithm locked; voucher-side FIFO is Module-C-internal; bottle-side warehouse-efficiency reads from Logilize per DEC-140 integration scope.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-099 (`qty - issued` shared-pool state) + DEC-076 (allocation visibility) + Module A allocation-pool constraint.
  - **Open follow-up**: Paolo to revisit producer-override before any Phase 2+ commitment — analyst will queue a brief explainer (Interpretation C concept: producer can specify a per-allocation selection rule — e.g., FEFO or specific-vintage-only — instead of system FIFO; relevant for producers who want their allocations rotated by drinking-window vs arrival-date).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-060 (v17 §C.5 inheritance for FIFO baseline) + DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: optional at v0.8 — BMD §5.5 prose could refresh to make the two-surface framing explicit ("voucher-side FIFO + bottle-side Logilize warehouse-efficiency"). Surgical edit.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-35 + E6-46)**: Voucher-side late-binding tiebreak when two Vouchers in the same Allocation have **identical expiry dates** — secondary criterion is **earliest-issuance-timestamp** (deterministic; the Voucher created first wins). Tertiary fallback for the rare residual case where issuance-timestamps also tie (bulk batch-issued Vouchers in a single millisecond): operator-manual-review via Admin Panel, captured by a new `ShippingOrderManualReviewRequired` event at Module C §15 (NewCo addition). Bottle-side Logilize warehouse-efficiency selection is unchanged. The two surfaces remain independent; voucher-side determinism preserves customer predictability and audit clarity. Anchored at Module C §3.3 footnote + §15; closes E6-35 + E6-46.

## DEC-138 — Returns + replacement workflow at Module C — module-owned end-to-end, no cash refunds (Wave 4 Module C Q-CL-15) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module C Q-CL-15. DEC-108 + Module S §12.3 + v17 line 3768 lock the principle (replacement workflow without new Voucher / new INV2; cost recorded as non-revenue event by Module E). PRD lock of event chain composition + module-boundary required.
- **Decision**: Module C-owned event chain end-to-end for post-shipment damage / loss / fault handling: (1) `PostShipmentIssueReported` (Customer reports via Customer Care); (2) `ReturnReceiptRecorded` (rare — usually unit unrecoverable); (3) `ReplacementShipmentIssued` (NewCo dispatches replacement, drawing from same Allocation pool if available, or substitution per DEC-104 if not); (4) `ReplacementShipmentDelivered`. Original Voucher's commercial state preserved — no new Voucher / new INV2 per DEC-108 + v17 line 3768. Module S consumes only `ReplacementShipmentIssued` for Customer notification. Module C does **NOT** issue cash refunds (replacements only); cash refunds are Module S supervisor-override surface per DEC-108 + Module S §12.3. Module E consumes the non-revenue cost event for accounting per DEC-072.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C PRD** (Wave 4): end-to-end event chain + replacements-only discipline locked.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: Module S retains Voucher-state authority (no state regression — DEC-102 8-state lock preserved); supervisor-override audit event lives in Module S per DEC-108 + Module S §12.3 (DEC-108 is the audit-event surface, restated here for the Module C boundary).
  - **Structural incompatibility note**: Interpretation B (Module-S-authoritative-on-Voucher-state) was rejected as structurally incompatible with DEC-102 8-state lock — the original Voucher state is preserved through replacement, not extended.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-108 + DEC-104 (substitution mechanic) + DEC-102 (Voucher 8-state lock) + DEC-072 (Module E accounting).
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §4.10 / §4.11 / §5.10 already aligned with the decision via DEC-108 v0.7 prose.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

At launch the SO state machine collapses to **5 states**: `draft → planned → picking → shipped → completed` + `cancelled` (terminal pre-shipped) + `returned` (resolution path post-shipment per DEC-108 + DEC-138) + `lost` (transit-loss resolution path). Sub-state flags: `compliance_hold` on `draft` (sanctions / age verification / destination-eligibility — Module K reads per Module K §9.3 + DEC-113); `manual_review` on `picking` (WMS pick-discrepancy resolution). Customer-initiated trigger only at NewCo (per BMD §9.2 — Customer requests delivery from cellar view; no system-initiated auto-SO at launch).

## DEC-140 — Logilize WMS integration scope at launch — 5-stream contract (Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-2) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-2. BMD §5.3 names integration scope; PRD lock of operational contract required.
- **Decision**: Module C ↔ Logilize integration scope at launch covers five streams: (1) **outbound shipment instruction** (pick request at SO `planned → picking` with SO id, BR-keyed line items + qty, allocation context, destination, late-binding strategy per DEC-137); (2) **pick confirmation** (Logilize emits pick-confirmation event Module C consumes — for serialized stock, the specific bottle's serial + NFT identity binds the Voucher per BMD §5.5 late binding; for non-serialized, dispatch records allocation + InboundBatch + qty); (3) **dispatch confirmation** (Logilize emits dispatch event when carrier receives shipment; Module C transitions SO `picking → shipped` and emits `ShipmentDispatched`); (4) **delivery confirmation** (best-effort tracking from carrier through Logilize feeds Module C's SO `shipped → completed`); (5) **storage-location tracking** (Logilize maintains storage location per bottle / per non-serialized batch; Module C exposes summary for cellar render per DEC-153). Inbound (NFC application + InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted) + stock state remain Module B + Module D scope per BMD §5.3.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C PRD** (Wave 4): 5-stream integration contract locked at PRD layer; literal Logilize API contract / event payload schemas / retry / failure-mode handling downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with BMD §5.3 + DEC-014 (Logilize same provider, separate integration) + DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Superseded by**: DEC-188 (Stage 8 / 2026-05-09) — Stage 8 splits the 5-stream contract: Module C retains 4 fulfillment streams; Module B owns 5 inventory-state streams (Stream 5 storage-location migrates to Module B; receiving + stocktake + adjustments added).

## DEC-142 — Late-binding event flow — `BottlePicked` cross-module chain (Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-4) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-4. BMD §5.5 names late-binding events; cross-module event-flow composition needs PRD lock.
- **Decision**: Module C event flow at late binding — 7-step chain: (1) Module C consumes Module S `VoucherRedemptionRequested` (Module S §11.7) → SO `draft → planned`; (2) Module C reads Allocation context (Module A `qty - issued`; sub-pool partition for serialized vs non-serialized; counterparty per Module A §11.6); (3) Module C sends pick request to Logilize per DEC-140; (4) Logilize emits pick-confirmation event Module C consumes; (5) Module C fires `BottlePicked` recording the bound bottle's serial / NFT identity (for serialized) or the allocation + InboundBatch + qty (for non-serialized); (6) SO `planned → picking → shipped`; (7) Module C fires `ShipmentDispatched` consumed by Module S → Module S transitions Voucher REDEMPTION_REQUESTED → SHIPPED + emits `VoucherShipped` (consumed by Module B for NFT burn per DEC-134). The bound-bottle serial / NFT identity flows through `ShipmentDispatched` to `VoucherShipped` to Module B's burn.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C PRD** (Wave 4): cross-module event chain + late-binding moment locked.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-099 (`qty - issued` shared-pool) + Module A §11.6 (counterparty) + DEC-137 (selection algorithm) + Module S §11.7 + §17.5 + DEC-134.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with BMD §5.5 + Module S PRD §11.7 + §17.5 + DEC-134 + DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-143 — In-transit voucher display contract — Direct Purchase + redemption-block business rule (Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-5) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-5. DEC-081 (Direct Purchase ACTIVE-on-payment + sellability-vs-shipment-gate decoupling) requires Module C to surface in-transit state on Customer-side surfaces.
- **Decision**: Module C in-transit voucher UX contract: (1) Module C reads Module D `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` for the bound Allocation; (2) for Vouchers whose Allocation has not yet had `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` fire, Module C surfaces "in transit; ETA X" on the Cellar render + on any Customer-facing Voucher detail surface (Consumer Portal); (3) ETA X computed from Module D in-transit metadata (carrier ETA if available; otherwise admin-configurable estimate per Module D's PI / PO context); (4) Customer cannot redeem the in-transit Voucher (REDEMPTION_REQUESTED rejected at SO `draft → planned` transition — Module C's shipment gate per DEC-081 — until `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` fires for the relevant qty); (5) once `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` fires, in-transit display clears + Voucher becomes redeemable.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C PRD** (Wave 4): in-transit-display + redemption-block business rule locked; UX rendering downstream per DEC-073.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-081 (Direct Purchase ACTIVE-on-payment) + Module A §11.6 + Module D §14.6 + §12.3 + Module S §11.7.
- **Amends / supersedes**: operationalises DEC-081 at the Module C surface; composes with DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-144 — Three shipping modes at launch — direct + customer pickup + events + gift sub-flag (Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-7) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-7. BMD §5.7 names three modes; PRD lock of mode-specific business-rule variations required.
- **Decision**: Module C supports three shipping modes at launch with mode-specific SO sub-flags + workflow variants: (1) **Direct shipment** (default; SO `dispatch_mode = direct`; carrier integration per DEC-145; standard `picking → shipped → completed` with carrier ETA tracking); (2) **Customer pickup** (SO `dispatch_mode = pickup`; appointment coordinated by Customer Care; INV2 fires at moment of physical handover at Vinlock per BMD §5.7; SO transitions `picking → shipped (= handed over) → completed`); (3) **Events** (SO `dispatch_mode = event`; ships to event venue — producer event, club event, NewCo event — where Customer collects in person; SO `picking → shipped → completed` with event venue as destination address). Gift shipments per BMD §4.13 + DEC-116 are a sub-flag on direct shipment (`is_gift = true`; recipient address used at shipment per Module S §13).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C PRD** (Wave 4): three modes + sub-flag + mode-specific business-rule variations locked; mode-specific UX (appointment scheduling for pickup, event coordination workflow) downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with BMD §5.7 + BMD §4.13 + DEC-116 (gifting OC preservation) + DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-145 — Carrier selection + shipping-fee quote — automatic rule-driven + manual operator-entry both supported (Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-8 — Paolo refinement) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-8. **Paolo refinement**: operator must be able to **manually create a quote** (not only select via configurable rule). Quote can be manual OR automatic depending on integration with carrier and system rules.
- **Decision**: Module C is the system of record for shipping-fee quotes + carrier selection. Quote-generation system supports two paths: (1) **automatic** via operator-configurable rule set + carrier-API integration where available; (2) **manual** operator-entered quote (operator types fee + selected carrier + transit estimate). The same `ShippingFeeQuoted` event fires in either case; a `quote_origin` discriminator (`auto` / `manual`) records which path produced the quote for audit. Operator surface lives in NewCo Admin Panel + customer-care workflow. Module S checkout calls Module C's quote generator at cart-finalisation; Module S records quote on Order for INV1 inclusion per Module S §10.6 + DEC-107. Carrier selection at launch = operator-configurable rule set per BMD §5.7 — admin-managed; not a customer-facing preference.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C PRD** (Wave 4): two-path quote-generation locked; manual-entry surface available via NewCo Admin Panel + CS workflow (used in white-glove cases per DEC-147).
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-107 (INV1 / INV2 events) + DEC-147 (white-glove fallback for non-eligible destinations).
  - Literal Admin Panel UX + carrier-API contracts + rate-matrix data shape downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with BMD §5.7 + BMD §8.5 + DEC-107 + DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: optional at v0.8 — BMD §5.7 prose could explicitly name the manual-quote-entry capability alongside the automated quote. Surgical edit.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-146 — Cross-module shipping-fee event flow + INV2 line-item composition incl. storage roll-in (Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-9) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-9. **Paolo's reminder**: INV2 may include storage fee accrued up to dispatch as a separate line item (per DEC-118 mid-semester carve-out + DEC-119 Module-S-internal computation).
- **Decision**: Cross-module event flow for shipping fees: (1) **At Checkout**: Module S calls Module C's quote generator → Module C emits `ShippingFeeQuoted` (per DEC-145) → Module S records on Order (informational; INV1 does NOT include shipping per DEC-045 — INV1 is bottle / Voucher amount only); (2) **At Shipment**: Module C dispatches → Module C emits `ShipmentDispatched` (carrying actual shipping cost — may differ from quote if re-quote occurred per DEC-145) → Module S consumes + emits `InvoiceINV2Issued` per DEC-107. **INV2 line items at NewCo launch include**: bottle / Voucher amount (already on INV1, not re-billed), shipping fee actual, destination VAT + excise (per DEC-045), **storage fee accrued up to dispatch date as a separate line item** (per DEC-118 mid-semester carve-out + DEC-119 Module-S-internal computation). Module C does **NOT** issue invoices directly (INV2 is Module-S-owned per Module S §10.7 + §17.6). For shipping modes other than direct (pickup / events per DEC-144), the quote may be zero (pickup) or minimal; INV2 fires at shipment regardless.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C PRD** (Wave 4): cross-module event flow + INV2 line-item composition locked.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: Module S §10.7 / §14.4 owns INV2 issuance + storage-fee mid-semester roll-in (Module-S-internal per DEC-119); Module C emits triggers; Module E consumes for accounting per DEC-072.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-045 + DEC-107 + DEC-118 (storage-fee mechanics) + DEC-119 (Module S ownership) + DEC-072.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-147 — Destination eligibility two-tier — automated pre-cleared + white-glove customer-service fallback (Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-10 — Paolo refinement) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Wave 4 Module C Q-AD-10. **Paolo refinement**: for non-eligible destinations, Customer can still submit "send shipping request" → Customer Care reviews case-by-case; sometimes shippable with customised quote depending on product + destination specifics. White-glove fallback path preserved.
- **Decision**: Destination eligibility two-tier model at launch: (1) **automated path** for the pre-cleared destination subset (operator-configurable; BMD §5.8 + DEC-041 25-country baseline); destination address validated against eligible-destinations list at Checkout (Module S) + at SO creation (Module C); eligible destination → standard checkout / SO progression; (2) **white-glove fallback** for non-eligible / complex destinations: Customer-facing surface offers "send shipping request" CTA → creates Customer Care ticket; CS reviews + may approve case-by-case with manually-entered quote per DEC-145; if approved, SO proceeds normally; if denied, Customer chooses continued-storage or cancellation per DEC-108 14-day window. NewCo Admin Panel exposes eligible-destinations list + case-management surface.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C PRD** (Wave 4): two-tier model locked; ineligible destination does NOT terminate path (no hard block at launch); CS-ticket integration is Module C's responsibility at the SO-side; Module S checkout offers the same fallback at the cart side.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-041 (25-country baseline + OFAC) + DEC-145 (manual quote) + DEC-108 (14-day window) + DEC-115 / DEC-083 (admin parity).
  - Literal CS ticket-management UX + workflow tooling downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: refines BMD §5.8 ineligible-destination handling; composes with DEC-041 + DEC-115 + DEC-083 + DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: required at v0.8 — BMD §5.8 prose needs the white-glove customer-service fallback explicit (currently just states "ineligible destinations block shipment + offer continued storage as alternative"). Surgical edit.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-156 — `ProducerSettlementStatementIssued` event shape — one statement per Producer with five-section breakdown (Wave 5 Module E Q-CL-16) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-CL-16. BMD §3.10 names the principle (one settlement statement per producer per quarter; sales detail club + Discovery separately broken down; refunds; clawbacks; OC shares earned and paid) but does not pick the granularity of breakdown when a single Producer operates multiple Clubs (BMD §3.4 admits multi-brand / multi-Club producers at launch). PRD lock of statement-shape contract required to drive `ProducerSettlementStatementIssued` event payload + Producer-Portal dashboard per BMD §3.11.
- **Decision**: Settlement statement shape locked as **Option C** — one statement per Producer per settlement period (default quarterly per DEC-042; per-producer override via ProducerAgreement per DEC-070), with **five explicit sections** on the document:
  - **Section A** — per-Club sell-through detail (one section per Club this Producer operates; line items per allocation).
  - **Section B** — Discovery sell-through detail (one section per Discovery Allocation where this Producer is the bottle's Producer per DEC-082 + DEC-088).
  - **Section C** — refunds + clawbacks netted against the period (per DEC-164 within-period netting + cross-period clawback rules).
  - **Section D** — OC shares earned and paid: 5% × P_d shares accrued where this Producer's Club was the buyer's Originating Club (per DEC-066 + DEC-161). **Section D content discipline (per BMD §3.11 + DEC-162 info-disclosure constraint)**: aggregate-only Discovery data — share amount + anonymized transaction reference + running balance; NO per-purchase-buyer detail; NO bottle's-Producer identity disclosure (Producer X cannot see that buyer A purchased bottles from Producer Y).
  - **Section E** — Direct Purchase informational reconciliation rows (per DEC-163 — units sold + refunds against the batch; NO monetary settlement amount due, since Direct Purchase pays at PO per DEC-063 + DEC-086).
- Producer issues one invoice-back-to-NewCo per settlement period matching the statement total (net-30 per BMD §3.10).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): `ProducerSettlementStatementIssued` event carries one statement per Producer per period with five-section breakdown; aggregation pipeline reads upstream events (`SellThroughSettled`, `OCShareAccrued`, `RefundExecuted`, `SupplierPaymentCompleted` for Direct Purchase informational rows) per allocation lineage + counterparty resolution. Section D info-disclosure constraint enforced at event-payload composition.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: Producer Portal dashboard reads same upstream events per BMD §3.11 (real-time view; statement is the formal financial document); composes with DEC-042 + DEC-066 + DEC-070 + DEC-082 + DEC-088 + DEC-092 + DEC-117 + DEC-161 + DEC-162 + DEC-163 + DEC-164.
  - Literal section-rendering UX, line-item field list, document numbering, PDF layout, Xero-side document generation per v17 §E.3 rule 14 are downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-042 + DEC-066 + DEC-070 + DEC-082 + DEC-088 + DEC-092; refines BMD §3.10 + §3.11 + §8.14 at PRD-event-payload layer.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §3.10 already accommodates the principle; PRD-level section breakdown lock.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-157 — Customer-facing invoice typology at NewCo launch — INV1 + INV2 + INV3 only (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-1) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-1. v17 §E.4 carries seven customer-facing invoice types (INV0 + INV1 + INV-P + INV2 + INV3 + INV4 + INV1_INV2_COMBINED) plus two financial-event-only types (SELL_THROUGH_SETTLEMENT + EVENT_CONSUMPTION_SETTLEMENT). NewCo BMD §8.13 commits to three customer-facing types (INV1 + INV2 + INV3); divergence from v17 baseline must be locked at the Module E PRD layer per DEC-074 self-contained delivery doc.
- **Decision**: Customer-facing invoice typology at NewCo launch = **INV1 + INV2 + INV3 only**. Explicit drops / deferrals from v17 §E.4 baseline:
  - **INV1 — KEPT**: commerce, at checkout / post-payment-cleared per DEC-107 + DEC-112 + DEC-119 (Module-S-emitted; Module E consumes for Xero routing + Airwallex charge per DEC-158).
  - **INV2 — KEPT**: excise + destination-VAT + shipping at fulfillment per DEC-107 + DEC-119.
  - **INV3 — KEPT**: semi-annual storage fee per DEC-118 + DEC-119 (Module-S-emitted; Module E consumes for charge + Xero routing per DEC-160).
  - **INV0 — DROPPED**: Hero Package = membership purchase per DEC-007; fires INV1 like any other purchase per DEC-114; no separate membership-fee invoice type.
  - **INV-P — DROPPED**: B2C bank transfer uses PENDING_PAYMENT order state per DEC-101 + DEC-112 (no proforma document); INV1 issues at funds-cleared per DEC-159; B2B wholesale quotation N/A per DEC-017 + DEC-068.
  - **INV4 — DEFERRED**: paid services / experiences per BMD §4.14; folded into Q-OQ batch DEC-171.
  - **INV1_INV2_COMBINED — DROPPED**: no B2B at launch per DEC-017 + DEC-068.
  - **SELL_THROUGH_SETTLEMENT — DROPPED**: no active consignment at launch per DEC-011 + BMD §13.1.
  - **EVENT_CONSUMPTION_SETTLEMENT — DROPPED**: no active consignment + no INV4 per DEC-011 + DEC-171.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): typology-collapse documented as divergence surface from v17 §E.4 (per DEC-074); cites v17 §E.4 by section number for inherited invoice-lifecycle pattern (per DEC-060).
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-007 (Hero Package = INV1), DEC-011 (no active consignment), DEC-017 + DEC-068 (no B2B), DEC-101 (PENDING_PAYMENT IS bank-transfer credit-terms state), DEC-107 + DEC-112 + DEC-118 + DEC-119 (Module-S-emitted invoices), DEC-171 (Q-OQ batch — INV4 deferred).
  - Literal document numbering, PDF layout, legal-text composition downstream per DEC-073 + Xero scope per v17 §E.3 rule 14.
- **Amends / supersedes**: refines v17 §E.4 inheritance (per DEC-060 + DEC-074); composes with DEC-073.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §8.13 already commits to the three-type set.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-158 — Card payment flow — Module E owns Airwallex API; Module S orchestrates customer-facing transaction (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-3) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-3. v17 §E.6 has Module E owning payment-processor calls via the Provider-Agnostic Adapter Pattern (StripeAdapter Module-E-internal). NewCo replaces Stripe with Airwallex per DEC-014; API-call ownership pattern + cross-module orchestration with Module S customer-facing invoice issuance per DEC-119 must be locked.
- **Decision**: Module E owns the Airwallex API-call layer at NewCo (inheriting v17 §E.6 pattern with **AirwallexAdapter substituting for StripeAdapter**). Card-payment flow at checkout: (1) **Cart submit (Module S)** — Customer finalizes cart; Module S calls Module E payment-execution service with order context (Customer ref, total amount, currency, line items, payment_method = card). (2) **Airwallex authorize+capture (Module E)** — Module E creates Payment record (status `pending`); AirwallexAdapter calls Airwallex authorize-and-capture (one step per DEC-101); Airwallex webhook returns `charge.succeeded` or `charge.failed`; Module E updates Payment record. (3) **Confirmation back to Module S (Module E → Module S)** — Module E confirms payment-cleared status to Module S. (4) **INV1 issuance (Module S)** — Module S transitions Order PENDING_PAYMENT → CONFIRMED + emits `InvoiceINV1Issued` per DEC-107 + DEC-112; Voucher PENDING_PAYMENT → ISSUED per DEC-102. (5) **Xero routing (Module E)** — Module E consumes the just-emitted `InvoiceINV1Issued` event + routes to Xero per DEC-072. For **INV2** + **INV3**: Module S emits invoice event first → Module E consumes + executes Airwallex charge against saved card per BMD §4.7 → Module E routes to Xero. INV3 failed-charge handling per DEC-160.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): cross-module ownership boundary locked (Module E owns Airwallex calls; Module S orchestrates customer-facing transaction). AirwallexAdapter implementation detail downstream per DEC-073.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-014 (Airwallex), DEC-101 (authorize+capture one step for cards), DEC-102 (Voucher state machine), DEC-107 + DEC-112 (post-payment-cleared INV1 timing), DEC-119 (Module-S-owned customer-facing invoices), DEC-159 (bank-transfer flow companion), DEC-160 (INV3 failed-charge escalation).
  - Literal AirwallexAdapter API contract (3-D Secure / SCA / PSD2 flow per BMD §4.7, retry semantics, webhook signature validation, idempotency keys) downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-014 + DEC-101 + DEC-102 + DEC-107 + DEC-112 + DEC-119; refines v17 §E.6 inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-159 — Bank-transfer funds-cleared notification — webhook-driven via Module E; v17 §E.6 manual reconciliation as operator fallback (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-4) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-4. For bank-transfer customers, Airwallex confirms funds-cleared outside the standard authorize-and-capture flow per DEC-101 + BMD §4.7. Notification path must be locked across (a) webhook-driven, (b) polling, or (c) Ops manual entry per v17 §E.6 BankTransferAdapter.
- **Decision**: Webhook-driven via Module E as the primary path at NewCo launch, with v17 §E.6 manual-reconciliation surface preserved as operator fallback. Bank-transfer flow: (1) **Cart submit with payment_method = bank_transfer (Module S)** — Module S creates Order in PENDING_PAYMENT per DEC-101; Cart Hold extends to 7 calendar days per DEC-049; Module S surfaces transfer instructions to Customer (Airwallex-provided IBAN / SWIFT instructions per DEC-014); Voucher PENDING_PAYMENT pre-state per DEC-102. (2) **Customer initiates wire transfer externally** — SEPA same-region (1-2 days) or SWIFT cross-region (3-5 days) per BMD §4.7. (3) **Airwallex webhook on funds-cleared (Airwallex → Module E)** — Airwallex pushes `transfer.received` webhook; Module E validates + matches Order via transfer-reference identifier set at PENDING_PAYMENT creation. (4) **Module E notifies Module S (Module E → Module S)** — Module E emits `BankTransferFundsCleared` (Order ref + amount + currency); Module S transitions Order PENDING_PAYMENT → PAYMENT_CONFIRMED → CONFIRMED + Voucher PENDING_PAYMENT → ISSUED + emits `InvoiceINV1Issued` per DEC-107 + DEC-112. (5) **Xero routing (Module E)** — Module E consumes the just-emitted INV1 + routes to Xero per DEC-072. **Operator-fallback (v17 §E.6 inheritance)**: NewCo Admin Panel manual-reconciliation surface for webhook-failure / mismatched-reference edge cases; Finance Analyst enters transfer details + matches to Order; on operator-confirmed match, Module E emits `BankTransferFundsCleared` as in primary path. **7-day expiry**: if no funds-cleared event fires within 7 calendar days per DEC-049, Module S auto-VOIDS Voucher + releases Allocation reservation per DEC-101; no INV1; no Module E financial event.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): webhook-driven primary path + operator-fallback surface locked.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-014 (Airwallex) + DEC-049 (7-day Cart Hold) + DEC-101 (PENDING_PAYMENT bank-transfer state) + DEC-102 (Voucher 8-state) + DEC-107 + DEC-112 (INV1 timing) + DEC-119 (Module-S-emitted INV1).
  - Literal Airwallex webhook contract (signature validation, retry semantics, idempotency keys) + Admin Panel UX downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-014 + DEC-049 + DEC-101 + DEC-102 + DEC-107 + DEC-112 + DEC-119; refines v17 §E.6 inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-160 — INV3 failed-charge → Hold escalation chain — 3-stage with admin-configurable cadences (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-5) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-5. Failed Airwallex charge for `InvoiceINV3Issued` triggers a cross-module escalation chain spanning Module E (retry + dunning) → Module K (Hold) → Module K (Profile Suspension). Operator-configurable thresholds per DEC-115 / DEC-083 admin parity.
- **Decision**: 3-stage escalation chain at NewCo launch with admin-configurable cadences:
  - **Stage 1 — retry within 14 calendar days of INV3 issuance (Module E)**: AirwallexAdapter retries per Airwallex's built-in retry behaviour (typically 3 attempts over 7-14 days for soft declines); Module E emits `AirwallexChargeFailed` per attempt for audit; HubSpot sends payment-reminder notification on Module E trigger event. No Hold; no Suspension. Aligns with v17 §E.6 failed-payment-handling (per-invoice retry counter; reset on successful charge).
  - **Stage 2 — `StoragePaymentFailed` → Module K Hold (Module E → Module K)**: after retry window expires (Day 14 default; admin-configurable), Module E emits `StoragePaymentFailed` (Customer ref + INV3 ref + outstanding amount); Module K creates Hold with `hold_type = STORAGE_PAYMENT_FAILED` per Module K v0.2 §14.8; Hold blocks NEW orders + NEW shipping per BR-K-Hold-1/2 (in-progress fulfillment unaffected per BR-K-Hold-5). Customer Hold-notification via HubSpot.
  - **Stage 3 — Profile Suspension (Module K)**: if Hold persists past BMD-§2.7 grace period (default 30 calendar days from `StoragePaymentFailed`; admin-configurable), Module K transitions Customer Profiles to Suspended per BMD §2.7 + Module K §6.3; Profile Suspension cascades per BMD §2.6 (Customer cannot purchase, cannot ship; stored bottles remain in custody until remediation).
  - **Hold lift on remediation**: Module E emits `StoragePaymentSucceeded` on successful charge; Module K lifts Hold per BR-K-Hold-Lift; Suspended Profiles transition back per BMD §2.6 reinstatement (operator review per BMD §2.6 retention discretion). Per v17 §E.3 rule 18 inheritance, write-off does NOT auto-lift the credit Hold — explicit operator action with auditable reason.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): 3-stage chain + cross-module event boundary + admin-configurable thresholds locked. NewCo Admin Panel surfaces thresholds for Finance Manager configuration.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-047 (chargeback Hold pattern companion) + DEC-083 + DEC-115 (admin parity) + DEC-118 + DEC-119 (Module-S-owned INV3).
  - Literal AirwallexAdapter retry-cadence configuration + dunning notification template selection + operator-UX for Hold-lift downstream per DEC-073 + `feedback_prd_rr_approval`.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-047 + DEC-083 + DEC-115 + DEC-118 + DEC-119; refines v17 §E.13 + v17 §E.3 rules 7 + 18 inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-07)**: Hold-lift discipline applies **per Hold type**, not uniformly. The v17 §E.3 rule 18 framing ("no auto-lift on write-off; explicit operator action with auditable reason code required") is binding for **chargeback / fraud / compliance / write-off / admin** Hold types — explicit operator lift required. **Auto-lift permitted** on payment-success (this DEC's `StoragePaymentSucceeded → Hold lift` mechanic preserved) and KYC-clear events — the underlying remediation event is itself an auditable record. Module K v0.2 §10.1 enumerates per-Hold-type discipline. Anchored at Module K v0.2 §10.1; closes E6-07.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-11)**: Multi-cycle INV3 composition under prior-cycle storage Hold — three rules: **(a)** Cadence continues unconditionally — INV3 fires every cycle regardless of prior Hold state (storage accrual is bottle-in-custody, not customer-state-dependent). **(b)** Per-cycle Hold-lift — `StoragePaymentSucceeded` for the current INV3 lifts the Hold tied to that cycle only; prior-cycle Holds remain until each is independently remediated. **(c)** Parallel chains — each cycle's failed INV3 runs its own 3-stage escalation chain independently; no cross-cycle aggregation. Anchored at Module E §3.3 + Module S §14; closes E6-11. — Settlement counterparty disambiguation — sell-through routes to Supplier; OC 5% × P_d routes to buyer's OC Producer regardless of bottle's Producer (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-6) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-6. Original analyst recommendation framed the OC payout as conditioned on the bottle's Producer ("OC share pays the bottle's Producer when the buyer's OC is operated by that Producer"). **Paolo flagged the slip** — buyer's OC gets 5% on every bottle that user buys on Discovery, regardless of bottle producer; bottle's Producer is irrelevant to OC routing. Correct rule per BMD §8.14 + DEC-066. Disambiguation must be locked at the Module E event-payload layer because sell-through compensation and OC share resolve to different counterparties in the common Discovery-with-Supplier-not-Producer pattern (DEC-082 + DEC-088).
- **Decision**: Module E settlement event payload carries the **counterparty Party reference resolved per the event's nature** (no generic "settlement counterparty" attribute):
  - **Sell-through settlement (per BMD §3.10 quarterly cadence)**: `SellThroughSettled` event carries `supplier_party_id` = PO counterparty per DEC-088; Module E aggregates per Supplier per settlement period for Supplier's quarterly settlement statement (per DEC-156 statement shape, scoped to Supplier's role on relevant Allocations).
  - **OC 5% × P_d share (per BMD §8.14, fired at INV1 issuance per DEC-112)**: `OCShareAccrued` event carries `originating_club_producer_party_id` = **buyer's OC Producer** resolved via `Customer.originating_club_id → Club.partner_producer_id` per DEC-066, **regardless of which Producer made the bottle**. Module E aggregates per OC Producer per settlement period; surfaces on **that OC Producer's** quarterly settlement statement (per DEC-156 section D).
  - **Producer-as-Supplier collapse (the common case for Club allocations + Discovery-direct-from-Producer per DEC-067)**: `supplier_party_id` and `originating_club_producer_party_id` may resolve to the same Party row when the bottle's Producer = OC Producer; Module E aggregates both events into the same producer's statement.
  - **Discovery-with-Supplier-not-Producer (the COMMON Discovery pattern per DEC-082)**: the two IDs differ; Module E generates two settlement statements per quarter — one to the Supplier (sell-through compensation per `commercial_terms` per DEC-092) + one to each OC Producer with member-OC accruals in the period (only if that Producer operates a Club whose members made Discovery purchases).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): event-payload disambiguation rule + cross-module Party-reference resolution boundary locked. `SellThroughSettled.supplier_party_id` and `OCShareAccrued.originating_club_producer_party_id` are independent FK targets resolved at emission time.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-066 (OC FK target = buyer's OC Producer) + DEC-067 (Producer ≠ Supplier separation) + DEC-082 (PO counterparty Supplier; Discovery-with-Supplier-not-Producer common) + DEC-088 (inbound-receiving Supplier always) + DEC-092 (commercial_terms drives sell-through amount) + DEC-112 (OC share emission timing) + DEC-156 (statement shape) + DEC-162 (info-disclosure constraint on section D).
  - Literal Module-K Party-reference resolution + statement-document data shape downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-066 + DEC-067 + DEC-082 + DEC-088 + DEC-092 + DEC-112; refines BMD §8.14 routing rule at Module E event-payload layer; corrects analyst slip in original Q-AD-6 question framing.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §8.14 prose already states the canonical rule ("Producer who operates the Originating Club"); correction is at Module E event-payload framing only.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-49)**: OC routing per-buyer for full multi-Allocation cart — per-buyer routing is preserved across partial-checkout splits. The OC Producer beneficiary is **single per-Order regardless of partial-checkout split** (buyer's OC Producer at Order time is locked; partial-checkout doesn't change it mid-flight); even a multi-Allocation cart that splits into multiple shipments routes all `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` events to the buyer's single OC Producer at Order time. Anchored at Module S §11 stacking prose; closes E6-49. — OC 5% × P_d share settlement timing + info-disclosure constraint — bundled in producer's quarterly statement; Section D aggregate-only (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-7) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-7. BMD §8.14 prose suggests OC share is bundled into the Producer's quarterly settlement statement. Settlement timing must be locked at the PRD level (bundled vs separate quarterly OC-share-only payment run vs real-time per-sale payment); Paolo's confirmation also surfaced a substantive **info-disclosure constraint** that composes with Q-CL-16 / DEC-156 section D content rule.
- **Decision**: OC share is **bundled in producer's quarterly settlement statement** (Option A — the BMD §8.14 prose interpretation):
  - **Settlement timing**: `OCShareAccrued` events fired at INV1 issuance per DEC-112; Module E aggregates per Originating-Club Producer per settlement period; OC-share section appears as **Section D** of the Producer's quarterly settlement statement per DEC-156; payment via Producer's invoice-back-to-NewCo on net-30 per BMD §3.10 (single invoice covers full settlement = direct club sales + direct Discovery sales + OC shares earned). OC share follows the SAME cadence as Producer's other settlement amounts (DEC-042 quarterly default; per-producer override via ProducerAgreement per DEC-070).
  - **Info-disclosure constraint (BMD §3.11)**: Section D shows **aggregate-only Discovery data** — share amount + anonymized transaction reference + running balance per period; **NO per-purchase-buyer detail** (cannot reveal that buyer A purchased bottles from Producer Y); **NO bottle's-Producer identity disclosure** (cannot reveal which other Producers' bottles drove the OC accrual). Full per-purchase detail (buyer identity, line items, allocation lineage) is shared ONLY for purchases on the producer's own club pages — i.e., own-club sales section A (where the producer is the bottle's Producer AND the buyer is their member). Composes with Q-CL-16 / DEC-156 section D content discipline.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): OC-share aggregation pipeline + Section D content discipline locked at event-payload composition layer. `OCShareAccrued` event payload carries anonymized transaction reference (no buyer identity, no bottle's-Producer identity).
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-032 (5% × P_d formula) + DEC-040 (no-OC admitted) + DEC-042 + DEC-066 + DEC-070 + DEC-112 + DEC-156 + DEC-161 (OC routing rule).
  - Literal Section D rendering UX + Producer Portal dashboard view per BMD §3.11 downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-032 + DEC-040 + DEC-042 + DEC-066 + DEC-070 + DEC-112 + DEC-156; reinforces BMD §3.11 info-disclosure principle at Module E event-payload layer.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §3.11 already states the principle.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-26)**: **No minimum-N redaction at NewCo launch**. Producer Portal Reporting v0.1 §6 OC accrual aggregates render at all N values, including small Clubs (N=1 trivial cases). The Section D info-disclosure constraint per BMD §3.11 + this DEC's quarterly-bundling discipline (no per-purchase-buyer detail; no bottle's-Producer identity; no buyer identity) is preserved at the event-payload + read-aggregation layers; member privacy at small Clubs is disclosed via T&C / membership terms (operating-manual scope per `feedback_prd_rr_approval`). Producer Portal Reporting §3 + §6 do not add a k-anonymity threshold or parent-period rollup at launch. Phase 2+ may revisit if member-volume composition risk grows or regulatory posture shifts. Closes E6-26 (no DEC-184 needed; the substantive call is "no threshold"). — Direct Purchase Module E flow — `SupplierPaymentCompleted` immediate Xero routing; informational reconciliation rows on settlement statement; V1 + V2 identical at settlement layer (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-8) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-8. For Direct Purchase Allocations, `SupplierPaymentCompleted` fires at PO creation per DEC-086. DEC-063 + BMD §3.10 lock the principle (no quarterly settlement aggregation for Direct Purchase) but Module E PRD must specify (a) immediate-vs-aggregated routing, (b) informational-row treatment on Supplier's quarterly statement, (c) V1-vs-V2 treatment at settlement layer.
- **Decision**:
  - **Direct Purchase (DEC-063 + DEC-086)**: Module E consumes Module D `SupplierPaymentCompleted` at the moment it fires (immediately on PO creation per DEC-086 Direct Purchase branch); routes the financial event to Xero per DEC-072 (real-time per DEC-156 + v17 §E.16 sync inheritance). Module E does NOT aggregate this event into the quarterly settlement-statement run — Direct Purchase is an immediate financial commitment, not a quarterly settlement amount due. Direct Purchase batches surface on Supplier's quarterly statement as **informational reconciliation rows only** per BMD §3.10 + DEC-156 Section E (units sold from the batch + refunds against the batch — no monetary settlement amount due). Producer-Portal dashboard surface per BMD §3.11 renders Direct Purchase activity for transparency.
  - **V1 + V2 (passive consignment, sell-through-settlement-cadence per DEC-086)**: Module D fires `PurchaseOrderIssued` at sell-through cadence + `SupplierPaymentCompleted` at Supplier's payment-completion moment per DEC-086 + DEC-091. From Module E's perspective, V1 and V2 are **identical** at the settlement-aggregation layer — both events feed the quarterly settlement statement per DEC-156. The DEC-086 distinction (V1 = goods-movement PO, V2 = financial PO against pre-positioned stock) is a Module D distinction; Module E records the same event regardless.
  - **Discriminator**: Module E `SupplierPaymentCompleted` consumer routes per `Allocation.sourcing_model`: Direct Purchase → immediate Xero routing + informational-only on settlement statement; V1 / V2 → quarterly aggregation + monetary amount on settlement statement.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): discriminator + cross-module event boundary locked. Per DEC-072, BMD/PRD do not take positions on GL-treatment difference between immediate-cash-out and quarterly-settlement; Xero decides.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-063 (Direct Purchase payment timing) + DEC-086 (PO timing three-way model) + DEC-091 (Module D event catalogue) + DEC-156 (statement shape Section E informational rows).
  - Literal Xero routing payload + reconciliation-row-vs-settlement-line data shape downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-063 + DEC-086 + DEC-091 + DEC-156; refines BMD §3.10 informational-row treatment at Module E event layer.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-164 — Refund clawback netting mechanics — within-period netting + cross-period clawback per DEC-025 cause matrix (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-9) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-9. BMD §3.10 names the netting principle (within-period: net at quarter-end; cross-period: claw back from next period). Module E PRD must lock: (a) which events Module E aggregates for clawback computation, (b) producer-fault vs NewCo-fault discrimination per DEC-025 matrix, (c) deduction-line treatment on producer's quarterly statement per DEC-156.
- **Decision**:
  - **Aggregation source**: Module E aggregates Module S `RefundIssued` events per Allocation per settlement period; each refund event carries `refund_cause` discriminator per DEC-025 matrix (`producer_fault` / `newco_fault` / `carrier_fault` / `customer_cancellation_pre_shipment` / `customer_fraud`).
  - **Producer-fault clawback (DEC-025 row 1)**: refund amount + any associated storage-fee pro-rata refund per DEC-046 clawed back from producer's settlement amount in the period the refund landed; appears as **deduction line in DEC-156 Section A or Section B** (depending on club vs Discovery). Cross-period clawbacks (sale settled in Q3, refunded in Q4) land in Q4's statement per BMD §3.10.
  - **NewCo-fault clawback (DEC-025 row 2 — in-custody breakage)**: NO clawback against producer; NewCo absorbs; Module E records cost on NewCo-side `NonRevenueCostRecorded` per DEC-167.
  - **Carrier-fault (DEC-025 row 3 — transit damage)**: carrier insurance recovery first; NewCo absorbs gap; Module E records gap as NewCo-side `NonRevenueCostRecorded` per DEC-167. NO producer clawback.
  - **Customer-cancellation-in-window (DEC-025 row 4 + DEC-108)**: NewCo absorbs the refund; Module E records as NewCo-side cost event. NO producer clawback (V1/V2 sell-through reverses cleanly — producer not yet paid; Direct Purchase clawback against producer-side commercial agreement, not customer's refund).
  - **Customer-fraud (DEC-025 row 6)**: NewCo absorbs immediately; Module E records as NewCo-side cost event; recovery via Airwallex dispute per DEC-168. NO producer clawback.
  - **Cross-period mechanics**: Module E indexes refund events by the **original sale's settlement period** (read from original `SellThroughSettled` event); refunds in the same period net within-period; refunds in a later period claw back from the later period's settlement amount.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): clawback aggregation pipeline + cause-discriminator routing + cross-period mechanics locked. Per DEC-072, BMD/PRD do not take positions on accounting-treatment of clawback (Xero decides whether to reverse prior-period revenue or treat as current-period adjustment).
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-025 (refund-cost matrix) + DEC-046 (storage-fee pro-rata refund) + DEC-108 (14-day window) + DEC-156 (statement shape Section A / B / C) + DEC-167 (`NonRevenueCostRecorded`) + DEC-168 (chargeback recovery).
  - Literal aggregation pipeline + Xero clawback-payload composition downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-025 + DEC-046 + DEC-108 + DEC-156 + DEC-167 + DEC-168; refines BMD §3.10 + §4.11 + §8.11 at Module E event-aggregation layer.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-165 — Refund execution ownership — Module S emits `RefundRequested`; Module E executes Airwallex refund API (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-10) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-10. When a Voucher is VOIDED via 14-day pre-shipment cancellation per DEC-108 or via supervisor-override post-delivery per DEC-138, the cash refund executes back to the customer's original payment method. Two ownership candidates (Module S executes vs Module E executes) — must be locked.
- **Decision**: Module S emits the refund event; Module E executes the Airwallex refund API call (Option A — v17 §E.6 inheritance with AirwallexAdapter substituting for StripeAdapter per DEC-014; Module E owns provider adapters). Refund flow at NewCo:
  1. **Refund trigger (Module S)**: Module S emits `RefundRequested` (Voucher ref + Order ref + cause discriminator per DEC-025 + refund amount + currency per DEC-109 1-voucher-per-bottle granularity per BMD §4.8 refund currency = original payment currency at original FX rate).
  2. **Airwallex refund execution (Module E)**: Module E reads original Payment record + AirwallexAdapter calls Airwallex refund API; on Airwallex confirmation, Module E updates Payment record + emits `RefundExecuted`.
  3. **Module S notification (Module E → Module S)**: Module E confirms refund-completed; Module S updates Order state (PARTIALLY_FULFILLED if partial-voucher cancellation; FULLY_FULFILLED if complete refund clears the order); customer-notification per HubSpot trigger.
  4. **Xero routing (Module E)**: Module E routes `RefundExecuted` to Xero per DEC-072 (real-time).
  5. **Producer clawback aggregation (Module E)**: per DEC-164, Module E aggregates `RefundExecuted` into producer's quarterly settlement clawback if cause = producer-fault per DEC-025.
- Per v17 §E.3 rule 1 inheritance, all refunds flow through credit-note discipline at the Xero layer; Module E does NOT direct-refund-to-payment-method outside the credit-note path (credit-note generation Xero scope per v17 §E.3 rule 14).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): Module-S-emit / Module-E-execute boundary + 5-step refund flow + cross-module event chain locked.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-014 (Airwallex) + DEC-025 (refund-cost matrix) + DEC-108 (14-day window + post-shipment WAIVED) + DEC-109 (1-voucher-per-bottle granularity) + DEC-119 (Module-S-owned customer-facing invoices) + DEC-138 (returns + replacement supervisor-override) + DEC-164 (clawback netting).
  - Literal Airwallex refund API contract + credit-note generation downstream per DEC-073 + Xero scope per v17 §E.3 rule 14.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-014 + DEC-025 + DEC-108 + DEC-109 + DEC-119 + DEC-138 + DEC-164; refines v17 §E.6 + v17 §E.3 rule 1 inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-166 — Credit-balance ownership Module K; credit-issuance + credit-application financial events Module E (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-11) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-11. NewCo has two credit instruments — Club Credit (Customer-Profile-level per Module K v0.2 §11 + DEC-043 / DEC-111) + store credit (Customer-level per DEC-044). Cross-module ownership of (a) the credit-balance entity, (b) read-and-debit at credit-application time, (c) credit-issuance + credit-application events for Xero accounting must be locked.
- **Decision**:
  - **Module K owns the credit-balance entity** (both Club Credit and store credit at Customer / Profile layer): Club Credit balance per Customer-Profile per Module K §11.2 (strict `credit.profile.club_id` match — no cross-Club credit pooling); store credit balance per Customer (Customer-level since portable across clubs); credit lifecycle entities (issuance reason, validity dates, conversion events per DEC-043); credit-application read-and-debit at checkout (Module S consumes Module K's read API per DEC-111 auto-apply).
  - **Module E records credit-issuance + credit-application financial events** for Xero routing, treating credit as a payment-method-equivalent payment instrument per v17 §E.3 rule 9 inheritance:
    - `StoreCreditIssued` / `ClubCreditAccrued` — credit-creation events (refund per DEC-044 goodwill mechanic; Hero Package per DEC-007; offboarding conversion per DEC-043).
    - `StoreCreditApplied` / `ClubCreditApplied` — credit-application events (consumed from Module S checkout per DEC-110 stacking step 3 + DEC-111 auto-apply).
    - All routed to Xero per DEC-072 (credit treated as prepayment instrument per v17 §E.3 rule 9 — INV1 issued at full sale price, credit offsets AR not invoice amount; Xero decides GL treatment).
  - Module E does NOT own the credit-balance entity; reads via Module K API for event-payload context (issuer, applied-amount, remaining-balance).
  - **Customer-Portal display**: balance from Module K source-of-truth; transaction history from Module E events for audit-trail completeness.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): cross-module read-from-Module-K + credit-as-payment-method discipline locked. Cites Module K v0.2 §11 by section number per DEC-074 self-contained delivery doc.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-007 (Hero Package = INV1) + DEC-043 (Club Credit on offboarding conversion) + DEC-044 (store credit goodwill premium) + DEC-110 + DEC-111 (stacking + auto-apply) + Module K v0.2 §11 (credit entities).
  - Literal Module-K-API contract for credit-balance read + credit-event-payload schema downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-007 + DEC-043 + DEC-044 + DEC-110 + DEC-111; refines v17 §E.3 rule 9 + v17 §E.12 inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-167 — `NonRevenueCostRecorded` unified wrapper financial event for replacement / breakage / transit-loss / write-off (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-12) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-12. Per DEC-072 + DEC-138 + DEC-151 + DEC-132, Module E records non-revenue cost events for replacement shipments + insurance claims + custody breakage + write-offs. PRD must lock whether Module E emits a unified wrapper financial event for Xero routing or consumes upstream events directly.
- **Decision**: Module E emits a unified `NonRevenueCostRecorded` wrapper financial event for each upstream non-revenue trigger (Option A — per v17 §E.5 Financial Event Record discipline). Wrapper carries `cost_cause` discriminator (`replacement_shipment_per_DEC-138` / `custody_breakage_per_DEC-132` / `transit_breakage_per_DEC-151` / `transit_loss_per_DEC-151` / `write_off_per_DEC-151` / `insurance_recovery_per_DEC-151`) + upstream event reference + cost basis + allocation lineage + currency. **Triggers**:
  - **Replacement (DEC-138)**: Module C `ReplacementShipmentIssued` → Module E records `NonRevenueCostRecorded` with cost = bottle cost basis + replacement shipping cost; routes to Xero per DEC-072.
  - **Custody breakage (DEC-132)**: Module B `BottleBreakageInCustody` → Module E records `NonRevenueCostRecorded` with cost = bottle cost basis; if customer-fault matrix per DEC-025 attributes to producer (rare for custody — typically NewCo-absorbed per DEC-025 row 2), Module E ALSO records the producer clawback per DEC-164.
  - **Transit breakage / loss (DEC-151)**: Module C `BottleBreakageInTransit` / `BottleLossInTransit` → Module E records `NonRevenueCostRecorded`; carrier-insurance recovery flows back as separate `InsuranceRecoveryReceived` event reducing net cost.
  - **Insurance claim resolution (DEC-151)**: Module C `InsuranceClaimResolved` → Module E records `InsuranceRecoveryReceived` (net negative cost = insurance settlement received); Xero offsets the prior `NonRevenueCostRecorded`.
  - **Write-off (DEC-151)**: Module C `BottleWriteOff` → Module E records `NonRevenueCostRecorded` (uncollectible loss).
- Per DEC-072, Module E records the events; Xero decides whether each becomes P&L line, balance-sheet adjustment, or other treatment per accounting policy.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): wrapper event + cost-cause discriminator + cross-module trigger boundary locked. Wrapper preserves v17 §E.5 Financial Event Record immutability discipline + provides uniform Xero-routing surface.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-025 (refund-cost matrix) + DEC-132 (Module B custody breakage) + DEC-138 (Module C replacement) + DEC-151 (Module C breakage / loss / write-off / insurance) + DEC-164 (producer clawback aggregation).
  - Literal payload schema + cost-basis-resolution algorithm downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-025 + DEC-132 + DEC-138 + DEC-151 + DEC-164; refines v17 §E.5 + v17 §E.17A inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-23)**: Replacement-trigger description + insurance-pool metadata. **Trigger timing**: NonRevenueCost wrapper fires at **replacement-ship** — cost recognised immediately when `ReplacementShipmentIssued` fires (Module C §15 per DEC-184 Returns/Replacement FSM); insurance recovery (if applicable per DEC-048 carrier-pool / NewCo-supplementary-pool framing) is a downstream net-back at claim resolution (deferred to `InsuranceClaimResolved → InsuranceRecoveryReceived` chain). **Insurance-pool metadata**: `insurance_pool ∈ {carrier, newco_supplementary}` enum captured on `InsuranceClaimOpened` event payload per DEC-048 to preserve recovery-routing lineage from claim through resolution. Anchored at Module E §8.2 + Module C §15.1; closes E6-23.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-24)**: Cost-basis on substitution. When DEC-167 NonRevenueCost wrapper fires for a replacement-shipment, the cost basis recorded is the **substitute Allocation's bottle cost** — the actual cost of the bottle that ships to the customer. The original Allocation's bottle cost is recorded as a **separate write-off event** per DEC-132 — the original bottle is the loss; insurance recovery (if applicable per DEC-048 / E6-23 above) offsets the write-off downstream at claim resolution. Substitution event metadata (`original_allocation_id` + `substitute_allocation_id` payload fields) preserves Allocation lineage. Margin reconciliation reads two distinct financial events (NonRevenueCost on substitute cost + WriteOff on original cost) plus optional InsurancePoolPayment, not a conflated single wrapper. Anchored at Module C §4.4 + §10.4 + Module E §9; closes E6-24.

---

## DEC-168 — Chargeback Module E flow — Airwallex webhook → Module E records loss + flags Customer → Module K Hold + fraud-pattern review (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-13) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-13. Per DEC-047, chargebacks via Airwallex; ops responds within 7 business days; Customer flagged for fraud-pattern review. Cross-module flow must be locked: Airwallex webhook ingestion + financial loss event recording + Module K Hold creation + dispute resolution treatment.
- **Decision**: 5-step cross-module chargeback chain:
  1. **Airwallex chargeback webhook (Airwallex → Module E)**: Airwallex pushes `dispute.created` (or analogous) webhook on customer-issuer chargeback; Module E validates + records receipt.
  2. **Module E records financial loss event + routes to Xero**: Module E emits `ChargebackReceived` financial event (Customer ref + Payment ref + chargeback amount + dispute-reason code + currency) + `ChargebackPotentialLoss` provisional cost event (loss provisional pending dispute resolution); both routed to Xero per DEC-072. Per DEC-072, Xero decides accounting treatment (provision for bad debt, contingent liability).
  3. **Module K Hold + fraud-flag (Module E → Module K)**: Module E emits `CustomerChargebackFlagged` (Customer ref + chargeback context); Module K creates Hold with `hold_type = CHARGEBACK_REVIEW` per Module K v0.2 §14.8 (blocks NEW orders + NEW shipping per BR-K-Hold-1/2) + flags Customer for fraud-pattern review (admin-visible attribute on Customer; field shape Module K PRD scope per DEC-073).
  4. **Ops dispute response (NewCo Admin Panel — Operations role)**: per DEC-047 7-business-day SLA, Operations submits dispute evidence package to Airwallex via Airwallex tooling per BMD §8.9.
  5. **Dispute resolution (Airwallex → Module E)**: Airwallex pushes `dispute.resolved` (or analogous) webhook with outcome (win / loss); Module E emits `ChargebackResolved`; on win, Module E records `ChargebackRecovered` financial event (loss reversed); on loss, prior `ChargebackPotentialLoss` materializes per Xero treatment.
- **Hold does NOT auto-lift on dispute resolution** — per v17 §E.3 rule 18 inheritance + Module K v0.2 BR-K-Hold-Lift discipline, lifting Hold requires explicit operator action with auditable reason; `fraud_pattern_review` flag persists for the configurable retention window per Module K policy.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): 5-step chain + cross-module event boundary + Hold-no-auto-lift discipline locked.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-014 (Airwallex) + DEC-047 (chargeback policy) + DEC-160 (general failed-charge → Hold pattern; chargeback uses distinct Hold type) + Module K v0.2 §14.8 (Hold entity) + v17 §E.3 rule 18 (Hold-lift discipline).
  - Literal Airwallex dispute-API contract + Admin Panel UX for dispute-evidence management downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-014 + DEC-047 + DEC-160; refines v17 §E.3 rule 7 + rule 18 + rule 20 inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-45)**: Chargeback cross-module event ownership at the **behavioral-contract layer**: Module K is the Hold registry-of-record per Module K v0.2 §10.1; on `CustomerChargebackFlagged` emission by Module E (Step 3 above), **Module K consumes the event and fires `HoldCreated` of type `chargeback` (CHARGEBACK_REVIEW)**. Module E does NOT create the Hold directly; Module S does NOT own this surface. The event-bus subscription mechanism vs synchronous API call between Module E and Module K is downstream tech per DEC-073; the behavioral contract (Module K owns Hold creation on chargeback) is explicit at the spec layer. Anchored at Module E §5.6 + Module K §14.8; closes E6-45.

---

## DEC-169 — Multi-currency event recording + DEC-038 FX policy operational mechanics — dual-currency on every financial event (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-16) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-16. NewCo runs multi-currency at launch per DEC-037 (5 customer-facing currencies — EUR + USD + GBP + CHF + JPY); base ledger currency EUR per BMD §8.8. DEC-038 commits the FX policy principle (daily-snapshot mid-rate-plus-buffer); operational mechanics deferred to PRD Module E. Module E records financial events that may be in any of the 5 currencies; dual-currency recording + FX rate resolution must be locked.
- **Decision**: Module E records dual-currency on every financial event (original currency + EUR equivalent) using DEC-038 FX model:
  - **Dual-currency recording**: every Module E financial event payload carries `amount` + `currency` (original) + `eur_equivalent_amount` + `fx_rate` + `fx_rate_date`. Inherits v17 §E.5 SELL_THROUGH_SETTLEMENT pattern — both numbers on the event for audit + Xero treatment.
  - **FX policy operational mechanics (DEC-038)**:
    - **Snapshot time** = end of day Europe/Rome (NewCo's incorporation jurisdiction per DEC-015 — provisional pending Q-AD-15 / DEC-171 deferral; alternative jurisdiction would substitute).
    - **Buffer percentage** = admin-configurable per DEC-115 / DEC-083 parity (default value left to Finance Manager configuration per `feedback_prd_rr_approval`; PRD does not hardcode).
    - **Refresh cadence** = daily (one snapshot per Europe/Rome business day).
    - **Rate source** = Airwallex's published mid-market rate (operational consistency between capture-time + event-recording FX per DEC-014).
    - **Saturday / Sunday / bank-holiday** = use prior business-day rate (no weekend FX refresh).
  - **Refund currency rule (BMD §4.8)**: refunds use original payment's currency at original payment's FX rate (NOT fresh snapshot); Module E `RefundExecuted` event carries original payment's `fx_rate` + `fx_rate_date` references.
  - **Settlement currency for producers (BMD §3.10)**: EUR by default; producers opting for their currency receive settlement amounts converted at snapshot rate at settlement-emission date; `ProducerSettlementStatementIssued` (DEC-156) carries snapshot rate + date.
  - **Airwallex capture-side**: if Airwallex's actual FX at capture differs from Module E's snapshot rate (rare but possible at low volumes), Module E records gap as `FXVarianceRecorded` event for Xero treatment per DEC-072.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): dual-currency event payload + FX policy operational mechanics + admin-configurable buffer locked.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: composes with DEC-014 (Airwallex multi-currency capture) + DEC-015 (Italy provisional incorporation; alternative jurisdiction would shift snapshot timezone) + DEC-028 (Xero multi-currency) + DEC-037 (5 launch currencies) + DEC-038 (FX policy principle) + DEC-083 + DEC-115 (admin parity) + DEC-156 (statement currency) + DEC-165 (refund currency rule) + DEC-171 (Q-AD-15 SDI deferral cross-link).
  - Literal FX-snapshot ingestion mechanism + FX-variance reconciliation algorithm downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-014 + DEC-015 + DEC-028 + DEC-037 + DEC-038 + DEC-083 + DEC-115 + DEC-156 + DEC-165; operationalises DEC-038 at Module E PRD layer; refines v17 §E.5 + v17 §E.15 inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §3.10 + §4.8 + §8.8 already commit to the principle.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
- **Stage 6.5 clarification (2026-05-08, E6-48)**: Multi-currency rate-lock per leg. For cross-currency transactions (e.g., customer pays USD on a Discovery purchase where supplier was paid EUR + OC accrued), each leg's FX rate is locked at its respective financial-event-emission moment, not at a single shared moment: **customer-USD rate locked at `PaymentCaptureSucceeded`** (or `BankTransferFundsCleared` for bank-transfer per DEC-159); **supplier-EUR rate locked at `SupplierPaymentCompleted`** (per DEC-086 / DEC-091); **OC rate locked at INV1 emission** (per DEC-112). Three independent FX moments, each preserving the rate-locked dual-currency recording per this DEC's payload schema. Inter-leg FX delta accumulates as P&L per Xero downstream treatment per DEC-072. Anchored at Module E §8 + Module D §16; closes E6-48.

---

## DEC-170 — Module E event catalogue at launch — emitted + consumed events (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-17) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-17. Module E PRD must lock the launch event catalogue (Module-E-side companion to DEC-091 Module D + DEC-136 Module B catalogue precedents). Catalogue covers events Module E emits + events Module E consumes from upstream modules.
- **Decision**: Module E launch event catalogue:
  - **EMITS at launch**:
    - `AirwallexChargeExecuted` / `AirwallexChargeFailed` (per DEC-158 / DEC-160 — INV1/INV2/INV3 charge execution).
    - `BankTransferFundsCleared` (per DEC-159 — Airwallex webhook consumption notification consumed by Module S to fire INV1).
    - `RefundExecuted` (per DEC-165 — Airwallex refund completed).
    - `ChargebackReceived` / `ChargebackResolved` / `ChargebackRecovered` (per DEC-168 — Airwallex chargeback lifecycle).
    - `CustomerChargebackFlagged` (per DEC-168 — emitted to Module K to create chargeback Hold + fraud-flag).
    - `StoragePaymentFailed` / `StoragePaymentSucceeded` (per DEC-160 — INV3 charge outcome events consumed by Module K for Hold / Suspension lifecycle).
    - `NonRevenueCostRecorded` (per DEC-167 — wrapper financial event for replacement / breakage / transit-loss / write-off).
    - `InsuranceRecoveryReceived` (per DEC-167 — insurance settlement received).
    - `ProducerSettlementStatementIssued` (per DEC-156 — quarterly settlement statement emitted with five-section breakdown).
    - `OCShareAccrued` (per DEC-161 + DEC-162 — 5% × P_d share accrued at INV1 issuance per DEC-112; alt name `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` per BMD §8.14 vocabulary — naming choice per DEC-073).
    - `SellThroughSettled` (per DEC-164 — sell-through settlement event aggregated for producer's quarterly statement).
    - `XeroSyncCompleted` / `XeroSyncFailed` (per v17 §E.16 inheritance — Xero sync lifecycle).
    - `COGSAdjustmentRecorded` (per v17 §E.5 inheritance — cost-basis revision; rare at NewCo since V2 default per DEC-092).
    - `FXVarianceRecorded` (per DEC-169 — Airwallex-vs-snapshot FX gap).
  - **CONSUMES at launch (upstream events from other modules)**:
    - **Module S**: `InvoiceINV1Issued` + `InvoiceINV2Issued` + `InvoiceINV3Issued` (per DEC-119); `RefundRequested` (per DEC-165); `OrderPaymentPending` (for bank-transfer flow per DEC-159); `StoreCreditApplied` / `ClubCreditApplied` (per DEC-166); supervisor-override post-delivery refund event per DEC-108 + DEC-138.
    - **Module D**: `SupplierPaymentCompleted` (per DEC-163 — direct routing for Direct Purchase, quarterly aggregation for V1/V2); `InboundEventCostFinalized` (for `COGSAdjustmentRecorded` per v17 §E.5).
    - **Module C**: `ReplacementShipmentIssued` (per DEC-167 + DEC-138); `BottleBreakageInTransit` / `BottleLossInTransit` / `BottleWriteOff` (per DEC-167 + DEC-151); `InsuranceClaimResolved` (per DEC-167 + DEC-151); `ShippingFeeQuoted` + `ShipmentDispatched` (informational — actual shipping fee on INV2).
    - **Module B**: `BottleBreakageInCustody` (per DEC-167 + DEC-132).
    - **Module K**: read-only access to ProducerAgreement.settlement_cadence (per DEC-070); read-only access to `Customer.originating_club_id → Club.partner_producer_id` (per DEC-066) for OC share routing per DEC-161; read-only access to credit-balance entities (per DEC-166).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): catalogue documented with v17-inheritance-vs-NewCo-addition flags + cross-module ownership boundaries (per DEC-091 + DEC-136 pattern precedents).
  - **Cross-module cascades**: catalogue is the system-of-record for Module E's event repertoire; all other Wave 5 DECs reference catalogue entries.
  - Literal event payload field-by-field listings stay out (event names + business signals only); tech team picks payload schema downstream per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-066 + DEC-070 + DEC-091 + DEC-108 + DEC-112 + DEC-119 + DEC-132 + DEC-136 + DEC-138 + DEC-151 + DEC-156 + DEC-158 + DEC-159 + DEC-160 + DEC-161 + DEC-162 + DEC-163 + DEC-164 + DEC-165 + DEC-166 + DEC-167 + DEC-168 + DEC-169; refines v17 §E.3-§E.5 inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
