## DEC-171 — Wave 5 Q-OQ batch confirmation + Q-AD-15 deferral — 3 deferrals stand (Wave 5 Module E Q-AD-15 + Q-OQ-19 + Q-OQ-20) (2026-05-12)
- **Context**: Wave 5 Module E Q-OQ-19 (paid services / experiences + INV4 invoice type) + Q-OQ-20 (partial PO settlement) confirmed deferred at launch by Paolo. Additionally, Q-AD-15 (SDI connector boundary) **reclassified from lock to deferral** by Paolo because Italian incorporation is not yet confirmed (per DEC-015 provisional disposition); SDI obligation is contingent on incorporation jurisdiction. All three deferrals folded into a single batch DEC mirroring DEC-058 / DEC-155 precedents.
- **Decision**: Three deferrals stand at NewCo launch; Module E v0.1 PRD documents each explicitly + flags Phase 2+ extension as future-DEC items:
  - **Q-AD-15 — SDI connector boundary (DEFERRED)**: cross-links DEC-015 (Italy incorporation provisional) + DEC-028 (Xero+SDI clause). The architectural principle (Module E sends payload to Xero only; document + regulatory-XML generation downstream per v17 §E.3 rule 14) remains valid as a working assumption per DEC-072, but the literal SDI connector selection + integration spec wait on incorporation confirmation. Phase 2+ revisits when incorporation jurisdiction confirmed; alternative jurisdiction (UK / France / other) would substitute the e-invoicing connector model accordingly.
  - **Q-OQ-19 — paid services / experiences + INV4 invoice type (DEFERRED)**: BMD §4.14 explicitly lists paid experiences as placeholder; mechanics not operationalized at launch. Q-OQ-8 / DEC-058 confirmed deferred upstream. Module E does NOT introduce INV4 at launch (per DEC-157 invoice typology lock = INV1 + INV2 + INV3 only). When paid experiences operationalize Phase 2+, INV4 invoice type lands in Module E typology + EVENT_CONSUMPTION_SETTLEMENT financial event lands for V2-event-consumption settlement (per v17 §E.4 + §E.5 EVENT_CONSUMPTION_SETTLEMENT pattern). Free experiences (per BMD §4.14) generate booking events but no transaction; Module E has no role for free experiences.
  - **Q-OQ-20 — partial PO settlement (DEFERRED)**: per `project_v12_partial_po_settlement_gap` memory + DEC-091 inheritance, `SupplierPaymentCompleted` is **atomic per PO** in the current event model — one event, fired when NewCo pays the entire PO. Real-world POs sometimes get partial settlements (NewCo pays 80% + disputes 20%; milestone-based payments; cashflow negotiation). Current model can't represent these — no `partial_amount` or `outstanding_balance` fields on the event. Phase 2+ extension would extend `SupplierPaymentCompleted` with partial-amount + outstanding-balance fields; Module E would aggregate per partial-event into the settlement statement; Xero would handle partial-payment accounting per its policy. At launch volume, partial PO settlements are operationally exceptional + handled via manual Xero adjustments + ops-managed dispute workflow.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module E PRD** (Wave 5): all three deferrals documented in §0 deferred-items section; per-PO-atomicity assumption explicitly stated (DEC-091 inheritance) at §10; SDI connector deferral cross-references DEC-015 + DEC-028 at §16; Phase 2+ flagged as future-DEC items.
  - **Cross-module cascades**: Module D (PO entity + `SupplierPaymentCompleted` event shape — Phase 2+ extension); Module S (no Offer subtype for paid services at launch); Module 0 (no service catalog entity at launch); Module K (no service-booking-related Customer/Profile attribute changes; ProducerAgreement payment-terms might evolve to include partial-settlement clauses).
  - **Wave 5 cross-cutting**: deferrals consolidated into `qa.deferred.md` register per Wave 5 cross-cutting deliverable per DEC-003 final wave + kickoff §7.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-015 (Italy provisional) + DEC-028 (Xero+SDI provisional inheritance) + DEC-058 (Wave 1 Q-OQ batch precedent) + DEC-091 (Module D event catalogue + atomicity inheritance) + DEC-155 (Wave 4 Q-OQ batch precedent) + DEC-157 (invoice typology lock — INV4 dropped/deferred); refines DEC-072 + v17 §E.4 + v17 §E.5 inheritance.
- **BMD revision**: none — all three deferrals already explicitly out-of-scope or provisional in BMD v0.8.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-172 — SO-cancellation Voucher revert restarts storage-fee accrual (Stage 4 Q-AD-1) (2026-05-13)
- **Context**: Stage 4 cross-module integration audit Q-AD-1. Module S BR-S-Storage-5 says storage-fee accrual stops on Voucher → REDEMPTION_REQUESTED. Module C `ShippingOrderCancelled` returns the Voucher state to ISSUED on SO cancellation pre-shipment. PRDs were silent on whether storage accrual re-starts when the Voucher returns from REDEMPTION_REQUESTED → ISSUED on SO cancellation.
- **Decision**: When a Voucher returns from REDEMPTION_REQUESTED → ISSUED on Module C `ShippingOrderCancelled`, storage-fee accrual **re-starts**. Customer continues to be billed monthly storage at €0.25/bottle/month per DEC-118. REDEMPTION_REQUESTED is the only stop trigger for BR-S-Storage-5; symmetric treatment with the storage-clock conditions (`max(INV1+12mo, InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted)` past + bottle at warehouse) preserved. Aligns with BMD §3.13 storage policy ("12 months free + €3/bottle/year for as long as the bottle is in custody").
- **Implications**: Module S v0.1 §11.2 + §14.2 + §18.10 BR-S-Storage-5 + §11.6 (per-state matrix) — clarify the only-stop-trigger semantics + REDEMPTION_REQUESTED → ISSUED revert path. Customer-facing storage-fee display + INV3 aggregation logic now coherent on SO-cancellation cycles. Operationally rare per DEC-108 14-day pre-shipment cancellation window; PRD-level disambiguation prevents implementation drift.
- **Amends / supersedes**: refines DEC-119 (Module S owns storage clock + accrual events) + DEC-118 (storage policy mechanics preserved) + DEC-108 (14-day pre-shipment cancellation window).
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §3.13 storage prose already neutral on the SO-cancellation cycle.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-174 — Club Credit + Store Credit lifecycle three-event-flow split (Stage 4 Q-CL-18) (2026-05-13)
- **Context**: Stage 4 cross-module integration audit Q-CL-18. Three-PRD inconsistency on Club Credit / Store Credit lifecycle: Module K v0.2 §15.8 (Module E emits to Module K — v17-inherited); Module S v0.1 §16.8 (Module S emits `ClubCreditAutoApplied` / `ClubCreditRemovedByCustomer` / `StoreCreditApplied` at checkout-render or customer action per DEC-111); Module E v0.1 §8.2 + §9.3 (Module E consumes Module S application events + emits `ClubCreditAccrued` / `StoreCreditIssued` to Module K per DEC-166). DEC-166 establishes credit-balance entity Module-K-owned + financial events Module-E-owned; cross-module emit/consume reconciliation needed.
- **Decision**: Club Credit + Store Credit lifecycle uses a **three-event-flow split** across Modules S / E / K:
  - **Module S** emits customer-facing application events (`ClubCreditAutoApplied` / `ClubCreditRemovedByCustomer` / `StoreCreditApplied`) at checkout-render or customer action per DEC-111.
  - **Module E** emits financial-event variants (`ClubCreditAccrued` / `StoreCreditIssued`) at credit-balance-creation moments (Hero Package asymmetric-price overflow per DEC-007; refund crediting per DEC-025; OC share routing per DEC-110) per DEC-166.
  - **Module K** is the credit-balance-entity owner per DEC-166 (Module K v0.2 §11) and consumes from BOTH Module S and Module E to maintain the balance state.
- **Implications**: Module K v0.2 §15.8 — drop "Module E emits Club Credit lifecycle events to Module K" framing; document the three-actor split explicitly (consumes from Module S for application; consumes from Module E for accrual / issuance; balance entity remains §11). Module K v0.2 §11 — preserve balance-entity mechanics; only upstream-emitter routing changes. Clusters with DEC-173 + DEC-175 in a single Module K v0.2 §15.8 reframe revision.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-007 + DEC-025 + DEC-110 + DEC-111 + DEC-166; supersedes Module K v0.2 §15.8 inherited framing on Club Credit + Store Credit lifecycle.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-175 — `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` emission = Module S; canonical event name (Stage 4 Q-CL-19) (2026-05-13)
- **Context**: Stage 4 cross-module integration audit Q-CL-19. Both Module S v0.1 §16.7 and Module E v0.1 §8.1 list this event in their EMIT catalogues with different names (Module S: `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued`; Module E: `OCShareAccrued` with note "alternative naming = `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued`; naming choice downstream per DEC-073"). The "alternative naming" framing in Module E §8.1 hides the cross-module ambiguity — the question is event-emission-ownership, not just naming.
- **Decision**: `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` is **Module-S-emitted at INV1 issuance** per DEC-112 (post-payment-cleared timing); Module E consumes for Xero routing per DEC-072. The canonical event name is `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` (BMD §8.14 vocabulary, more descriptive of business meaning) — `OCShareAccrued` is internal shorthand, not the cross-module canonical event. The reversal event `DiscoveryRevenueShareReversed` (per DEC-108 + DEC-112 cancellation flow) follows the same shape: Module S emits, Module E consumes.
- **Implications**: Module E v0.1 §8.1 — move `OCShareAccrued` from EMIT list to CONSUME list under canonical name `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued`; document the consume side ("consumes `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` from Module S per DEC-112; routes to Xero per DEC-072 + DEC-162 Section D aggregate-only"); drop "alternative naming downstream per DEC-073" framing. Composes with DEC-180 on event payload composition (no Customer ref). Clusters with DEC-173 + DEC-174 in the post-DEC-119 three-actor split realignment.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-072 + DEC-112 + DEC-119 + DEC-161 + DEC-162; supersedes Module E v0.1 §8.1 stale framing.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §8.14 vocabulary is the authoritative source for the canonical event name.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-176 — `RefundRequested` + `OrderRefunded` as two distinct events (Stage 4 Q-AD-4) (2026-05-13)
- **Context**: Stage 4 cross-module integration audit Q-AD-4. Module S v0.1 §16.3 + §16.11 emit list does NOT list `RefundRequested`; Module E v0.1 §8.2 + §9.1 + Architecture v0.1 §3.5 step 5 assume Module S emits it. Either two distinct events at two lifecycle stages, or naming variants for one event. The refund flow has two natural moments (request → execution; execution → completion).
- **Decision**: Refund flow uses **two distinct events** at two lifecycle stages:
  - **`RefundRequested`** — Module S emits at refund-issuance moment; Module E consumes to execute the Airwallex refund per DEC-165. Carries Order ref + Voucher ref(s) + refund cause per DEC-025 cause matrix + amount.
  - **`OrderRefunded`** — Module S emits at refund-completion moment after Module E `RefundExecuted`. Carries the Module E `RefundExecuted` reference + final Order state.
  Pattern mirrors the bank-transfer two-stage chain (Module S `OrderPaymentPending` → Module E `BankTransferFundsCleared` → Module S `OrderConfirmed`).
- **Implications**: Module S v0.1 §16.3 + §16.11 emit list — add `RefundRequested`. Module S v0.1 §17.7 — split the two events along the lifecycle. Module S v0.1 §11 / §12.7 — document the Order state transitions surrounding the two events. No Module E PRD edit needed (Module E §8.2 + §9.1 already document `RefundRequested` consumption per DEC-165).
- **Amends / supersedes**: refines DEC-165 (refund execution Module-S-emit / Module-E-execute split) at the event-catalogue layer; closes Module S v0.1 §16 emit-list completeness gap.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-177 — `AllocationPoolDebitedDueToLoss` = Module-A-emitted (Stage 4 Q-AD-9) (2026-05-13)
- **Context**: Stage 4 cross-module integration audit Q-AD-9. Module B v0.1 §7.4.4 + §8.3 + Module C v0.1 §15.4 reference Module A as emitter of `AllocationPoolDebitedDueToLoss` for the §6.11.4 in-custody-destruction cascade per DEC-132 + DEC-136. Module A v0.1 §12 event catalogue does NOT list the event. Module B + Module C reference an event Module A's PRD does not document.
- **Decision**: `AllocationPoolDebitedDueToLoss` is **Module-A-emitted** on consumption of Module B `BottleDestroyedInCustody` per DEC-132 + DEC-136. Payload carries source allocation reference + debited qty + source bottle's serial reference + destruction event reference. Consumers: Module C (replacement-stock-availability per Module C §15.4) + Module E (cost-basis traceability per `NonRevenueCostRecorded` allocation lineage per DEC-167). Pool debit fires only on bottles in the unsold sub-pool per BR-S-Voucher-6 ↔ DEC-117 recall scope discipline; rare bound-Voucher case routes via Module S substitution per DEC-104.
- **Implications**: Module A v0.1 §12.2 (Operations events) — add the event to the catalogue with consume-from-B + emit-on-A cascade documented. Module A v0.1 §11.5 (Module B cross-module section) — document the cascade. Module A v0.1 §10.2 BR-A-Mutability-1 — clarify destruction-driven decrement respects the anti-orphan invariant.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-117 + DEC-132 + DEC-136 + DEC-167; closes Module A v0.1 §12 event-catalogue completeness gap.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §6.11.4 already neutral on cross-module event ownership.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-178 — Cart Hold per-Allocation `qty_held` aggregation owner = Module S (Stage 4 Q-AD-11) (2026-05-13)
- **Context**: Stage 4 cross-module integration audit Q-AD-11. Producer Portal Reporting v0.1 §4 surfaces a per-Allocation `qty_held` count (active Cart Holds at any given moment) for the Producer-side sell-through report; aggregation owner unspecified across PRDs (Module A maintains a transient counter? Module S exposes via aggregation surface? Producer Reporting composes from raw events?).
- **Decision**: The per-Allocation Cart Hold count aggregation owner is **Module S**. Module S maintains the aggregation as a transient indicator (read-on-demand or refreshed via Cart Hold lifecycle event emission); Producer Portal Reporting reads from Module S surface. Aligns with DEC-095 Cart-as-Module-S-entity boundary; preserves Module A's upstream-supply-primitive boundary (Module A owns Allocation-level state — qty, sub-pool, commercial-terms — not transient Cart Hold aggregation).
- **Implications**: Module S v0.1 §16.2 (Cart-family events) or §18.4 (BR-S-CartHold rules) — document per-Allocation aggregation surface; refresh cadence at the product-event level: real-time per Cart Hold lifecycle event emission. Producer Portal Reporting v0.1 §8 cross-module read contract (table row §4 sell-through) — clarify aggregation owner is Module S; driving events are `CartHoldCreated` / `CartHoldExpired` / `CartHoldConvertedToOrder`.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-095 + DEC-105 + DEC-106; closes Producer Portal Reporting v0.1 §4 + §8 cross-module aggregation-owner ambiguity.
- **BMD revision**: none.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-179 — Composite Offer atomic transactional rollback at voucher issuance (Stage 4 Q-AD-12) (2026-05-13)
- **Context**: Stage 4 cross-module integration audit Q-AD-12. Multi-producer Discovery composite Offer voucher issuance per DEC-097 + DEC-061: at voucher-issuance time, what happens if one or more constituent Allocations cannot fulfill the per-bottle decrement? Cart Hold acquisition + 15-min strict timer per DEC-105 + DEC-106 makes failure rare but not negligible; composite SKU atomicity per Module 0 §13.5 BR-SKU-3 requires unambiguous failure-handling.
- **Decision**: At voucher-issuance time on a multi-producer Discovery composite Offer, if any constituent Allocation cannot fulfill the per-bottle decrement, the entire Order rolls back: no Vouchers issue, payment is voided / refunded, Order transitions to PAYMENT_FAILED with cause = `composite_constituent_unavailable`. **Atomic transactional rollback**; partial-Voucher-set issuance is forbidden. Aligns with composite SKU atomicity per Module 0 §13.5 BR-SKU-3 and customer's commercial commitment (purchased composite, not N independent items).
- **Implications**: Module S v0.1 §16.3 (Order-family events) — add `OrderPaymentFailed` cause discriminator for composite-constituent-unavailable case (or document the cause as a free-text reason on the existing `OrderPaymentFailed` payload). Module S v0.1 §18.1 BR-S-Identity-3 + §18.3 BR-S-Publication-6 — extend with a voucher-issuance-time invariant analogous to publication-time ("all N constituent Allocations must successfully decrement at composite-Offer voucher issuance, or the Order rolls back entirely; no partial-Voucher set issuance"). Customer-facing UX (failure message, refund path) is downstream tech per DEC-073.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-061 + DEC-097 + DEC-105 + DEC-106 + Module 0 §13.5 BR-SKU-3.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §4.6 transaction shape already implies composite atomicity.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-180 — Discovery share event payload structural Section D enforcement (Stage 4 Q-AD-13) (2026-05-13)
- **Context**: Stage 4 cross-module integration audit Q-AD-13. The `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` event payload (per Module S v0.1 §16.7) carries Customer ref for OC-routing purposes. The Section D info-disclosure constraint per BMD §3.11 + DEC-162 requires aggregate-only Discovery data at the Producer Portal — Discovery buyer identity NEVER traverses to the Producer side. The constraint is currently enforced at the read layer (Producer Portal Reporting aggregation discipline); future Producer-side integration that bypasses the aggregation layer could leak Discovery buyer identity.
- **Decision**: Strip Customer ref from the `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued` event payload; enforce the Section D info-disclosure constraint at the **data layer** (event payload structure), not only at the read layer. Module S resolves OC routing internally before emission (reads Customer's locked `originating_club_id` per DEC-066 + DEC-112 → resolves to `Club.partner_producer_id` → derefs to the OC Producer recipient); the emitted event payload carries only the resolved Producer reference + aggregate amount + Order ref (for internal allocation lineage; not Producer-Portal-rendered). Same shape applies to `DiscoveryRevenueShareReversed`. Producer Portal Reporting aggregation discipline at the read layer becomes defense-in-depth, not sole enforcement.
- **Implications**: Module S v0.1 §16.7 — strip Customer ref from payload; payload composition: Order ref (internal lineage only) + resolved `Club.partner_producer_id` (the OC Producer recipient; no Customer identity) + share amount (5% × headline `P_d`). Module S v0.1 §18.11 BR-S-OCShare-2 — re-frame "read-at-emission" as Module S internal state-lookup before emission; emitted event carries only the resolved Producer reference + aggregate. Producer Portal Reporting v0.1 §3 + §6 — clarify structural constraint enforced at event-payload level. Module E v0.1 §8.1 (per DEC-175) — align consumed-event documentation with aggregate-only payload. Composes with DEC-175 (emission ownership + canonical name).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-066 + DEC-112 + DEC-161 + DEC-162 + DEC-175; structurally hardens BMD §3.11 Section D info-disclosure constraint at the event-payload layer.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §3.11 commitment is the source; structural enforcement is downstream.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-181 — Sanctions/Hold uniformity principle: every transaction-initiation surface reads sanctions and Hold state at the moment of action (Stage 6.5 E6-01) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Stage 5 Phase 5 invariant audit surfaced two FAILs (I-C-08 sanctions cross-surface uniformity + I-C-09 Hold blocking matrix uniformity); Phase 4 dual-persona walkthroughs flagged W-CC-04 firm REAL_BUG plus W-CC-03 / W-CC-05 / W-CC-09 candidates plus W-CC-12 GDPR×Hold edge; Phase 6 surfaced L6-01 Cart Hold sanctions-gate finding + L6-04 SO `planned` Hold finding; Phase 2 surfaced L2-24.a/b gifting × Hold gate. Pattern: per-surface enumeration of sanctions and Hold gates leaks at every unenumerated surface — Cart Hold reservation, SO `planned` transition, INV3 charge, refund routing, gifting initiation, and pickup handover were each under-enumerated at one or more sites. Surface-by-surface enumeration is finite; new surfaces require explicit re-implementation; the structural invariant cannot be maintained that way.
- **Decision**: Anchor a generic principle at Module K v0.2 §4.8 (Hold entity) + §14.8 BR-K-Hold-2: **every transaction-initiation surface reads sanctions state and Hold state at the moment of action**. Transaction-initiation surfaces include (non-exhaustive at launch): order completion / purchase (Module S §10.1), gifting initiation (Module S §13), pickup handover (Module C §5), INV3 charge (Module E §3.3 + Module S §14.1), refund routing (Module E §5), Cart Hold reservation at cart-add (Module S §8), SO `planned` transition (Module C §2.3), Voucher redemption-request (Module S §11.7), shipment-request initiation (Module C §3.5). Each downstream module's gate prose locally re-cites the principle; the upstream principle wording at Module K v0.2 §4.8 is the source-of-truth. Future transaction-initiation surfaces inherit by-property without explicit re-enumeration; the spec does not need to be amended each time a new surface is added — the principle covers them. (Stage 7.1 anchor cleanup 2026-05-08: prior enumeration anchors of `Module K v0.2 §10.1`, `Module E §10`, `Module S §11.6`, `Module S §11.5`, `Module C §3.3` corrected to actual PRD landings.)
- **Implications**:
  - **Module K v0.2 §4.8** (Hold entity) — generic-principle wording added; **§14.8 BR-K-Hold-2** reframed to anchor the cross-surface invariant at the upstream layer.
  - **Module S** — §10.1 sanctions gate prose re-cites the principle; §13.1 gifting initiation re-cites; §14.1 INV3 reads sanctions/Hold at charge moment; §11.7 Voucher redemption-request re-cites (Stage 7.1); §8 Cart Hold reservation at cart-add re-cites (Stage 7.1).
  - **Module C** — §2.3 SO `planned` transition re-cites; §5 pickup handover re-cites; §3.5 shipment-request initiation re-cites (Stage 7.1).
  - **Module E** — §5.1 refund routing re-cites; §3.3 INV3 charge execution re-cites.
  - **BRs touched**: BR-K-Hold-2 (re-anchor); BR-S-Hold-* family (gate-uniformity principle inherited); BR-C-* SO transition gates (re-cite); BR-E-* refund + INV3 charge gates (re-cite).
  - **Closes**: E6-01 + E6-02 + E6-03 + E6-04 + E6-05 + E6-06 + E6-37 + E6-50 (Phase 5 I-C-08 + I-C-09 FAILs; Phase 4 W-CC cluster; Phase 6 L6-01 + L6-04; Phase 2 L2-24.a/b).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-160 (Hold-lift discipline) + DEC-168 (chargeback Hold) + the v17 §E.3 sanctions-gate rule heritage. Supersedes the per-surface enumeration discipline that was implicit at Wave 1/3/4/5 PRD drafting.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §10 sanctions stance + §10.7 KYC discipline are upstream; this DEC anchors the cross-surface invariant at the PRD layer.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-182 — OC accrual reversal symmetry on refund and replacement (Stage 6.5 E6-22) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Phase 2 L1-28 REAL_BUG candidate. When a Discovery purchase that triggered OC accrual (DEC-112 — 5% × `P_d` paid to buyer's OC Producer) is refunded or replaced, the spec did not name the reversal symmetry explicitly. DEC-180 already named `DiscoveryRevenueShareReversed` as a possible event but the trigger conditions and the replacement-vs-refund semantics were unstated. Phase 5 I-B-02 OC immutability (CONDITIONAL LOW) holds — immutability locks at the first-purchase moment; reversal is a separate event composition.
- **Decision**: OC accrual **reverses symmetrically** on refund and on replacement. The reversal is implemented via `DiscoveryRevenueShareReversed` (already named per DEC-180) firing as a mirror-event to the original `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued`. Replacement does **not** preserve OC binding from the original purchase: on replacement the original accrual reverses + a fresh accrual fires keyed to the buyer's current `originating_club_id` at replacement time. (In practice the OC Producer is typically the same — buyer's OC Producer rarely changes mid-flight — but if it has changed, the replacement's fresh accrual routes to the current OC Producer.) Producer Settlement Statement Section D rendering reads the net (accruals − reversals) per period.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module S §16.7** — `DiscoveryRevenueShareReversed` event catalogued symmetrically alongside `DiscoveryRevenueShareAccrued`; payload mirrors per DEC-180 structural Section D enforcement (no Customer ref; resolved Producer reference + reversal amount + Order ref).
  - **Module E §8** — refund and replacement triggers both compose the OC-reversal mirror event into the financial-event chain; Producer Settlement Statement Section D rendering reads net (accruals − reversals).
  - **Module C §15** — Returns/Replacement FSM (per DEC-184) at REPLACEMENT_ISSUED transition emits both the original-OC-reversal and the fresh-OC-accrual on the new purchase composition (when the OC Producer is unchanged the reversal + re-accrual net to zero by construction; explicit composition preserved for audit clarity).
  - **BRs touched**: BR-S-OCShare-* (extend to cover reversal symmetry); BR-E-Refund-* (compose with OC reversal mirror).
  - **Closes**: E6-22.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-066 + DEC-112 + DEC-138 + DEC-161 + DEC-162 + DEC-175 + DEC-180.
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §3.11 + §1.3 OC mechanic preserved; reversal symmetry is downstream PRD-layer event composition.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-183 — Allocation activation harmonized as "sellable" across sourcing models; SupplierPaymentCompleted is financial-event-only (Stage 6.5 E6-32) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Phase 2 L2-03.b REAL_BUG candidate. Voucher issuance for Direct Purchase customers can occur while the parent Allocation is in DRAFT state, because DEC-081 / DEC-086 wired the DRAFT → ACTIVE trigger to `SupplierPaymentCompleted` (which fires after the customer has already purchased). This creates a "Voucher ISSUED on a DRAFT Allocation" gap window between customer purchase and supplier payment. Paolo correctly observed during Stage 6.5 Phase B that an Allocation with a live Offer attached (which is selling) is *de facto* active; "DRAFT while selling" is semantically inconsistent. Under passive consignment (V1/V2), Allocation already activates at operator-publish without any cash flow — so "ACTIVE = paid" was never the rule for V1/V2; Direct Purchase was the anomaly.
- **Decision**: **Harmonize the DRAFT → ACTIVE trigger across sourcing models**. ACTIVE is defined as **"Allocation is sellable"** (offer can go live, Vouchers can be ISSUED) uniformly across sourcing models. Direct Purchase Allocations activate at **operator-publish post-PO-commit**, not at `SupplierPaymentCompleted`. `SupplierPaymentCompleted` remains a Module D / Module E financial event recording supplier payment, but it does **not** drive Allocation FSM. Supplier-payment-failure on a Direct Purchase becomes a financial-recovery scenario (operator queue + customer refund per DEC-104 + DEC-165), not an Allocation-FSM-state-mismatch scenario. The "Voucher ISSUED on DRAFT Allocation" gap window dissolves at the FSM layer (Voucher issuance can no longer occur on a DRAFT Allocation by construction). The 4-state FSM (DRAFT → ACTIVE → CLOSED → RETIRED) is preserved.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module A v0.1 §4 + §5.3.2** — DRAFT → ACTIVE trigger description updated: uniform "operator-publish post-PO-commit" trigger across V1 / V2 / Direct Purchase; `SupplierPaymentCompleted` removed from FSM-trigger framing (retained as financial event reference only).
  - **DEC-081 + DEC-086** — Stage 6.5 clarification entries appended explaining that the DRAFT → ACTIVE trigger reframing aligns activation with sellability and demotes `SupplierPaymentCompleted` to financial-event scope only; original DEC bodies preserved.
  - **Module S §11.6** — gap-window prose (Voucher-ISSUED-on-DRAFT-Allocation) replaced with a brief note that supplier-payment-failure on Direct Purchase is a financial-recovery path (operator queue + refund per DEC-104 + DEC-165), not an FSM-state mismatch.
  - **Module D §14.4** — clarify that `SupplierPaymentCompleted` records supplier payment but does not drive Allocation activation; the upstream Allocation activation is operator-driven at offer-publish.
  - **BRs touched**: BR-A-Lifecycle-1 (trigger description harmonized); BR-A-Lifecycle-4 (no impact — terminal-state rules preserved); BR-S-Voucher-* (issuance gate now strict on Allocation ACTIVE by construction).
  - **Closes**: E6-32 + E6-33 (cluster-folded — Discovery DRAFT case closes by the same harmonization).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-077 + DEC-063 + DEC-104 + DEC-165; refines the trigger description in DEC-081 + DEC-086 (the DEC bodies are preserved verbatim; clarification entries appended for the Stage 6.5 reframing).
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §3 sourcing models + §5 commercial flow preserved; the harmonization is a PRD-layer FSM-trigger refinement.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-184 — Module C Returns/Replacement FSM at NewCo launch (Stage 6.5 E6-34) (2026-05-08)
- **Context**: Phase 2 L2-09.a REAL_BUG. Module C v0.1 lacks an explicit Returns/Replacement state machine; events are anchored at DEC-138 but state is implicit (computed-on-read from event sequence). Other Module C entities follow explicit-FSM discipline (SO 5-state per DEC-139); Returns is the lone event-only flow. PRD readability + downstream operator-tooling design benefit from explicit FSM; consistency with the other Module C entities is preserved.
- **Decision**: Module C v0.1 introduces an **explicit Returns/Replacement entity with FSM** at launch: `REPORTED → INVESTIGATED → APPROVED → REPLACEMENT_ISSUED → CLOSED` with `REJECTED` and `WITHDRAWN` as terminal pre-replacement off-ramps. Each transition emits the event already named at DEC-138 + DEC-167 (`PostShipmentIssueReported` → `ReturnReceiptRecorded` (rare) → `ReplacementShipmentIssued` → `ReplacementShipmentDelivered` plus closure). Replacement-routing dispatches per the late-binding two-surface algorithm (DEC-137); cost-basis on the NonRevenueCost wrapper is the substitute Allocation's bottle cost per DEC-167 Stage 6.5 clarification (this DEC composes with E6-24's clarification of DEC-167).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module C v0.1 §15** — Returns/Replacement FSM added; transitions enumerated; each transition's event citation per DEC-138 + DEC-167 + this DEC.
  - **Module C v0.1 §15** — `ShippingOrderManualReviewRequired` event added (NewCo addition; tertiary fallback for the late-binding tiebreak per DEC-137 Stage 6.5 clarification).
  - **Module S §17.4** — cross-module contract: Module S consumes `ReplacementShipmentIssued` (Customer notification) per DEC-138; original Voucher state preserved through replacement (no new Voucher; no new INV2) per DEC-108 + DEC-138.
  - **Module E §8** — replacement financial routing: NonRevenueCost wrapper at `ReplacementShipmentIssued` per DEC-167 Stage 6.5 clarification (substitute cost basis); InsurancePoolPayment downstream at claim resolution per DEC-048 + DEC-167.
  - **BRs touched**: new BR-C-Returns-* family (FSM transitions + emission + Voucher-state preservation); BR-S-Voucher-* (clarification on no-state-change-on-replacement).
  - **Closes**: E6-34.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-104 (substitution mechanic) + DEC-108 (no new Voucher / no new INV2) + DEC-137 (late-binding) + DEC-138 (replacement event chain) + DEC-167 (NonRevenueCost wrapper).
- **BMD revision**: none — BMD §4.10 / §4.11 / §5.10 (returns + replacement principle) preserved; FSM is downstream PRD layer.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-185 — Module B inventory-authority restoration scope (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-1) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-1 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.1 (lines 3341-3345) framed Module B as "the authoritative system of record for Crurated's physical inventory" tracking inventory across four orthogonal dimensions (ownership, custody, commercial status, allocation lineage). NewCo Module B v0.1 (released 2026-05-08 as part of v1.0) narrowed scope to a digital-provenance layer (SerializedBottle / NFC / NFT / Bottle Page); §1.3 boundary statement explicitly disclaimed physical-inventory authority. v0.1's narrowing leaves five architectural gaps: vendor-risk concentration on Logilize, four-way reconciliation collapse to three-way, non-serialized stock unhomed (DEC-133 smoking-gun), WMS-agnostic future blocked, and custody/ownership/lineage as commercial-not-WMS concerns. Stage 8 launch decision (2026-05-09) corrects.
- **Decision**: Module B v0.2 restores the v17 §B.1 inventory-authority framing in full. **Module B = ERP-side inventory authority** — ledger discipline; entity ownership for InboundBatch + StockPosition + Case + QuarantineRecord; ATP source; receiving physical-match authority; stocktake + adjustment authority; provenance immutability; no-overselling at physical level; committed-inventory protection. **Logilize = physical-state execution arm** — in-warehouse / in-transit / delivered / damaged / lost-in-custody state; pick-pack-dispatch execution; storage-location detail at sub-warehouse granularity. Inventory tracked across four orthogonal dimensions: (1) **ownership** — 2-value enum `PRODUCER` / `CRURATED` at NewCo launch per DEC-001 + DEC-068 (v17's third value `THIRD_PARTY` is OUT per Q-CL-2 confirmation; AgencyAgreement entity stays OUT); (2) **custody** — warehouse + storage-location reference; (3) **commercial status** — `available` / `committed` / `reserved`; (4) **allocation lineage** — immutable UUID per DEC-076. Provenance immutability (Q-CL-1) extends to all state / custody / ownership / commercial-status changes — internal audit chain at SerializedBottle (per-bottle) + InboundBatch (per-batch NS) granularity; customer-facing Bottle Page provenance trail per DEC-128 reads downstream of the internal chain. No-overselling **two-layer guard** (Q-CL-5) restored: Module A enforces at allocation-pool level (`qty − issued ≥ 0` per DEC-099); Module B enforces at physical-inventory level (`physical_in_storage − reserved − quarantined − under_adjustment ≥ 0` per v17 §B.8); both must pass at hold placement / voucher issuance, strongly consistent at the transactional boundary. **Committed-inventory protection** (Q-CL-6) restored: inventory committed to vouchers cannot be diverted for internal transfers / adjustments without first releasing the commitment via Module A `VoucherCancelled`; the v17 §B.3 rule 7 "event consumption" clause is N/A at NewCo launch (no events at launch per DEC-068) and reactivates if events land in Phase 2+. **Storage-location read contract** (Q-CL-3) preserved: Module B exposes warehouse-level summary per SerializedBottle (serialized) and per InboundBatch (NS) for Cellar render + Bottle Page; sub-warehouse granular detail (row / rack / cellar zone) stays Logilize-internal per DEC-153. **Bottle-days-in-storage data contract** (Q-CL-4) preserved: Module B answers the per-allocation bottle-days query; Module S computes the storage fee at INV2 per DEC-119; Module E records the financial event per DEC-072. v0.1 NFT/provenance content (DEC-120..DEC-132 + DEC-134..DEC-136) preserved unchanged in v0.2 as a sub-layer of Module B's broader ledger role.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §0 + §1 purpose + boundary restored to v17 §B.1 framing; §2 entity catalogue extended to include InboundBatch + StockPosition + Case + QuarantineRecord (per DEC-191..DEC-196); §3 invariants restate provenance-immutability (BR-8), no-overselling two-layer (BR-6), committed-inventory protection (BR-7), quarantine-before-trust (BR-9), recorder-not-gatekeeper (BR-10), and the four orthogonal dimensions; subsequent §B.4-§B.13 inventory-ledger sections added per DEC-186..DEC-196; v0.1 §5 SerializedBottle / NFC / NFT / Bottle Page content folded as digital-provenance sub-layer; §1.2 boundary statement explicitly disclaims `THIRD_PARTY` ownership (Q-CL-2 confirmation), AgencyAgreement entity, ConsignmentPlacement entity (per DEC-193), and v17 §B.9a third-party custody intake.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module A v0.2 (ATP-feed-from-Module-B path per DEC-187); Module C v0.2 (DEC-140 5-stream contract split per DEC-188); Module D v0.2 (receiving discrepancy authority restoration per DEC-194); Module E v0.2 (inventory-adjustment + loss/damage event ingestion per DEC-190); Module S v0.1 (storefront ATP source verification — touch-only); Module 0 + Module K (no inventory-side dependencies — verify only).
  - **BMD cascade** (Phase D — informational only): BMD v0.9 §6 + §9.8 + reconciliation discipline reframing (Logilize = execution arm, Module B = inventory authority).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-076 (allocation lineage immutability) + DEC-068 (B2C-only at launch — locks ownership_flag enum at 2-value) + DEC-001 (no agency at NewCo launch) + DEC-099 (Module A allocation-pool arithmetic preserved as the first guard layer) + DEC-128 (Bottle Page provenance trail customer-facing rendering) + DEC-153 (storage-location warehouse-level customer-facing display) + DEC-118 + DEC-119 (storage-fee mechanic Module-S-internal). Foundational for DEC-186..DEC-196 (Stage 8 Module B inventory-ledger entity + workflow DECs); v0.1 boundary-statement narrowing (Module B PRD v0.1 §1.3) is restated by this DEC.
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-186 — Non-serialized inventory at InboundBatch level — DEC-133 supersession (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-2) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-2 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.5a (lines 3454-3468) tracks non-serialized inventory at InboundBatch level with four counters: `qty_planned_serialize`, `qty_actually_serialized`, `qty_non_serialized_committed`, `qty_non_serialized_reserved`. NS inventory is **permanent / fulfillable** state, NOT transitional. v0.1 DEC-133's five no-op clauses (no SerializedBottle, no NFC, no NFT, no Bottle Page, no recovery chain) are correct on the **digital-provenance** axis but wrong on the **inventory-ledger** axis — NS stock has no ERP-side home in v0.1.
- **Decision**: Module B v0.2 tracks non-serialized inventory at the **InboundBatch level** with the v17 §B.5a counter set: `qty_planned_serialize` (planned serialization target), `qty_actually_serialized` (actual serialization completed), `qty_non_serialized_committed` (NS units committed to vouchers), `qty_non_serialized_reserved` (NS units in cart-hold / pre-issuance reservation). NS-pool ATP = `received_quantity − qty_planned_serialize − qty_non_serialized_committed − qty_non_serialized_reserved`. Serialization-plan-vs-actual divergence emits `BatchSerializationDiscrepancy` event (per v17 §B.5 late-serialization-on-plan-increase path). DEC-133's five no-op clauses are **re-scoped** from "Module B no-op on NS" to "Module B no-op on NS **digital-provenance** only" — NS stock has full inventory-ledger discipline at the InboundBatch level (counters, ATP, audit, adjustments); the absence of state in DEC-133's five clauses is reframed as absence of *digital-provenance* state, not absence of inventory-ledger state. DEC-133 is **superseded** by this DEC.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B.5a NS-at-InboundBatch counter set + ATP formula + `BatchSerializationDiscrepancy` event; §1.2 boundary clarified (NS no-op = digital-provenance only); v0.1 DEC-133 prose reframed accordingly; cross-link to DEC-186 supersession.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module A v0.2 (`AllocationSerializationPlanChanged` consumer + late-serialization-on-plan-increase path per v17 §B.5); Module C v0.2 (NS batch-quantity pick instructions per v17 §C.6 + DEC-188 fulfillment streams); Module E v0.2 (NS adjustment financial events per DEC-190).
- **Amends / supersedes**: **supersedes DEC-133** (re-scopes the five no-op clauses from inventory-ledger axis to digital-provenance axis; DEC-133 informational-event clarification at Stage 6.5 / E6-47 preserved); composes with DEC-080 (per-allocation NS opt-out) + DEC-052 (NS Offer badge) + DEC-125 (NFC application controlled by sub-pool partition) + DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational).
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-187 — ATP feed pattern: Module B → Module A push (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-4) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-4 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.8 (lines 3523-3545) commits to dual ATP exposure (`atp_serialized` / `atp_non_serialized`) per allocation, with Module A reading Module B's sub-pool ATP for the sub-pool overselling rule (Module A §3.3a rule 2). Display ATP staleness ≤5s; transactional ATP at hold placement strongly consistent. v0.1 has no ATP feed (Module A v0.1 §7 self-serves from `qty − issued` allocation-pool arithmetic per DEC-099). Restoring Module B's inventory-authority role per DEC-185 makes Module B's physical-custody count the second number Module A needs alongside its allocation-pool count to detect Logilize-side inventory loss before it surfaces at fulfillment.
- **Decision**: ATP feed pattern between Module B (physical-custody count) and Module A (allocation-pool count) is **Module B → Module A push** (v17 model). Module B emits inventory events on every state change (`BottleStateChanged`, `InventoryAdjusted`, `OwnershipTransitioned`, `BottleQuarantined`, `BottleQuarantineResolved`, `StocktakeReconciled`, NS-pool counter mutations); Module A maintains a cached ATP per allocation; hold placement reads the cache (real-time strongly consistent by construction). Display-ATP cache staleness ≤5s; transactional reads (hold placement) cannot tolerate stale ATP, so the push pattern bounds latency cheaply. Pull pattern (Module A queries Module B on demand) rejected — hold-placement latency unbounded, failure-mode coupling at Module B unavailability blocks all hold placement. Hybrid (push for transactional + pull for display) rejected — more moving parts without matching benefit. Sub-pool ATP (`atp_serialized` + `atp_non_serialized`) exposed separately per allocation; both layers (Module A allocation-pool + Module B physical) must pass at hold placement per Q-CL-5 two-layer guard.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B.8 ATP-feed contract restored; emitted-event catalogue for Module A consumption documented; sub-pool ATP formula per allocation; cross-link to DEC-187 + DEC-196.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module A v0.2 (ATP cache per allocation; sub-pool overselling rule restored at hold placement; consumer of Module B inventory events; composes with DEC-099 allocation-pool layer); Module S v0.1 (storefront display ATP read path verification — touch-only); Module C v0.2 (late-binding warehouse-efficiency reads per DEC-137 + DEC-188 unchanged).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-099 (`qty − issued` allocation-pool arithmetic preserved as Module A's allocation-pool layer; Module B's physical layer adds the second guard) + DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational) + DEC-076 (allocation lineage UUID stable) + DEC-196 (StockPosition mutations source the push).
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-188 — Logilize stream split: Module C 4-stream fulfillment + Module B 5-stream inventory-state — DEC-140 supersession (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-12) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-12 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). DEC-140 (decisions.md line 1571) committed Module C ↔ Logilize integration to a 5-stream contract: (1) outbound shipment instruction; (2) pick confirmation; (3) dispatch confirmation; (4) delivery confirmation; (5) storage-location tracking. DEC-140 is correct on the **fulfillment** axis but wrong on the **inventory-state** axis — Stream 5 (storage-location tracking) is inventory-state (custody dimension per DEC-185 four-orthogonal framing), not fulfillment, and the stocktake / adjustment / quarantine streams that v17 §B.10 commits Module B to are absent from DEC-140 entirely.
- **Decision**: Logilize streams **split between Module C (fulfillment) and Module B (inventory-state)** at NewCo launch. **Module C owns ~4 fulfillment streams**: outbound pick instruction (1), pick confirmation (2), dispatch confirmation (3), delivery confirmation (4) — DEC-140's first four streams retained verbatim. **Module B owns ~5 inventory-state streams**: storage-location tracking (5 — migrated from Module C per the original DEC-140 framing), inbound receiving + physical-match (existing — was already Module B / Module D scope per BMD §5.3 + DEC-194 receiving-discrepancy authority), stocktake instruction + variance reporting (new per DEC-189), inventory-adjustment proposal-and-confirmation (new per DEC-190), QuarantineRecord resolution flow (new per DEC-191). The two-system split preserves DEC-140's clarity on the fulfillment side while restoring Module B's inventory-state authority. Module B observes Module C dispatch events for SerializedBottle digital-state transitions (NFT burn cross-module chain per DEC-134 unchanged) but does not own them. DEC-140 is **superseded** by this DEC on the inventory-state axis (Stream 5 storage-location migrates Module C → Module B; new inventory-state streams added net-new); the 4 fulfillment streams remain Module C's per the original DEC-140 framing.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B-Logilize-integration (new section) documents the 5 inventory-state streams; storage-location tracking documented as Module B's read-summary contract for Cellar render per DEC-153 (sub-warehouse detail stays Logilize-internal); receiving + stocktake + adjustments + quarantine streams cited from DEC-194 / DEC-189 / DEC-190 / DEC-191.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module C v0.2 (§4 5-stream contract reduced to ~4-stream fulfillment contract; Stream 5 storage-location migration noted; Cellar render data composition unchanged per DEC-153); Module D v0.2 (no change — receiving was already Module B / Module D scope per BMD §5.3); BMD v0.9 §6.3 + §11.3 reframing (Phase D).
- **Amends / supersedes**: **supersedes DEC-140** (splits the 5-stream contract; Stream 5 storage-location migrates Module C → Module B; new inventory-state streams added net-new); composes with DEC-141 (Logilize / NewCo ERP reconciliation contract — split source-of-truth preserved) + DEC-014 (Logilize same provider, separate integration) + DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational) + DEC-153 (storage-location warehouse-level summary contract).
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 §6.3 + §11.3 reframing lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-189 — Stocktake authority + 4-state lifecycle at Module B (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-6) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-6 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.10 (lines 3625-3629) commits Module B to a stocktake authority + 4-state lifecycle: `planned → in_progress → variance_review → reconciled`. Supervisor plans stocktake scoped by warehouse / location / Bottle Reference, with target date and configurable variance tolerance threshold; WMS executes the physical count; Module B compares counts to the ledger per scoped entity and computes variances. v17 §B.1b primary persona is Logistics / Operations Manager. v0.1 has no stocktake. Without stocktake, Logilize-side drift goes undetected for months and the four-way reconciliation discipline collapses — stocktake is the third leg alongside receiving (DEC-194) and adjustments (DEC-190).
- **Decision**: Module B v0.2 owns the **Stocktake entity + 4-state lifecycle** (`planned → in_progress → variance_review → reconciled`). Scope at planning: warehouse / storage-location / Bottle Reference; target date; variance tolerance threshold (configurable per scope). WMS (Logilize) executes the physical count per DEC-188 (stocktake instruction + variance reporting stream); Module B compares Logilize counts to the ledger and computes variances per scoped entity. Variance resolution path emits `InventoryAdjusted` event (per DEC-190) per the supervisor's resolution decision (`damage` / `loss` / `recount` / `transfer` / `found`). **Stocktake-cadence policy is operator setting**, not PRD content — per `feedback_prd_rr_approval` (no authority-tier policy at PRD layer); no committee-vs-single-approver policy at PRD; single-supervisor-approval discipline applied uniformly. Persona = Logistics / Operations Manager per BMD v0.8 §11 ops staffing.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B.10 Stocktake entity + 4-state FSM + variance computation discipline + supervisor-approval flow restored; cadence-policy explicitly left to operator setting; cross-link to DEC-190 adjustment event chain.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module A v0.2 (ATP recalculation on stocktake-driven adjustments per DEC-187 push); Module E v0.2 (variance-driven adjustments emit financial events per DEC-072 + DEC-190).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational) + DEC-188 (Logilize stocktake stream) + DEC-190 (adjustment event composition) + `feedback_prd_rr_approval` (no authority-tier policy at PRD).
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-190 — Inventory-adjustment workflow + event catalogue (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-7) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-7 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.10 (lines 3608-3624) commits Module B to an adjustment workflow: WMS variance / operator observation → operator proposal → supervisor approval → terminal state (`damage` / `loss` / `consumption` / `recount` / `transfer` / `found`) + provenance event. Cross-module: damage / loss / write-off events emit to Module E for financial-event recording per DEC-072. v0.1 has no adjustments. NewCo simplification (DEC-068 + v0.1): no event consumption at launch (`consumption` adjustment type retained as placeholder reason; reactivated when events land in Phase 2+ per BMD v0.8 simplifications).
- **Decision**: Module B v0.2 owns the **inventory-adjustment workflow + event catalogue** at launch. Adjustment proposal flow: operator-initiated (or stocktake-variance-derived per DEC-189; or QuarantineRecord-resolution-derived per DEC-191) → supervisor approval → terminal-state event emission. Adjustment types: `damage`, `loss`, `consumption` (placeholder for Phase 2+), `recount`, `transfer`, `found`. **Events emitted by Module B**: `InventoryAdjusted` (with `adjustment_type` discriminator + scope: bottle id for serialized / batch id + qty for non-serialized / case id for case-integrity adjustments per DEC-192); `InventoryShortfallDetected` (when adjustment reduces committed inventory below outstanding vouchers — emitted to Module A to drive shortfall workflow per Module C §C.8 inheritance + Module S substitution path per DEC-104). **Module E consumes** `InventoryAdjusted` for damage / loss / write-off financial-event recording per DEC-072; Xero decides GL treatment per `feedback_bmd_prd_no_accounting`. Single-supervisor-approval path uniformly per `feedback_prd_rr_approval` (no committee-vs-single approval policy at PRD layer). **Loss / damage / write-off catalogue is coterminous with this DEC** — originally anticipated as a separate Stage 8 plan §5 DEC; folded here per kickoff guidance because the `adjustment_type` discriminator in `InventoryAdjusted` already captures `damage` / `loss` / write-off (`recount` covering write-off as the reason discriminator value when the resolution is "qty was wrong on the books"); no separate event-set required at launch. **Committed-inventory protection guard** (per DEC-185 Q-CL-6) enforced at adjustment-proposal-validation: a proposal that would reduce committed inventory below outstanding vouchers is rejected and instead emits `InventoryShortfallDetected` to Module A — the proposal cannot proceed until Module A `VoucherCancelled` first releases the commitment.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B.10 adjustment workflow + event catalogue + supervisor-approval flow + `InventoryShortfallDetected` short-circuit on committed-inventory reduction; loss/damage/write-off discriminator values enumerated; v0.2 §B.10 explicitly notes `consumption` as Phase-2+ placeholder.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module A v0.2 (`InventoryShortfallDetected` consumer; substitution / refund path per DEC-104 + DEC-138); Module C v0.2 (§C.8 shortfall workflow inheritance — fulfillment-time shortfall handling); Module E v0.2 (financial-event ingestion per DEC-072 for damage / loss / write-off; `consumption` placeholder no-op at launch).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-072 (Module E events not accounting policy) + DEC-104 (substitution mechanic) + DEC-138 (replacement event chain) + DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational) + DEC-189 (stocktake variance-derived adjustments) + DEC-191 (QuarantineRecord resolution-derived adjustments) + `feedback_prd_rr_approval` + `feedback_bmd_prd_no_accounting`.
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-191 — QuarantineRecord entity + quarantine-before-trust principle (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-10) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-10 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.2 (line 3380) + §B.3 rule 9 (line 3400) commit Module B to "**Quarantine Before Trust**: Module B never creates inventory records from unverified WMS data. Unknown entities reported by WMS are quarantined pending manual investigation." Resolution paths: associate with existing batch / create new record / reject as invalid / escalate. Each resolution captures supervisor identity + decision + reason + resulting mutation. Resolved QuarantineRecords are immutable. v0.1 has no QuarantineRecord. Without it, four-way reconciliation degrades — Logilize-side errors (serial mismatches, batch confusion) propagate undetected into Module B's ledger, the exact failure mode Stage 8 corrects.
- **Decision**: Module B v0.2 owns the **QuarantineRecord entity** with the quarantine-before-trust principle. Module B never creates inventory records from unverified Logilize data; unknown entities reported by Logilize land in QuarantineRecord pending manual supervisor investigation. **Resolution paths** (each captured with supervisor identity + decision + reason + resulting mutation + timestamp): (1) **associate with existing InboundBatch** — serial / batch id mapping; downstream cost-basis reconciliation if InboundBatch lineage touched; (2) **create new inventory record** — Logilize emitted entity Module B did not anticipate; supervisor confirms creation; (3) **reject as invalid** — Logilize entity disregarded; provenance record kept; (4) **escalate** — supervisor cannot resolve in real time; queued for cross-functional review. Resolved QuarantineRecords are **immutable** post-resolution (audit-trail discipline). Single-supervisor-approval path per `feedback_prd_rr_approval` (no committee-vs-single approval policy at PRD; operator setting downstream). Resolution-driven mutations may emit `InventoryAdjusted` per DEC-190 if the resolution requires inventory state change.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B.2 QuarantineRecord entity introduction + §B.3 rule 9 quarantine-before-trust restored + §B.10 resolution workflow + immutability discipline post-resolution; cross-link to DEC-188 Logilize quarantine stream + DEC-190 adjustment event composition.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module D v0.2 (QuarantineRecord resolution may associate with existing InboundBatch — cost-basis reconciliation event downstream per v13 Stage 2.3 split-inbound-acceptance lineage); Module E v0.2 (resolution-driven adjustments emit financial events per DEC-072 + DEC-190).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational) + DEC-188 (Logilize integration QuarantineRecord stream) + DEC-190 (adjustment event composition on resolution) + `feedback_prd_rr_approval`.
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-192 — Case entity + 3-state integrity FSM; Module B as recorder, not gatekeeper (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-8) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-8 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.2 (line 3372) + §B.7 (lines 3503-3522) commit Module B to a Case entity with three integrity states: `intact` / `partially_broken` / `broken` (terminal). v17 §B.3 rule 10 (line 3402) commits Module B to "**Recorder, Not Gatekeeper**" discipline — case-breaking authorisation is resolved upstream by the layered breakability model (Module 0 BR-020): `effective_unbreakable = allocation.producer_breakability[case_config] OR offer.commercial_unbreakable`. Module S enforces at cart validation; Module A at voucher issuance; Module C at fulfillment planning. Module B records and executes the break; **does NOT re-derive or gate the effective rule**. v0.1 has no Case entity. `project_layered_breakability` memory locks the architectural pattern (v13 Stage 2.5 closure); changing it would re-open Stage 2.5.
- **Decision**: Module B v0.2 owns the **Case entity** with a 3-state integrity FSM: `intact → partially_broken → broken (terminal)`. Bottles are members of a Case; Case integrity tracks how many bottles in the Case have been removed (case-breaking event). Module B is **recorder, not gatekeeper** — it records and executes case-breaking events; it does **NOT** re-derive or gate the layered-breakability rule. The effective-unbreakable composition stays at upstream layers per `project_layered_breakability`: **Layer 1** = Module 0 BR-020 (`producer_breakability` per allocation × case_config); **Layer 2** = Module A (allocation-creation enforcement per allocation creation); **Layer 3** = Module S (offer-creation `commercial_unbreakable` per offer creation + cart-add validation) + Module A (voucher issuance) + Module C (fulfillment planning per §C.3 rule 2 — whole-case dispatch for SERIALIZED + bottles-per-case multiple for NS). Module B records the break event when fulfillment requires it (e.g., case opened to extract a single bottle for an SO line); Case transitions `intact → partially_broken`; further breaks transition to `broken`. The 3-state FSM is monotonic non-decreasing.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B.2 Case entity introduction + §B.7 3-state FSM + §B.3 rule 10 recorder-not-gatekeeper restored + cross-link to layered-breakability composition at upstream layers.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module 0 (BR-020 effective-unbreakable composition unchanged); Module A v0.2 (Layer 2 producer breakability per allocation creation unchanged); Module S v0.1 (Layer 3 commercial unbreakable per offer creation + cart-add validation unchanged); Module C v0.2 (whole-case dispatch for SERIALIZED + bottles-per-case multiple for NS per §C.3 rule 2 unchanged).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational) + `project_layered_breakability` (architectural pattern locked at v13 Stage 2.5; not re-opened by Stage 8).
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

---

## DEC-193 — ConsignmentPlacement deferred at NewCo launch (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-11) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-11 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.2 (line 3378) + §B.11 (lines 3635-3641) carry the ConsignmentPlacement entity for "CRURATED-owned stock physically placed at a consignee location (restaurant, wine bar, merchant)." Consignee = `party_type = CUSTOMER` with B2B Account per Module K §6.3. Lifecycle: created on placement (`ConsignmentPlacementRecorded`), decremented per sell-through (`ConsignmentSellThroughRecorded`), decremented per return. NewCo BMD v0.8 + DEC-068 commit to **B2C-only** at launch — every NewCo Customer is B2C; no B2B Account; no restaurant / wine bar / merchant active-consignment placements. Restoring v17 §B.11 would cascade beyond Stage 8 scope into Module C §C.12 active-consignment sell-through + Module E SELL_THROUGH_SETTLEMENT — three coordinated module restorations not justified at NewCo launch.
- **Decision**: ConsignmentPlacement entity is **deferred at NewCo launch**. NewCo v0.2 §B.11 (B2B active-consignment placement) is **OUT** at launch per DEC-068 (B2C-only). No ConsignmentPlacement entity, no `ConsignmentPlacementRecorded` event, no `ConsignmentSellThroughRecorded` event, no Module C §C.12 active-consignment sell-through workflow, no Module E SELL_THROUGH_SETTLEMENT financial event. **Stage 2+ recovery**: when NewCo BMD scope expands to admit B2B-customer relationships (post-launch), v17 §B.11 + Module C §C.12 + Module E SELL_THROUGH_SETTLEMENT compose back as a coordinated three-module restoration; this DEC is the load-bearing pointer to that future restoration. v0.2 §1.2 boundary statement explicitly disclaims the ConsignmentPlacement entity at launch (defensive lock-down so v0.2 doesn't accidentally inherit v17 §B.11 content).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §1.2 boundary statement disclaims ConsignmentPlacement at launch; cross-link to DEC-193 + DEC-068; no §B.11 prose in v0.2.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module C v0.2 (§C.12 active-consignment sell-through stays out); Module E v0.2 (SELL_THROUGH_SETTLEMENT financial event stays out); Module K v0.2 (B2B Account `party_type` stays out of v0.2 inventory side); Stage 2+ tri-module restoration trace recorded for future re-opening.
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-068 (B2C-only at NewCo launch) + DEC-001 (NewCo greenfield ERP track) + DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational); defers v17 §B.11 + Module C §C.12 + Module E SELL_THROUGH_SETTLEMENT to Stage 2+ when B2B-customer scope expands.
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-194 — Receiving discrepancy authority restored: Module D = documents, Module B = physical match (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-5) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-5 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.9 (lines 3565-3568) commits Module B to the authoritative physical-count check at receiving: "Module B compares physically counted bottles against the quantity specified in Module D's `InboundPhysicallyAccepted` event. Any variance triggers the `InboundBatchDiscrepancy` event back to Module D, which reopens the InboundEvent into DISCREPANCY (Module D §4.3) without retroactively invalidating the already-live Inbound Batch records." v17 distinction: Module D = **documents in order** (3-gate inbound QC at line 3202); Module B = **physical match**. v0.1 has no Module B receiving role; Module D PRD §7 carries Phase 1 PHYSICALLY_ACCEPTED as the only acceptance gate, leaving Logilize-side count errors undetected at the ERP layer. v17 KPI: "inbound physical-discrepancy rate <5% (baseline 15-20%)" — independent ledger detects what single-stage cannot.
- **Decision**: Receiving discrepancy authority **restored** as a two-stage check at NewCo launch. **Module D = documents in order**: 3-gate inbound QC (per Module D PRD v0.1 §7) gates Phase 1 PHYSICALLY_ACCEPTED on Vinlock acceptance (paperwork + provenance + physical-condition-on-arrival). **Module B = physical match**: a separate downstream check on each InboundBatch — Module B compares physically-counted bottles against the qty declared in Module D's `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` payload. Any variance emits `InboundBatchDiscrepancy` event back to Module D, which **reopens the InboundEvent into DISCREPANCY state** (per Module D §4.3 to be restored at Phase C cascade); already-live InboundBatch records are not retroactively invalidated. Resolution flow downstream per Module D's existing DiscrepancyResolution pattern (DEC-091). Cost-basis consequences: if discrepancy resolution adjusts qty, downstream `InboundEventCostFinalized` (Phase 2 of v13 Stage 2.3 split inbound) reflects adjusted qty.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B.9 receiving section (Module B's physical-match role) restored; `InboundBatchDiscrepancy` event emitter; cross-link to Module D `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` consumer + DiscrepancyResolution downstream per DEC-091.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module D v0.2 (InboundEvent DISCREPANCY state restoration; `InboundBatchDiscrepancy` consumer; DiscrepancyResolution flow per DEC-091); Module C v0.2 (no direct impact — fulfillment runs on accepted-and-matched stock); Module E v0.2 (cost-basis consequences if discrepancy resolution adjusts qty per v13 Stage 2.3 lineage).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-091 (Module D DiscrepancyResolution pattern) + DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational) + DEC-195 (InboundBatch entity ownership) + DEC-188 (Logilize integration receiving stream) + v13 Stage 2.3 split-inbound-acceptance lineage.
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-195 — InboundBatch entity ownership at Module B + cost-basis flow (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-3) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-3 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.2 (lines 3366-3368) commits Module B to ownership of the InboundBatch entity — "the **logical container for goods arriving from a single source** (PO or consignment receipt)." Tracks expected vs received quantities, serialization progress, ownership flag, cost basis (provisional → finalized per v13 Stage 2.3 split inbound), serialization-plan target. Module B owns; consumes Module D `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` (v17 §B.9 receiving workflow at line 3550) to create. v0.1 has no InboundBatch entity. v17's choice to land cost-basis on the batch was forced by v13 Stage 2.3 split-inbound + v13 Stage 2.4 dual-fulfillment + Stage 2.6 active-consignment dispatch payload — NewCo inherits all three; same forcing function applies.
- **Decision**: Module B v0.2 owns the **InboundBatch entity** with the v17 §B.2 attribute set: expected quantity (from PO line / consignment intake), received quantity (from Logilize physical match per DEC-194), serialization progress (`qty_planned_serialize` + `qty_actually_serialized` per DEC-186), ownership flag (per DEC-185 2-value enum at NewCo launch), **cost basis flow** (provisional at PHYSICALLY_ACCEPTED → finalized at COST_FINALIZED per v13 Stage 2.3), serialization-plan target. Module D triggers InboundBatch creation via `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` (Phase 1 of v13 Stage 2.3 two-phase event chain per Module D PRD v0.1 §7); Module D's downstream `InboundEventCostFinalized` (Phase 2) flips InboundBatch cost-basis from provisional to finalized. Cost-basis on the batch is referenced at dispatch-time per v17 §C.6 `inventory_cost_basis` payload (composes with Module C dispatch event chain per DEC-142 late-binding event flow).
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B.2 InboundBatch entity introduction with full attribute set; cost-basis flow (provisional → finalized) documented; cross-link to Module D `InboundEventPhysicallyAccepted` Phase 1 trigger + `InboundEventCostFinalized` Phase 2 trigger.
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module D v0.2 (InboundEvent two-phase preserved per v13 Stage 2.3 lineage); Module E v0.2 (cost-basis reads at dispatch); BMD v0.9 §9.8 bottle-lifecycle restatement (Phase D).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational) + DEC-186 (NS counter set on InboundBatch) + DEC-194 (receiving physical-match check) + DEC-188 (Logilize integration receiving stream) + DEC-142 (late-binding event flow consumes cost-basis at dispatch) + v13 Stage 2.3 split-inbound-acceptance lineage + v13 Stage 2.4 dual-fulfillment lineage + v13 Stage 2.6 active-consignment dispatch lineage.
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 §9.8 bottle-lifecycle restatement lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.

## DEC-196 — StockPosition aggregated view at 5-dimension intersection (Stage 8 / Module B Q-AD-9) (2026-05-09)
- **Context**: Phase A atom Q-AD-9 ([`qa.modB.s8.md`](../03-qa/qa.modB.s8.md)). v17 §B.2 (line 3374) + §B.4 (lines 3408-3424) commit Module B to a StockPosition view: "aggregated view of inventory at the **intersection of bottle reference, warehouse, case configuration, allocation lineage, and ownership**." Reports total, committed, and available quantities. Sellable quantity feeds Module A + storefront; shippable quantity feeds Module C. v0.1 has no StockPosition view. Five-dimension aggregation is the architectural surface that lets ATP land per allocation per case-config per warehouse — exactly what Module C late-binding needs for whole-case dispatch under effective-unbreakable per DEC-192 + DEC-137 + DEC-188.
- **Decision**: Module B v0.2 owns the **StockPosition aggregated view** at the canonical 5-dimension intersection: `(bottle_reference, warehouse, case_config, allocation, ownership)`. View reports: `total_quantity`, `committed_quantity` (committed to vouchers — protected per DEC-185 Q-CL-6), `available_quantity` (= `total − committed − reserved − quarantined − under_adjustment` per v17 §B.8 sub-pool ATP formula). **Sub-pool decomposition**: `available_serialized` + `available_non_serialized` per allocation (feeds DEC-187 ATP push to Module A). Sellable quantity feeds Module A + storefront ATP read path; shippable quantity feeds Module C late-binding selection (per DEC-137 + DEC-188). Five-dimension aggregation is preserved without simplification — dropping `case_config` dimension would lose case-integrity-aware ATP and break mixed-case unbreakable dispatch per DEC-192.
- **Implications**:
  - **Module B PRD v0.2 (Phase B.2/B.3)**: §B.4 StockPosition view introduction with 5-dimension aggregation + ATP formula (sub-pool decomposition); read contract documented for Module A (ATP feed) + Module S (storefront display) + Module C (late-binding selection).
  - **Cross-module cascades** (Phase C — informational only): Module A v0.2 (ATP per allocation per sub-pool reads StockPosition); Module C v0.2 (late-binding selection reads StockPosition shippable quantity per DEC-137 + DEC-188); Module S v0.1 (storefront ATP read path verification — touch-only).
- **Amends / supersedes**: composes with DEC-185 (inventory-authority foundational) + DEC-186 (NS counter set composes into StockPosition NS sub-pool) + DEC-187 (ATP push from StockPosition mutations) + DEC-192 (case-config dimension serves case-integrity-aware ATP) + DEC-137 (late-binding two-surface selection reads StockPosition).
- **BMD revision**: none for Stage 8 / Phase B; BMD v0.9 lands at Phase D.
- **Owner**: Paolo.
